# copyright_long:       Contemporary English Version (US Version)<br><br>Uncompromising simplicity marked the American Bible Society's translation of the Contemporary English Version that was first published in 1995. The text is easily read by grade schoolers, second language readers, and those who prefer the more contemporized form. The CEV is not a paraphrase; it is an accurate and faithful translation of the original manuscripts.<br>After almost 200 years of ongoing ministry, American Bible Society invites people to experience the life-changing message of the Bible. Offering an increasing range of innovative ministries to address core life questions and struggles, the Bible Society partners with Christian churches and national Bible societies to share God’s Word both in the United States and around the globe. For more information, visit www.americanbible.org. To purchase a copy of this translation, visit www.bibles.com.
40001001	Jesus Christ came from the family of King David and also from the family of Abraham . And this is a list of his ancestors .
40001017	There were 14 generations from Abraham to David . There were also 14 from David to the exile in Babylonia and 14 more to the birth of the Messiah .
40001018	This is how Jesus Christ was born . A young woman named Mary was engaged to Joseph from King David's family . But before they were married , she learned that she was going to have a baby by God's Holy Spirit .
40001019	Joseph was a good man and did not want to embarrass Mary in front of everyone . So he decided to quietly call off the wedding .
40001020	While Joseph was thinking about this , an angel from the Lord appeared to him in a dream . The angel said , “ Joseph , the baby that Mary will have is from the Holy Spirit . Go ahead and marry her .
40001021	Then after her baby is born , name him Jesus , because he will save his people from their sins . ”
40001022	So the Lord's promise came true , just as the prophet had said ,
40001023	“ A virgin will have a baby boy , and he will be called Immanuel , ” which means “ God is with us . ”
40001024	After Joseph woke up , he and Mary were soon married , just as the Lord's angel had told him to do .
40001025	But they did not sleep together before her baby was born . Then Joseph named him Jesus .
40002001	When Jesus was born in the village of Bethlehem in Judea , Herod was king . During this time some wise men from the east came to Jerusalem
40002002	and said , “ Where is the child born to be king of the Jews ? We saw his star in the east and have come to worship him . ”
40002003	When King Herod heard about this , he was worried , and so was everyone else in Jerusalem .
40002004	Herod brought together the chief priests and the teachers of the Law of Moses and asked them , “ Where will the Messiah be born ? ”
40002005	They told him , “ He will be born in Bethlehem , just as the prophet wrote ,
40002006	‘ Bethlehem in the land of Judea , you are very important among the towns of Judea . From your town will come a leader , who will be like a shepherd for my people Israel . ’ ”
40002007	Herod secretly called in the wise men and asked them when they had first seen the star .
40002008	He told them , “ Go to Bethlehem and search carefully for the child . As soon as you find him , let me know . I also want to go and worship him . ”
40002009	The wise men listened to what the king said and then left . And the star they had seen in the east went on ahead of them until it stopped over the place where the child was .
40002010	They were thrilled and excited to see the star .
40002011	When the men went into the house and saw the child with Mary , his mother , they knelt down and worshiped him . They took out their gifts of gold , frankincense , and myrrh and gave them to him .
40002012	Later they were warned in a dream not to return to Herod , and they went back home by another road .
40002013	After the wise men had gone , an angel from the Lord appeared to Joseph in a dream and said , “ Get up ! Hurry and take the child and his mother to Egypt ! Stay there until I tell you to return , because Herod is looking for the child and wants to kill him . ”
40002014	That night , Joseph got up and took his wife and the child to Egypt ,
40002015	where they stayed until Herod died . So the Lord's promise came true , just as the prophet had said , “ I called my son out of Egypt . ”
40002016	When Herod found out that the wise men from the east had tricked him , he was very angry . He gave orders for his men to kill all the boys who lived in or near Bethlehem and were two years old and younger . This was based on what he had learned from the wise men .
40002017	So the Lord's promise came true , just as the prophet Jeremiah had said ,
40002018	“ In Ramah a voice was heard crying and weeping loudly . Rachel was mourning for her children , and she refused to be comforted , because they were dead . ”
40002019	After King Herod died , an angel from the Lord appeared in a dream to Joseph while he was still in Egypt .
40002020	The angel said , “ Get up and take the child and his mother back to Israel . The people who wanted to kill him are now dead . ”
40002021	Joseph got up and left with them for Israel .
40002022	But when he heard that Herod's son Archelaus was now ruler of Judea , he was afraid to go there . Then in a dream he was told to go to Galilee ,
40002023	and they went to live there in the town of Nazareth . So the Lord's promise came true , just as the prophet had said , “ He will be called a Nazarene . ”
40003001	Years later , John the Baptist started preaching in the desert of Judea .
40003002	He said , “ Turn back to God ! The kingdom of heaven will soon be here . ”
40003003	John was the one the prophet Isaiah was talking about , when he said , “ In the desert someone is shouting , ‘ Get the road ready for the Lord ! Make a straight path for him . ’ ”
40003004	John wore clothes made of camel's hair . He had a leather strap around his waist and ate grasshoppers and wild honey .
40003005	From Jerusalem and all Judea and from the Jordan River Valley crowds of people went to John .
40003006	They told how sorry they were for their sins , and he baptized them in the river .
40003007	Many Pharisees and Sadducees also came to be baptized . But John said to them :
40003013	Jesus left Galilee and went to the Jordan River to be baptized by John .
40003014	But John kept objecting and said , “ I ought to be baptized by you . Why have you come to me ? ”
40003015	Jesus answered , “ For now this is how it should be , because we must do all God wants us to do . ” Then John agreed .
40003016	So Jesus was baptized . And as soon as he came out of the water , the sky opened , and he saw the Spirit of God coming down on him like a dove .
40003017	Then a voice from heaven said , “ This is my own dear Son , and I am pleased with him . ”
40004001	The Holy Spirit led Jesus into the desert , so that the devil could test him .
40004002	After Jesus had gone without eating for 40 days and nights , he was very hungry .
40004003	Then the devil came to him and said , “ If you are God's Son , tell these stones to turn into bread . ”
40004004	Jesus answered , “ The Scriptures say : ‘ No one can live only on food . People need every word that God has spoken . ’ ”
40004005	Next , the devil took Jesus into the holy city to the highest part of the temple .
40004006	The devil said , “ If you are God's Son , jump off . The Scriptures say : ‘ God will give his angels orders about you . They will catch you in their arms , and you won't hurt your feet on the stones . ’ ”
40004007	Jesus answered , “ The Scriptures also say , ‘ Don't try to test the Lord your God ! ’ ”
40004008	Finally , the devil took Jesus up on a very high mountain and showed him all the kingdoms on earth and their power .
40004009	The devil said to him , “ I will give all this to you , if you will bow down and worship me . ”
40004010	Jesus answered , “ Go away Satan ! The Scriptures say : ‘ Worship the Lord your God and serve only him . ’ ”
40004011	Then the devil left Jesus , and angels came to help him .
40004012	When Jesus heard that John had been put in prison , he went to Galilee .
40004013	But instead of staying in Nazareth , Jesus moved to Capernaum . This town was beside Lake Galilee in the territory of Zebulun and Naphtali .
40004014	So God's promise came true , just as the prophet Isaiah had said ,
40004015	“ Listen , lands of Zebulun and Naphtali , lands along the road to the sea and across the Jordan . Listen Galilee , land of the Gentiles !
40004016	Although your people live in darkness , they will see a bright light . Although they live in the shadow of death , a light will shine on them . ”
40004017	Then Jesus started preaching , “ Turn back to God ! The kingdom of heaven will soon be here . ”
40004018	While Jesus was walking along the shore of Lake Galilee , he saw two brothers . One was Simon , also known as Peter , and the other was Andrew . They were fishermen , and they were casting their net into the lake .
40004019	Jesus said to them , “ Follow me ! I will teach you how to bring in people instead of fish . ”
40004020	Right then the two brothers dropped their nets and went with him .
40004021	Jesus walked on until he saw James and John , the sons of Zebedee . They were in a boat with their father , mending their nets . Jesus asked them to come with him .
40004022	At once they left the boat and their father and went with Jesus .
40004023	Jesus went all over Galilee , teaching in their synagogues and preaching the good news about God's kingdom . He also healed every kind of disease and sickness .
40004024	News about him spread all over Syria , and people with every kind of sickness or disease were brought to him . Some of them had a lot of demons in them , others were thought to be crazy , and still others could not walk . But Jesus healed them all .
40004025	Large crowds followed Jesus from Galilee and the region around the ten cities known as Decapolis . They also came from Jerusalem , Judea , and from across the Jordan River .
40005001	When Jesus saw the crowds , he went up on the side of a mountain and sat down . Jesus' disciples gathered around him ,
40005002	and he taught them :
40005003	God blesses those people who depend only on him . They belong to the kingdom of heaven !
40005004	God blesses those people who grieve . They will find comfort !
40005005	God blesses those people who are humble . The earth will belong to them !
40005006	God blesses those people who want to obey him more than to eat or drink . They will be given what they want !
40005007	God blesses those people who are merciful . They will be treated with mercy !
40005008	God blesses those people whose hearts are pure . They will see him !
40005009	God blesses those people who make peace . They will be called his children !
40005010	God blesses those people who are treated badly for doing right . They belong to the kingdom of heaven .
40006010	Come and set up your kingdom , so that everyone on earth will obey you , as you are obeyed in heaven .
40006011	Give us our food for today .
40006012	Forgive us for doing wrong , as we forgive others .
40006013	Keep us from being tempted and protect us from evil .
40007028	When Jesus finished speaking , the crowds were surprised at his teaching .
40007029	He taught them like someone with authority , and not like their teachers of the Law of Moses .
40008001	As Jesus came down the mountain , he was followed by large crowds .
40008002	Suddenly a man with leprosy came and knelt in front of Jesus . He said , “ Lord , you have the power to make me well , if only you wanted to . ”
40008003	Jesus put his hand on the man and said , “ I want to ! Now you are well . ” At once the man's leprosy disappeared .
40008004	Jesus told him , “ Don't tell anyone about this , but go and show the priest that you are well . Then take a gift to the temple just as Moses commanded , and everyone will know that you have been healed . ”
40008005	When Jesus was going into the town of Capernaum , an army officer came up to him and said ,
40008006	“ Lord , my servant is at home in such terrible pain that he can't even move . ”
40008007	“ I will go and heal him , ” Jesus replied .
40008008	But the officer said , “ Lord , I'm not good enough for you to come into my house . Just give the order , and my servant will get well .
40008009	I have officers who give orders to me , and I have soldiers who take orders from me . I can say to one of them , ‘ Go ! ’ and he goes . I can say to another , ‘ Come ! ’ and he comes . I can say to my servant , ‘ Do this ! ’ and he will do it . ”
40008010	When Jesus heard this , he was so surprised that he turned and said to the crowd following him , “ I tell you in all of Israel I've never found anyone with this much faith !
40008011	Many people will come from everywhere to enjoy the feast in the kingdom of heaven with Abraham , Isaac , and Jacob .
40008012	But the ones who should have been in the kingdom will be thrown out into the dark . They will cry and grit their teeth in pain . ”
40008013	Then Jesus said to the officer , “ You may go home now . Your faith has made it happen . ” Right then his servant was healed .
40008014	Jesus went to the home of Peter , where he found that Peter's mother-in-law was sick in bed with fever .
40008015	He took her by the hand , and the fever left her . Then she got up and served Jesus a meal .
40008016	That evening many people with demons in them were brought to Jesus . And with only a word he forced out the evil spirits and healed everyone who was sick .
40008017	So God's promise came true , just as the prophet Isaiah had said , “ He healed our diseases and made us well . ”
40008018	When Jesus saw the crowd , he went across Lake Galilee .
40008019	A teacher of the Law of Moses came up to him and said , “ Teacher , I'll go anywhere with you ! ”
40008020	Jesus replied , “ Foxes have dens , and birds have nests . But the Son of Man doesn't have a place to call his own . ”
40008021	Another disciple said to Jesus , “ Lord , let me wait till I bury my father . ”
40008022	Jesus answered , “ Follow me , and let the dead bury their dead . ”
40008023	After Jesus left in a boat with his disciples ,
40008024	a terrible storm suddenly struck the lake , and waves started splashing into their boat . Jesus was sound asleep ,
40008025	so the disciples went over to him and woke him up . They said , “ Lord , wake up ! Save us before we drown ! ”
40008026	But Jesus replied , “ Why are you so afraid ? You surely don't have much faith . ” Then he got up and ordered the wind and the waves to calm down . And everything was calm .
40008027	The men in the boat were amazed and said , “ Who is this ? Even the wind and the waves obey him . ”
40008028	After Jesus had crossed the lake , he came to shore near the town of Gadara and started down the road . Two men with demons in them came to him from the tombs . They were so fierce that no one could travel that way .
40008029	Suddenly they shouted , “ Jesus , Son of God , what do you want with us ? Have you come to punish us before our time ? ”
40008030	Not far from there a large herd of pigs was feeding .
40008031	So the demons begged Jesus , “ If you force us out , please send us into those pigs ! ”
40008032	Jesus told them to go , and they went out of the men and into the pigs . All at once the pigs rushed down the steep bank into the lake and drowned .
40008033	The people taking care of the pigs ran to the town and told everything , especially what had happened to the two men .
40008034	Everyone in town came out to meet Jesus . When they saw him , they begged him to leave their part of the country .
40009001	Jesus got into a boat and crossed back over to the town where he lived .
40009002	Some people soon brought to him a man lying on a mat because he could not walk . When Jesus saw how much faith they had , he said to the man , “ My friend , don't worry ! Your sins are forgiven . ”
40009003	Some teachers of the Law of Moses said to themselves , “ Jesus must think he is God ! ”
40009004	But Jesus knew what was in their minds , and he said , “ Why are you thinking such evil things ?
40009005	Is it easier for me to tell this man his sins are forgiven or to tell him to get up and walk ?
40009006	But I will show you that the Son of Man has the right to forgive sins here on earth . ” So Jesus said to the man , “ Get up ! Pick up your mat and go on home . ”
40009007	The man got up and went home .
40009008	When the crowds saw this , they were afraid and praised God for giving such authority to people .
40009009	As Jesus was leaving , he saw a tax collector named Matthew sitting at the place for paying taxes . Jesus said to him , “ Follow me . ” Matthew got up and went with him .
40009010	Later , Jesus and his disciples were having dinner at Matthew's house . Many tax collectors and other sinners were also there .
40009011	Some Pharisees asked Jesus' disciples , “ Why does your teacher eat with tax collectors and other sinners ? ”
40009012	Jesus heard them and answered , “ Healthy people don't need a doctor , but sick people do .
40009013	Go and learn what the Scriptures mean when they say , ‘ Instead of offering sacrifices to me , I want you to be merciful to others . ’ I didn't come to invite good people to be my followers . I came to invite sinners . ”
40009014	Some followers of John the Baptist came and asked Jesus , “ Why do we and the Pharisees often go without eating , while your disciples never do ? ”
40009015	Jesus answered :
40009018	While Jesus was still speaking , an official came and knelt in front of him . The man said , “ My daughter has just now died ! Please come and place your hand on her . Then she will live again . ”
40009019	Jesus and his disciples got up and went with the man .
40009020	A woman who had been bleeding for twelve years came up behind Jesus and barely touched his clothes .
40009021	She had said to herself , “ If I can just touch his clothes , I will be healed . ”
40009022	Jesus turned . He saw the woman and said , “ Don't worry ! You are now healed because of your faith . ” At that moment she was healed .
40009023	When Jesus went into the home of the official and saw the musicians and the crowd of mourners ,
40009024	he said , “ Get out of here ! The little girl isn't dead . She is just asleep . ” Everyone started laughing at Jesus .
40009025	But after the crowd had been sent out of the house , Jesus went to the girl's bedside . He took her by the hand and helped her up .
40009026	News about this spread all over that part of the country .
40009027	As Jesus was leaving that place , two blind men began following him and shouting , “ Son of David , have pity on us ! ”
40009028	After Jesus had gone indoors , the two blind men came up to him . He asked them , “ Do you believe I can make you well ? ” “ Yes , Lord , ” they answered .
40009029	Jesus touched their eyes and said , “ Because of your faith , you will be healed . ”
40009030	They were able to see , and Jesus strictly warned them not to tell anyone about him .
40009031	But they left and talked about him to everyone in that part of the country .
40009032	As Jesus and his disciples were on their way , some people brought to him a man who could not talk because a demon was in him .
40009033	After Jesus had forced the demon out , the man started talking . The crowds were so amazed they began saying , “ Nothing like this has ever happened in Israel ! ”
40009034	But the Pharisees said , “ The leader of the demons gives him the power to force out demons . ”
40009035	Jesus went to every town and village . He taught in their synagogues and preached the good news about God's kingdom . Jesus also healed every kind of disease and sickness .
40009036	When he saw the crowds , he felt sorry for them . They were confused and helpless , like sheep without a shepherd .
40009037	He said to his disciples , “ A large crop is in the fields , but there are only a few workers .
40009038	Ask the Lord in charge of the harvest to send out workers to bring it in . ”
40010001	Jesus called together his twelve disciples . He gave them the power to force out evil spirits and to heal every kind of disease and sickness .

40012010	where there was a man whose hand was paralyzed . Some Pharisees wanted to accuse Jesus of doing something wrong , so they asked him , “ Is it right to heal someone on the Sabbath ? ”
40012011	Jesus answered , “ If one of your sheep fell into a ditch on the Sabbath , wouldn't you lift it out ?
40012012	People are worth much more than sheep , and so it is right to do good on the Sabbath . ”

40014001	About this time Herod the ruler heard the news about Jesus
40014002	and told his officials , “ This is John the Baptist ! He has come back from death , and that's why he has the power to work these miracles . ”
40014005	Herod wanted to kill John . But the people thought John was a prophet , and Herod was afraid of what they might do .
40014006	When Herod's birthday came , the daughter of Herodias danced for the guests . She pleased Herod
40014007	so much he swore to give her whatever she wanted .
40014008	But the girl's mother told her to say , “ Here on a serving plate I want the head of John the Baptist ! ”
40014009	Herod was sorry for what he had said . But he did not want to break the promise he had made in front of his guests . So he ordered a guard
40014010	to go to the prison and cut off John's head .

40014012	John's followers took his body and buried it . Then they told Jesus what had happened .
40014013	After Jesus heard about John , he crossed Lake Galilee to go to some place where he could be alone . But the crowds found out and followed him on foot from the towns .
40014014	When Jesus got out of the boat , he saw the large crowd . He felt sorry for them and healed everyone who was sick .
40014015	That evening the disciples came to Jesus and said , “ This place is like a desert , and it's already late . Let the crowds leave , so they can go to the villages and buy some food . ”
40014016	Jesus replied , “ They don't have to leave . Why don't you give them something to eat ? ”
40014017	But they said , “ We have only five small loaves of bread and two fish . ”
40014018	Jesus asked his disciples to bring the food to him ,
40014019	and he told the crowd to sit down on the grass . Jesus took the five loaves and the two fish . He looked up toward heaven and blessed the food . Then he broke the bread and handed it to his disciples , and they gave it to the people .
40014020	After everyone had eaten all they wanted , Jesus' disciples picked up twelve large baskets of leftovers .
40014021	There were about 5,000 men who ate , not counting the women and children .
40014022	At once , Jesus made his disciples get into a boat and start back across the lake . But he stayed until he had sent the crowds away .
40014023	Then he went up on a mountain where he could be alone and pray . Later in the evening , he was still there .
40014024	By this time the boat was a long way from the shore . It was going against the wind and was being tossed around by the waves .
40014025	A little while before morning , Jesus came walking on the water toward his disciples .
40014026	When they saw him , they thought he was a ghost . They were terrified and started screaming .
40014027	At once , Jesus said to them , “ Don't worry ! I am Jesus . Don't be afraid . ”
40014028	Peter replied , “ Lord , if it really is you , tell me to come to you on the water . ”
40014029	“ Come on ! ” Jesus said . Peter then got out of the boat and started walking on the water toward him .
40014030	But when Peter saw how strong the wind was , he was afraid and started sinking . “ Save me , Lord ! ” he shouted .
40014031	At once , Jesus reached out his hand . He helped Peter up and said , “ You surely don't have much faith . Why do you doubt ? ”
40014032	When Jesus and Peter got into the boat , the wind died down .
40014033	The men in the boat worshiped Jesus and said , “ You really are the Son of God ! ”
40014034	Jesus and his disciples crossed the lake and came to shore near the town of Gennesaret .
40014035	The people found out he was there , and they sent word to everyone who lived in this part of the country . So they brought all the sick people to Jesus .
40014036	They begged him just to let them touch his clothes , and everyone who did was healed .
40015001	About this time some Pharisees and teachers of the Law of Moses came from Jerusalem . They asked Jesus ,

41014014	and when he goes into a house , say to the owner , ‘ Our teacher wants to know if you have a room where he can eat the Passover meal with his disciples . ’
41014015	The owner will take you upstairs and show you a large room furnished and ready for you to use . Prepare the meal there . ”
41014016	The two disciples went into the city and found everything just as Jesus had told them . So they prepared the Passover meal .
41014019	This made the disciples sad , and one after another they said to Jesus , “ You surely don't mean me ! ”
41014020	He answered , “ It is one of you twelve men who is eating from this dish with me .
41014021	The Son of Man will die , just as the Scriptures say . But it is going to be terrible for the one who betrays me . That man would be better off if he had never been born . ”
41014022	During the meal Jesus took some bread in his hands . He blessed the bread and broke it . Then he gave it to his disciples and said , “ Take this . It is my body . ”
41014023	Jesus picked up a cup of wine and gave thanks to God . He gave it to his disciples , and they all drank some .
41014024	Then he said , “ This is my blood , which is poured out for many people , and with it God makes his agreement .
41014025	From now on I will not drink any wine , until I drink new wine in God's kingdom . ”
41014026	Then they sang a hymn and went out to the Mount of Olives .
41014027	Jesus said to his disciples , “ All of you will reject me , as the Scriptures say , ‘ I will strike down the shepherd , and the sheep will be scattered . ’
41014029	Peter spoke up , “ Even if all the others reject you , I never will ! ”
41014030	Jesus replied , “ This very night before a rooster crows twice , you will say three times that you don't know me . ”
41014031	But Peter was so sure of himself that he said , “ Even if I have to die with you , I will never say I don't know you ! ” All the others said the same thing .
41014032	Jesus went with his disciples to a place called Gethsemane , and he told them , “ Sit here while I pray . ”
41014033	Jesus took along Peter , James , and John . He was sad and troubled and
41014034	told them , “ I am so sad that I feel as if I am dying . Stay here and keep awake with me . ”
41014037	When Jesus came back and found the disciples sleeping , he said to Simon Peter , “ Are you asleep ? Can't you stay awake for just one hour ?
41014038	Stay awake and pray that you won't be tested . You want to do what is right , but you are weak . ”
41014039	Jesus went back and prayed the same prayer .
41014040	But when he returned to the disciples , he found them sleeping again . They simply could not keep their eyes open , and they did not know what to say .
41014041	When Jesus returned to the disciples the third time , he said , “ Are you still sleeping and resting ? Enough of this ! The time has come for the Son of Man to be handed over to sinners .
41014042	Get up ! Let's go . The one who will betray me is already here . ”
41014043	Jesus was still speaking , when Judas the betrayer came up . He was one of the twelve disciples , and a mob of men armed with swords and clubs were with him . They had been sent by the chief priests , the nation's leaders , and the teachers of the Law of Moses .
41014044	Judas had told them ahead of time , “ Arrest the man I greet with a kiss . Tie him up tight and lead him away . ”
41014045	Judas walked right up to Jesus and said , “ Teacher ! ” Then Judas kissed him ,
41014046	and the men grabbed Jesus and arrested him .
41014047	Someone standing there pulled out a sword . He struck the servant of the high priest and cut off his ear .
41014048	Jesus said to the mob , “ Why do you come with swords and clubs to arrest me like a criminal ?
41014049	Day after day I was with you and taught in the temple , and you didn't arrest me . But what the Scriptures say must come true . ”
41014050	All of Jesus' disciples ran off and left him .
41014051	One of them was a young man who was wearing only a linen cloth . And when the men grabbed him ,
41014052	he left the cloth behind and ran away naked .
41014053	Jesus was led off to the high priest . Then the chief priests , the nation's leaders , and the teachers of the Law of Moses all met together .
41014054	Peter had followed at a distance , and when he reached the courtyard of the high priest's house , he sat down with the guards to warm himself beside a fire .
41014055	The chief priests and the whole council tried to find someone to accuse Jesus of a crime , so they could put him to death . But they could not find anyone to accuse him .
41014056	Many people did tell lies against Jesus , but they did not agree on what they said .
41014057	Finally , some men stood up and lied about him . They said ,
41014058	“ We heard him say he would tear down this temple that we built . He also claimed that in three days he would build another one without any help . ”
41014059	But even then they did not agree on what they said .
41014060	The high priest stood up in the council and asked Jesus , “ Why don't you say something in your own defense ? Don't you hear the charges they are making against you ? ”
41014061	But Jesus kept quiet and did not say a word . The high priest asked him another question , “ Are you the Messiah , the Son of the glorious God ? ”
41014062	“ Yes , I am ! ” Jesus answered . “ Soon you will see the Son of Man sitting at the right side of God All-Powerful , and coming with the clouds of heaven . ”
41014063	At once the high priest ripped his robe apart and shouted , “ Why do we need more witnesses ?
41014064	You heard him claim to be God ! What is your decision ? ” They all agreed he should be put to death .
41014065	Some of the people started spitting on Jesus . They blindfolded him , hit him with their fists , and said , “ Tell us who hit you ! ” Then the guards took charge of Jesus and beat him .
41014066	While Peter was still in the courtyard , a servant girl of the high priest came up
41014067	and saw Peter warming himself by the fire . She stared at him and said , “ You were with Jesus from Nazareth ! ”
41014068	Peter replied , “ That isn't true ! I don't know what you're talking about . I don't have any idea what you mean . ” He went out to the gate , and a rooster crowed .
41014069	The servant girl saw Peter again and said to the people standing there , “ This man is one of them ! ”
41014070	“ No , I'm not ! ” Peter replied . A little while later some of the people said to Peter , “ You certainly are one of them . You're a Galilean ! ”
41014071	This time Peter began to curse and swear , “ I don't even know the man you're talking about ! ”
41014072	At once the rooster crowed a second time . Then Peter remembered that Jesus had told him , “ Before a rooster crows twice , you will say three times that you don't know me . ” So Peter started crying .
41015001	Early the next morning the chief priests , the nation's leaders , and the teachers of the Law of Moses met together with the whole Jewish council . They tied up Jesus and led him off to Pilate .
41015002	He asked Jesus , “ Are you the king of the Jews ? ” “ Those are your words , ” Jesus answered .
41015003	The chief priests brought many charges against Jesus .
41015004	Then Pilate questioned him again , “ Don't you have anything to say ? Don't you hear what crimes they say you have done ? ”
41015005	But Jesus did not answer , and Pilate was amazed .
41015006	During Passover , Pilate always freed one prisoner chosen by the people .
41015007	And at that time there was a prisoner named Barabbas . He and some others had been arrested for murder during a riot .
41015008	The crowd now came and asked Pilate to set a prisoner free , just as he usually did .
41015009	Pilate asked them , “ Do you want me to free the king of the Jews ? ”
41015010	Pilate knew that the chief priests had brought Jesus to him because they were jealous .
41015011	But the chief priests told the crowd to ask Pilate to free Barabbas .
41015012	Then Pilate asked the crowd , “ What do you want me to do with this man you say is the king of the Jews ? ”
41015013	They yelled , “ Nail him to a cross ! ”
41015014	Pilate asked , “ But what crime has he done ? ” “ Nail him to a cross ! ” they yelled even louder .
41015015	Pilate wanted to please the crowd , so he set Barabbas free . Then he ordered his soldiers to beat Jesus with a whip and nail him to a cross .
41015016	The soldiers led Jesus inside the courtyard of the fortress and called together the rest of the troops .
41015017	They put a purple robe on him , and on his head they placed a crown they had made out of thorn branches .
41015018	They made fun of Jesus and shouted , “ Hey , you king of the Jews ! ”
41015019	Then they beat him on the head with a stick . They spit on him and knelt down and pretended to worship him .
41015020	When the soldiers had finished making fun of Jesus , they took off the purple robe . They put his own clothes back on him and led him off to be nailed to a cross .
41015021	Simon from Cyrene happened to be coming in from a farm , and they forced him to carry Jesus' cross . Simon was the father of Alexander and Rufus .
41015022	The soldiers took Jesus to Golgotha , which means “ Place of a Skull . ”
41015023	There they gave him some wine mixed with a drug to ease the pain , but he refused to drink it .
41015024	They nailed Jesus to a cross and gambled to see who would get his clothes .
41015025	It was about nine o'clock in the morning when they nailed him to the cross .
41015026	On it was a sign that told why he was nailed there . It read , “ This is the King of the Jews . ”
41015029	People who passed by said terrible things about Jesus . They shook their heads and shouted , “ Ha ! So you're the one who claimed you could tear down the temple and build it again in three days .
41015030	Save yourself and come down from the cross ! ”
41015031	The chief priests and the teachers of the Law of Moses also made fun of Jesus . They said to each other , “ He saved others , but he can't save himself .
41015032	If he is the Messiah , the king of Israel , let him come down from the cross ! Then we will see and believe . ” The two criminals also said cruel things to Jesus .
41015033	About noon the sky turned dark and stayed that way until around three o'clock .
41015034	Then about that time Jesus shouted , “ Eloi , Eloi , lema sabachthani ? ” which means , “ My God , my God , why have you deserted me ? ”
41015035	Some of the people standing there heard Jesus and said , “ He is calling for Elijah . ”
41015036	One of them ran and grabbed a sponge . After he had soaked it in wine , he put it on a stick and held it up to Jesus . He said , “ Let's wait and see if Elijah will come and take him down ! ”
41015037	Jesus shouted and then died .
41015038	At once the curtain in the temple tore in two from top to bottom .
41015039	A Roman army officer was standing in front of Jesus . When the officer saw how Jesus died , he said , “ This man really was the Son of God ! ”
41015042	It was now the evening before the Sabbath , and the Jewish people were getting ready for that sacred day .
41015043	A man named Joseph from Arimathea was brave enough to ask Pilate for the body of Jesus . Joseph was a highly respected member of the Jewish council , and he was also waiting for God's kingdom to come .
41015044	Pilate was surprised to hear that Jesus was already dead , and he called in the army officer to find out if Jesus had been dead very long .
41015045	After the officer told him , Pilate let Joseph have Jesus' body .
41015046	Joseph bought a linen cloth and took the body down from the cross . He had it wrapped in the cloth , and he put it in a tomb that had been cut into solid rock . Then he rolled a big stone against the entrance to the tomb .
41015047	Mary Magdalene and Mary the mother of Joseph were watching and saw where the body was placed .
41016001	After the Sabbath , Mary Magdalene , Salome , and Mary the mother of James bought some spices to put on Jesus' body .
41016002	Very early on Sunday morning , just as the sun was coming up , they went to the tomb .
41016003	On their way , they were asking one another , “ Who will roll the stone away from the entrance for us ? ”
41016004	But when they looked , they saw that the stone had already been rolled away . And it was a huge stone !
41016005	The women went into the tomb , and on the right side they saw a young man in a white robe sitting there . They were alarmed .
41016006	The man said , “ Don't be alarmed ! You are looking for Jesus from Nazareth , who was nailed to a cross . God has raised him to life , and he isn't here . You can see the place where they put his body .
41016007	Now go and tell his disciples , and especially Peter , that he will go ahead of you to Galilee . You will see him there , just as he told you . ”
41016008	When the women ran from the tomb , they were confused and shaking all over . They were too afraid to tell anyone what had happened .
41016009	Very early on the first day of the week , after Jesus had risen to life , he appeared to Mary Magdalene . Earlier he had forced seven demons out of her .
41016010	She left and told his friends , who were crying and mourning .
41016011	Even though they heard that Jesus was alive and that Mary had seen him , they still would not believe it .
41016012	Later , Jesus appeared in another form to two disciples , as they were on their way out of the city .
41016013	But when these disciples told what had happened , the others would not believe either .
41016014	Afterwards , Jesus appeared to his eleven disciples as they were eating . He scolded them because they were too stubborn to believe the ones who had seen him after he had been raised to life .
41016015	Then he told them :
41016019	After the Lord Jesus had said these things to the disciples , he was taken back up to heaven where he sat down at the right side of God .
41016020	Then the disciples left and preached everywhere . The Lord was with them , and the miracles they worked proved that their message was true .
42001001	Many people have tried to tell the story of what God has done among us .
42001002	They wrote what we had been told by the ones who were there in the beginning and saw what happened .
42001003	So I made a careful study of everything and then decided to write and tell you exactly what took place . Honorable Theophilus ,
42001004	I have done this to let you know the truth about what you have heard .
42001005	When Herod was king of Judea , there was a priest by the name of Zechariah from the priestly group of Abijah . His wife Elizabeth was from the family of Aaron .
42001006	Both of them were good people and pleased the Lord God by obeying all that he had commanded .
42001007	But they did not have children . Elizabeth could not have any , and both Zechariah and Elizabeth were already old .
42001008	One day Zechariah's group of priests were on duty , and he was serving God as a priest .
42001009	According to the custom of the priests , he had been chosen to go into the Lord's temple that day and to burn incense ,
42001010	while the people stood outside praying .
42001011	All at once an angel from the Lord appeared to Zechariah at the right side of the altar .
42001012	Zechariah was confused and afraid when he saw the angel .
42001013	But the angel told him :
42001018	Zechariah said to the angel , “ How will I know this is going to happen ? My wife and I are both very old . ”
42001019	The angel answered , “ I am Gabriel , God's servant , and I was sent to tell you this good news .
42001020	You have not believed what I have said . So you will not be able to say a thing until all this happens . But everything will take place when it is supposed to . ”
42001021	The crowd was waiting for Zechariah and kept wondering why he was staying in the temple so long .
42001022	When he did come out , he could not speak , and they knew he had seen a vision . He motioned to them with his hands , but did not say a thing .
42001023	When Zechariah's time of service in the temple was over , he went home .
42001024	Soon after this , his wife was expecting a baby , and for five months she did not leave the house . She said to herself ,
42001025	“ What the Lord has done for me will keep people from looking down on me . ”
42001026	One month later God sent the angel Gabriel to the town of Nazareth in Galilee
42001027	with a message for a virgin named Mary . She was engaged to Joseph from the family of King David .
42001028	The angel greeted Mary and said , “ You are truly blessed ! The Lord is with you . ”
42001029	Mary was confused by the angel's words and wondered what they meant .
42001030	Then the angel told Mary , “ Don't be afraid ! God is pleased with you ,
42001031	and you will have a son . His name will be Jesus .
42001032	He will be great and will be called the Son of God Most High . The Lord God will make him king , as his ancestor David was .
42001033	He will rule the people of Israel forever , and his kingdom will never end . ”
42001034	Mary asked the angel , “ How can this happen ? I am not even married ! ”
42001035	The angel answered , “ The Holy Spirit will come down to you , and God's power will come over you . So your child will be called the holy Son of God .
42001036	Your relative Elizabeth is also going to have a son , even though she is old . No one thought she could ever have a baby , but in three months she will have a son .
42001037	Nothing is impossible for God ! ”
42001038	Mary said , “ I am the Lord's servant ! Let it happen as you have said . ” And the angel left her .
42001039	A short time later Mary hurried to a town in the hill country of Judea .
42001040	She went into Zechariah's home , where she greeted Elizabeth .
42001041	When Elizabeth heard Mary's greeting , her baby moved within her . The Holy Spirit came upon Elizabeth .
42001042	Then in a loud voice she said to Mary :
42001046	Mary said : With all my heart I praise the Lord ,
42001047	and I am glad because of God my Savior .
42001048	God cares for me , his humble servant . From now on , all people will say God has blessed me .
42001049	God All-Powerful has done great things for me , and his name is holy .
42001050	He always shows mercy to everyone who worships him .
42001051	The Lord has used his powerful arm to scatter those who are proud .
42001052	God drags strong rulers from their thrones and puts humble people in places of power .
42001053	God gives the hungry good things to eat , and sends the rich away with nothing .
42001054	God helps his servant Israel and is always merciful to his people .
42001055	The Lord made this promise to our ancestors , to Abraham and his family forever !
42001056	Mary stayed with Elizabeth about three months . Then she went back home .
42001057	When Elizabeth's son was born ,
42001058	her neighbors and relatives heard how kind the Lord had been to her , and they too were glad .
42001059	Eight days later they did for the child what the Law of Moses commands . They were going to name him Zechariah , after his father .
42001060	But Elizabeth said , “ No ! His name is John . ”
42001061	The people argued , “ No one in your family has ever been named John . ”
42001062	So they motioned to Zechariah to find out what he wanted to name his son .
42001063	Zechariah asked for a writing tablet . Then he wrote , “ His name is John . ” Everyone was amazed .
42001064	At once , Zechariah started speaking and praising God .
42001065	All the neighbors were frightened because of what had happened , and everywhere in the hill country people kept talking about these things .
42001066	Everyone who heard about this wondered what this child would grow up to be . They knew the Lord was with him .
42001067	The Holy Spirit came upon Zechariah , and he began to speak :
42001068	Praise the Lord , the God of Israel ! He has come to save his people .
42001069	Our God has given us a mighty Savior from the family of David his servant .
42001070	Long ago the Lord promised by the words of his holy prophets
42001071	to save us from our enemies and from everyone who hates us .
42001072	God said he would be kind to our people and keep his sacred promise .
42001073	He told our ancestor Abraham
42001074	that he would rescue us from our enemies . Then we could serve him without fear ,
42001075	by being holy and good as long as we live .
42001076	You , my son , will be called the prophet of God Most High . You will go ahead of the Lord to get everything ready for him .
42001077	You will tell his people that they can be saved when their sins are forgiven .
42001078	God's love and kindness will shine upon us like the sun that rises in the sky .
42001079	On us who live in the dark shadow of death this light will shine to guide us into a life of peace .
42001080	As John grew up , God's Spirit gave him great power . John lived in the desert until the time he was sent to the people of Israel .
42002001	About that time Emperor Augustus gave orders for the names of all the people to be listed in record books .
42002002	These first records were made when Quirinius was governor of Syria .
42002003	Everyone had to go to their own hometown to be listed .
42002004	So Joseph had to leave Nazareth in Galilee and go to Bethlehem in Judea . Long ago Bethlehem had been King David's hometown , and Joseph went there because he was from David's family .
42002005	Mary was engaged to Joseph and traveled with him to Bethlehem . She was soon going to have a baby ,
42002006	and while they were there ,
42002007	she gave birth to her first-born son . She dressed him in baby clothes and laid him on a bed of hay , because there was no room for them in the inn .
42002008	That night in the fields near Bethlehem some shepherds were guarding their sheep .
42002009	All at once an angel came down to them from the Lord , and the brightness of the Lord's glory flashed around them . The shepherds were frightened .
42002010	But the angel said , “ Don't be afraid ! I have good news for you , which will make everyone happy .
42002011	This very day in King David's hometown a Savior was born for you . He is Christ the Lord .
42002012	You will know who he is , because you will find him dressed in baby clothes and lying on a bed of hay . ”
42002013	Suddenly many other angels came down from heaven and joined in praising God . They said :
42002014	“ Praise God in heaven ! Peace on earth to everyone who pleases God . ”
42002015	After the angels had left and gone back to heaven , the shepherds said to each other , “ Let's go to Bethlehem and see what the Lord has told us about . ”
42002016	They hurried off and found Mary and Joseph , and they saw the baby lying on a bed of hay .
42002017	When the shepherds saw Jesus , they told his parents what the angel had said about him .
42002018	Everyone listened and was surprised .
42002019	But Mary kept thinking about all this and wondering what it meant .
42002020	As the shepherds returned to their sheep , they were praising God and saying wonderful things about him . Everything they had seen and heard was just as the angel had said .
42002021	Eight days later Jesus' parents did for him what the Law of Moses commands . And they named him Jesus , just as the angel had told Mary when he promised she would have a baby .
42002022	The time came for Mary and Joseph to do what the Law of Moses says a mother is supposed to do after her baby is born . They took Jesus to the temple in Jerusalem and presented him to the Lord ,
42002023	just as the Law of the Lord says , “ Each first-born baby boy belongs to the Lord . ”
42002024	The Law of the Lord also says parents have to offer a sacrifice , giving at least a pair of doves or two young pigeons . So that is what Mary and Joseph did .
42002025	At this time a man named Simeon was living in Jerusalem . Simeon was a good man . He loved God and was waiting for him to save the people of Israel . God's Spirit came to him
42002026	and told him that he would not die until he had seen Christ the Lord .
42002027	When Mary and Joseph brought Jesus to the temple to do what the Law of Moses says should be done for a new baby , the Spirit told Simeon to go into the temple .
42002028	Simeon took the baby Jesus in his arms and praised God ,
42002029	“ Lord , I am your servant , and now I can die in peace , because you have kept your promise to me .
42002030	With my own eyes I have seen what you have done to save your people ,
42002031	and foreign nations will also see this .
42002032	Your mighty power is a light for all nations , and it will bring honor to your people Israel . ”
42002033	Jesus' parents were surprised at what Simeon had said .
42002034	Then he blessed them and told Mary , “ This child of yours will cause many people in Israel to fall and others to stand . The child will be like a warning sign . Many people will reject him ,
42002035	and you , Mary , will suffer as though you had been stabbed by a dagger . But all this will show what people are really thinking . ”
42002036	The prophet Anna was also there in the temple . She was the daughter of Phanuel from the tribe of Asher , and she was very old . In her youth she had been married for seven years , but her husband died .
42002037	And now she was 84 years old . Night and day she served God in the temple by praying and often going without eating .
42002038	At this time Anna came in and praised God . She spoke about the child Jesus to everyone who hoped for Jerusalem to be set free .
42002039	After Joseph and Mary had done everything that the Law of the Lord commands , they returned home to Nazareth in Galilee .
42002040	The child Jesus grew . He became strong and wise , and God blessed him .
42002041	Every year Jesus' parents went to Jerusalem for Passover .
42002042	And when Jesus was twelve years old , they all went there as usual for the celebration .
42002043	After Passover his parents left , but they did not know that Jesus had stayed on in the city .
42002044	They thought he was traveling with some other people , and they went a whole day before they started looking for him .
42002045	When they could not find him with their relatives and friends , they went back to Jerusalem and started looking for him there .
42002046	Three days later they found Jesus sitting in the temple , listening to the teachers and asking them questions .
42002047	Everyone who heard him was surprised at how much he knew and at the answers he gave .
42002048	When his parents found him , they were amazed . His mother said , “ Son , why have you done this to us ? Your father and I have been very worried , and we have been searching for you ! ”
42002049	Jesus answered , “ Why did you have to look for me ? Didn't you know that I would be in my Father's house ? ”
42002050	But they did not understand what he meant .
42002051	Jesus went back to Nazareth with his parents and obeyed them . His mother kept on thinking about all that had happened .
42002052	Jesus became wise , and he grew strong . God was pleased with him and so were the people .
42003001	For 15 years Emperor Tiberius had ruled that part of the world . Pontius Pilate was governor of Judea , and Herod was the ruler of Galilee . Herod's brother , Philip , was the ruler in the countries of Iturea and Trachonitis , and Lysanias was the ruler of Abilene .
42003002	Annas and Caiaphas were the Jewish high priests . At that time God spoke to Zechariah's son John , who was living in the desert .
42003003	So John went along the Jordan Valley , telling the people , “ Turn back to God and be baptized ! Then your sins will be forgiven . ”
42003004	Isaiah the prophet wrote about John when he said , “ In the desert someone is shouting , ‘ Get the road ready for the Lord ! Make a straight path for him .
42003005	Fill up every valley and level every mountain and hill . Straighten the crooked paths and smooth out the rough roads .
42003006	Then everyone will see the saving power of God . ’ ”
42003007	Crowds of people came out to be baptized , but John said to them , “ You bunch of snakes ! Who warned you to run from the coming judgment ?
42003008	Do something to show that you really have given up your sins . Don't start saying you belong to Abraham's family . God can turn these stones into children for Abraham .
42003009	An ax is ready to cut the trees down at their roots . Any tree that doesn't produce good fruit will be cut down and thrown into a fire . ”
42003010	The crowds asked John , “ What should we do ? ”
42003011	John told them , “ If you have two coats , give one to someone who doesn't have any . If you have food , share it with someone else . ”
42003012	When tax collectors came to be baptized , they asked John , “ Teacher , what should we do ? ”
42003013	John told them , “ Don't make people pay more than they owe . ”
42003014	Some soldiers asked him , “ And what about us ? What do we have to do ? ” John told them , “ Don't force people to pay money to make you leave them alone . Be satisfied with your pay . ”
42003015	Everyone became excited and wondered , “ Could John be the Messiah ? ”
42003016	John said , “ I am just baptizing with water . But someone more powerful is going to come , and I am not good enough even to untie his sandals . He will baptize you with the Holy Spirit and with fire .
42003017	His threshing fork is in his hand , and he is ready to separate the wheat from the husks . He will store the wheat in his barn and burn the husks with a fire that never goes out . ”
42003018	In many different ways John preached the good news to the people .
42003019	But to Herod the ruler , he said , “ It was wrong for you to take Herodias , your brother's wife . ” John also said Herod had done many other bad things .
42003020	Finally , Herod put John in jail , and this was the worst thing he had done .

44005004	The property was yours before you sold it , and even after you sold it , the money was still yours . What made you do such a thing ? You didn't lie to people . You lied to God ! ”
44005005	As soon as Ananias heard this , he dropped dead , and everyone who heard about it was frightened .
44005006	Some young men came in and wrapped up his body . Then they took it out and buried it .
44005007	Three hours later Sapphira came in , but she did not know what had happened to her husband .
44005008	Peter asked her , “ Tell me , did you sell the property for this amount ? ” “ Yes , ” she answered , “ that's the amount . ”
44005009	Then Peter said , “ Why did the two of you agree to test the Lord's Spirit ? The men who buried Ananias are by the door , and they will carry you out ! ”
44005010	At once she fell at Peter's feet and died . When the young men came back in , they found Sapphira lying there dead . So they carried her out and buried her beside her husband .

44007002	Stephen answered :

44008003	Saul started making a lot of trouble for the church . He went from house to house , arresting men and women and putting them in jail .

44008038	He ordered the chariot to stop . Then they both went down into the water , and Philip baptized him .

So a group of them went to see Blastus , who was one of Herod's high officials . They convinced Blastus that they wanted to make peace between their cities and Herod ,
44012021	and a day was set for them to meet with him . Herod came dressed in his royal robes . He sat down on his throne and made a speech .

44013006	Barnabas and Saul went all the way to the city of Paphos on the other end of the island , where they met a Jewish man named Bar-Jesus . He practiced witchcraft and was a false prophet .
44013007	He also worked for Sergius Paulus , who was very smart and was the governor of the island . Sergius Paulus wanted to hear God's message , and he sent for Barnabas and Saul .
44013008	But Bar-Jesus , whose other name was Elymas , was against them . He even tried to keep the governor from having faith in the Lord .
44013009	Then Saul , better known as Paul , was filled with the Holy Spirit . He looked straight at Elymas
44013010	and said , “ You son of the devil ! You are a liar , a crook , and an enemy of everything that is right . When will you stop speaking against the true ways of the Lord ?
44013011	The Lord is going to punish you by making you completely blind for a while . ” Suddenly the man's eyes were covered by a dark mist , and he went around trying to get someone to lead him by the hand .
44013012	When the governor saw what had happened , he was amazed at this teaching about the Lord . So he put his faith in the Lord .

44013041	“ Look , you people who make fun of God ! Be amazed and disappear . I will do something today that you won't believe , even if someone tells you about it ! ”
44013042	As Paul and Barnabas were leaving the synagogue , the people begged them to say more about these same things on the next Sabbath .
44013043	After the service , many Jews and a lot of Gentiles who worshiped God went with them . Paul and Barnabas begged them all to remain faithful to God , who had treated them with undeserved grace .
44013044	The next Sabbath almost everyone in town came to hear the message about the Lord .
44013045	When the Jewish people saw the crowds , they were very jealous . They insulted Paul and spoke against everything he said .
44013046	But Paul and Barnabas bravely said : “ I have placed you here as a light for the Gentiles . You are to take the saving power of God to people everywhere on earth . ”
44013048	This message made the Gentiles glad , and they praised what they had heard about the Lord . Everyone who had been chosen for eternal life then put their faith in the Lord .
44013049	The message about the Lord spread all over this region .
44013050	But the Jewish leaders went to some of the important men in the town and to some respected women who were religious . They turned them against Paul and Barnabas and started making trouble for them . They even chased them out of this part of the country .
44013051	Paul and Barnabas shook the dust from that place off their feet and went on to the city of Iconium .
44013052	But the Lord's followers in Antioch were very happy and were filled with the Holy Spirit .
44014001	Paul and Barnabas spoke in the synagogue in Iconium , just as they had done at Antioch , and many Jews and Gentiles put their faith in the Lord .
44014002	But the Jews who did not have faith in him made the other Gentiles angry and turned them against the Lord's followers .
44014003	Paul and Barnabas stayed there for a while , having faith in the Lord and bravely speaking his message . The Lord gave them the power to work miracles and wonders , and he showed that their message about his gift of undeserved grace was true .
44014004	The people of Iconium did not know what to think . Some of them believed the Jewish group , and others believed the apostles .
44014005	Finally , some Gentiles and Jews , together with their leaders , decided to make trouble for Paul and Barnabas and to stone them to death .
44014008	In Lystra there was a man who had been born with paralyzed feet and had never been able to walk .
44014009	The man was listening to Paul speak , when Paul saw that he had faith in Jesus and could be healed . So he looked straight at the man
44014010	and shouted , “ Stand up ! ” The man jumped up and started walking around .
44014011	When the crowd saw what Paul had done , they yelled out in the language of Lycaonia , “ The gods have turned into humans and have come down to us ! ”
44014012	The people then gave Barnabas the name Zeus , and they gave Paul the name Hermes , because he did the talking .
44014013	The temple of Zeus was near the entrance to the city . Its priest and the crowds wanted to offer a sacrifice to Barnabas and Paul . So the priest brought some bulls and flowers to the city gates .
44014014	When the two apostles found out about this , they tore their clothes in horror and ran to the crowd , shouting :
44014018	Even after Paul and Barnabas had said all this , they could hardly keep the people from offering a sacrifice to them .
44014019	Some Jewish leaders from Antioch and Iconium came and turned the crowds against Paul . They hit him with stones and dragged him out of the city , thinking he was dead .
44014020	But when the Lord's followers gathered around Paul , he stood up and went back into the city . The next day he and Barnabas went to Derbe .
44014021	Paul and Barnabas preached the good news in Derbe and won some people to the Lord . Then they went back to Lystra , Iconium , and Antioch in Pisidia .
44014022	They encouraged the followers and begged them to remain faithful . They told them , “ We have to suffer a lot before we can get into God's kingdom . ”
44014023	Paul and Barnabas chose some leaders for each of the churches . Then they went without eating and prayed that the Lord would take good care of these leaders who had trusted in the Lord .
44014024	Paul and Barnabas went on through Pisidia to Pamphylia ,
44014025	where they preached in the town of Perga . Then they went down to Attalia
44014026	and sailed to Antioch in Syria . It was there that they had been placed in God's care for the work they had now completed .
44014027	After arriving in Antioch , they called the church together . They told the people what God had helped them do and how he had made it possible for the Gentiles to believe .
44014028	Then they stayed there with the followers for a long time .
44015001	Some people came from Judea and started teaching the Lord's followers that they could not be saved , unless they were circumcised as Moses had taught .
44015002	This caused trouble , and Paul and Barnabas argued with them about this teaching . So it was decided to send Paul and Barnabas and a few others to Jerusalem to discuss this problem with the apostles and the church leaders .
44015003	The men who were sent by the church went through Phoenicia and Samaria , telling how the Gentiles had turned to God . This news made the Lord's followers very happy .
44015004	When the men arrived in Jerusalem , they were welcomed by the church , including the apostles and the leaders . They told them everything God had helped them do .
44015005	But some Pharisees had become followers of the Lord . They stood up and said , “ Gentiles who have faith in the Lord must be circumcised and told to obey the Law of Moses . ”
44015006	The apostles and church leaders met to discuss this problem about Gentiles .
44015007	They had talked it over for a long time , when Peter got up and said :
44015012	Everyone kept quiet and listened as Barnabas and Paul told how God had given them the power to work a lot of miracles and wonders for the Gentiles .
44015013	After they had finished speaking , James said :
44015016	“ I , the Lord , will return and rebuild David's fallen house . I will build it from its ruins and set it up again .
44015017	Then other nations will turn to me and be my chosen ones . I , the Lord , say this .
44015018	I promised it long ago . ”
44015022	The apostles , the leaders , and all the church members decided to send some men to Antioch along with Paul and Barnabas . They chose Silas and Judas Barsabbas , who were two leaders of the Lord's followers .
44015023	They wrote a letter that said :
44015030	The four men left Jerusalem and went to Antioch . Then they called the church members together and gave them the letter .
44015031	When the letter was read , everyone was pleased and greatly encouraged .
44015032	Judas and Silas were prophets , and they spoke a long time , encouraging and helping the Lord's followers .
44015033	The men from Jerusalem stayed on in Antioch for a while . And when they left to return to the ones who had sent them , the followers wished them well .
44015036	Sometime later Paul said to Barnabas , “ Let's go back and visit the Lord's followers in the cities where we preached his message . Then we will know how they are doing . ”
44015037	Barnabas wanted to take along John , whose other name was Mark .
44015038	But Paul did not want to , because Mark had left them in Pamphylia and had stopped working with them .
44015039	Paul and Barnabas argued , then each of them went his own way . Barnabas took Mark and sailed to Cyprus ,
44015040	but Paul took Silas and left after the followers had placed them in God's care .
44015041	They traveled through Syria and Cilicia , encouraging the churches .
44016001	Paul and Silas went back to Derbe and Lystra , where there was a follower named Timothy . His mother was also a follower . She was Jewish , and his father was Greek .
44016002	The Lord's followers in Lystra and Iconium said good things about Timothy ,
44016003	and Paul wanted him to go with them . But Paul first had him circumcised , because all the Jewish people around there knew that Timothy's father was Greek .
44016004	As Paul and the others went from city to city , they told the followers what the apostles and leaders in Jerusalem had decided , and they urged them to follow these instructions .
44016005	The churches became stronger in their faith , and each day more people put their faith in the Lord .
44016006	Paul and his friends went through Phrygia and Galatia , but the Holy Spirit would not let them preach in Asia .
44016007	After they arrived in Mysia , they tried to go into Bithynia , but the Spirit of Jesus would not let them .
44016008	So they went on through Mysia until they came to Troas .
44016009	During the night , Paul had a vision of someone from Macedonia who was standing there and begging him , “ Come over to Macedonia and help us ! ”
44016010	After Paul had seen the vision , we began looking for a way to go to Macedonia . We were sure that God had called us to preach the good news there .
44016011	We sailed straight from Troas to Samothrace , and the next day we arrived in Neapolis .
44016012	From there we went to Philippi , which is a Roman colony in the first district of Macedonia . We spent several days in Philippi .
44016013	Then on the Sabbath we went outside the city gate to a place by the river , where we thought there would be a Jewish meeting place for prayer . We sat down and talked with the women who came .
44016014	One of them was Lydia , who was from the city of Thyatira and sold expensive purple cloth . She was a worshiper of the Lord God , and he made her willing to accept what Paul was saying .
44016015	Then after she and her family were baptized , she kept on begging us , “ If you think I really do have faith in the Lord , come stay in my home . ” Finally , we accepted her invitation .
44016016	One day on our way to the place of prayer , we were met by a slave girl . She had a spirit in her that gave her the power to tell the future . By doing this she made a lot of money for her owners .
44016017	The girl followed Paul and the rest of us , and she kept yelling , “ These men are servants of the Most High God ! They are telling you how to be saved . ”
44016018	This went on for several days . Finally , Paul got so upset that he turned and said to the spirit , “ In the name of Jesus Christ , I order you to leave this girl alone ! ” At once the evil spirit left her .
44016019	When the girl's owners realized they had lost all chances for making more money , they grabbed Paul and Silas and dragged them into court .
44016020	They told the officials , “ These Jews are upsetting our city !
44016021	They are telling us to do things we Romans are not allowed to do . ”
44016022	The crowd joined in the attack on Paul and Silas . Then the officials tore the clothes off the two men and ordered them to be beaten with a whip .
44016023	After they had been badly beaten , they were put in jail , and the jailer was told to guard them carefully .
44016024	The jailer did as he was told . He put them deep inside the jail and chained their feet to heavy blocks of wood .
44016025	About midnight Paul and Silas were praying and singing praises to God , while the other prisoners listened .
44016026	Suddenly a strong earthquake shook the jail to its foundations . The doors opened , and the chains fell from all the prisoners .
44016027	When the jailer woke up and saw that the doors were open , he thought that the prisoners had escaped . He pulled out his sword and was about to kill himself .
44016028	But Paul shouted , “ Don't harm yourself ! No one has escaped . ”
44016029	The jailer asked for a torch and went into the jail . He was shaking all over as he knelt down in front of Paul and Silas .
44016030	After he had led them out of the jail , he asked , “ What must I do to be saved ? ”
44016031	They replied , “ Have faith in the Lord Jesus and you will be saved ! This is also true for everyone who lives in your home . ”
44016032	Then Paul and Silas told him and everyone else in his house about the Lord .
44016033	While it was still night , the jailer took them to a place where he could wash their cuts and bruises . Then he and everyone in his home were baptized .
44016034	They were very glad they had put their faith in God . After this , the jailer took Paul and Silas to his home and gave them something to eat .
44016035	The next morning the officials sent some police with orders for the jailer to let Paul and Silas go .
44016036	The jailer told Paul , “ The officials have ordered me to set you free . Now you can leave in peace . ”
44016037	But Paul told the police , “ We are Roman citizens , and the Roman officials had us beaten in public without giving us a trial . They threw us into jail . Now do they think they can secretly send us away ? No , they cannot ! They will have to come here themselves and let us out . ”
44016038	When the police told the officials that Paul and Silas were Roman citizens , the officials were afraid .
44016039	So they came and apologized . They led them out of the jail and asked them to please leave town .
44016040	But Paul and Silas went straight to the home of Lydia , where they saw the Lord's followers and encouraged them . Then they left .
44017001	After Paul and his friends had traveled through Amphipolis and Apollonia , they went on to Thessalonica . A synagogue was in that city .
44017002	So as usual , Paul went there to worship , and on three Sabbaths he spoke to the people . He used the Scriptures
44017003	to show them that the Messiah had to suffer , but that he would rise from death . Paul also told them that Jesus is the Messiah he was preaching about .
44017004	Some of them believed what Paul had said , and they became followers with Paul and Silas . Some Gentiles and many important women also believed the message .
44017005	The Jewish leaders were jealous and got some troublemakers who hung around the marketplace to start a riot in the city . They wanted to drag Paul and Silas out to the mob , and so they went straight to Jason's home .
44017006	But when they did not find them there , they dragged out Jason and some of the Lord's followers . They took them to the city authorities and shouted , “ Paul and Silas have been upsetting things everywhere . Now they have come here ,
44017007	and Jason has welcomed them into his home . All of them break the laws of the Roman Emperor by claiming that someone named Jesus is king . ”
44017008	The officials and the people were upset when they heard this .
44017009	So they made Jason and the other followers pay bail before letting them go .
44017010	That same night the Lord's followers sent Paul and Silas on to Berea , and after they arrived , they went to the synagogue .
44017011	The people in Berea were much nicer than those in Thessalonica , and they gladly accepted the message . Day after day they studied the Scriptures to see if these things were true .
44017012	Many of them put their faith in the Lord , including some important Greek women and several men .
44017013	When the Jewish leaders in Thessalonica heard that Paul had been preaching God's message in Berea , they went there and caused trouble by turning the crowds against Paul .
44017014	At once the followers sent Paul down to the coast , but Silas and Timothy stayed in Berea .
44017015	Some men went with Paul as far as Athens , and then returned with instructions for Silas and Timothy to join him as soon as possible .
44017016	While Paul was waiting in Athens , he was upset to see all the idols in the city .
44017017	He went to the synagogue to speak to the Jews and to anyone who worshiped with them . Day after day he also spoke to everyone he met in the market .
44017018	Some of them were Epicureans and some were Stoics , and they started arguing with him . People were asking , “ What is this know-it-all trying to say ? ” Some even said , “ Paul must be preaching about foreign gods ! That's what he means when he talks about Jesus and about people rising from death . ”
44017019	They brought Paul before a council called the Areopagus , and said , “ Tell us what your new teaching is all about .
44017020	We have heard you say some strange things , and we want to know what you mean . ”
44017021	More than anything else the people of Athens and the foreigners living there loved to hear and to talk about anything new .
44017022	So Paul stood up in front of the council and said :
44017032	As soon as the people heard Paul say a man had been raised from death , some of them started laughing . Others said , “ We will hear you talk about this some other time . ”
44017033	When Paul left the council meeting ,
44017034	some of the men put their faith in the Lord and went with Paul . One of them was a council member named Dionysius . A woman named Damaris and several others also put their faith in the Lord .
44018001	Paul left Athens and went to Corinth ,
44018002	where he met Aquila , a Jewish man from Pontus . Not long before this , Aquila had come from Italy with his wife Priscilla , because Emperor Claudius had ordered the Jewish people to leave Rome . Paul went to see Aquila and Priscilla
44018003	and found out they were tent makers . Paul was also a tent maker , so he stayed with them , and they worked together .
44018004	Every Sabbath , Paul went to the synagogue . He spoke to Jews and Gentiles and tried to win them over .
44018005	But after Silas and Timothy came from Macedonia , he spent all his time preaching to the Jews about Jesus the Messiah .
44018006	Finally , they turned against him and insulted him . So he shook the dust from his clothes and told them , “ Whatever happens to you will be your own fault ! I am not to blame . From now on I am going to preach to the Gentiles . ”
44018007	Paul then moved into the house of a man named Titius Justus , who worshiped God and lived next door to the synagogue .
44018008	Crispus was the leader of the synagogue . He and everyone in his family put their faith in the Lord . Many others in Corinth also heard the message , and all the people who had faith in the Lord were baptized .
44018009	One night , Paul had a vision , and in it the Lord said , “ Don't be afraid to keep on preaching . Don't stop !
44018010	I am with you , and you won't be harmed . Many people in this city belong to me . ”
44018011	Paul stayed on in Corinth for a year and a half , teaching God's message to the people .
44018012	While Gallio was governor of Achaia , some of the Jewish leaders got together and grabbed Paul . They brought him into court
44018013	and said , “ This man is trying to make our people worship God in a way that is against our Law ! ”
44018014	Even before Paul could speak , Gallio said , “ If you were charging this man with a crime or some other wrong , I would have to listen to you .
44018015	But since this concerns only words , names , and your own law , you will have to take care of it yourselves . I refuse to judge such matters . ”
44018016	Then he sent them out of the court .
44018017	The crowd grabbed Sosthenes , the Jewish leader , and beat him up in front of the court . But none of this mattered to Gallio .
44018018	After Paul had stayed for a while with the Lord's followers in Corinth , he told them goodbye and sailed on to Syria with Aquila and Priscilla . But before he left , he had his head shaved at Cenchreae because he had made a promise to God .
44018019	The three of them arrived in Ephesus , where Paul left Priscilla and Aquila . He then went into the synagogue to talk with the people there .
44018020	They asked him to stay longer , but he refused .
44018021	He told them goodbye and said , “ If God lets me , I will come back . ”
44018022	Paul sailed to Caesarea , where he greeted the church . Then he went on to Antioch .
44018023	After staying there for a while , he left and visited several places in Galatia and Phrygia . He helped the followers there to become stronger in their faith .
44018024	A Jewish man named Apollos came to Ephesus . Apollos had been born in the city of Alexandria . He was a very good speaker and knew a lot about the Scriptures .
44018025	He also knew much about the Lord's Way , and he spoke about it with great excitement . What he taught about Jesus was right , but all he knew was John's message about baptism .
44018026	Apollos started speaking bravely in the synagogue . But when Priscilla and Aquila heard him , they took him to their home and helped him understand God's Way even better .
44018027	Apollos decided to travel through Achaia . So the Lord's followers wrote letters , encouraging the followers there to welcome him . After Apollos arrived in Achaia , he was a great help to everyone who had put their faith in the Lord Jesus because of God's gift of undeserved grace .
44018028	He got into fierce arguments with the Jewish people , and in public he used the Scriptures to prove that Jesus is the Messiah .
44019001	While Apollos was in Corinth , Paul traveled across the hill country to Ephesus , where he met some of the Lord's followers .
44019002	He asked them , “ When you put your faith in Jesus , were you given the Holy Spirit ? ” “ No ! ” they answered . “ We have never even heard of the Holy Spirit . ”
44019003	“ Then why were you baptized ? ” Paul asked . They answered , “ Because of what John taught . ”
44019004	Paul replied , “ John baptized people so they would turn to God . But he also told them someone else was coming , and they should put their faith in him . Jesus is the one that John was talking about . ”
44019005	After the people heard Paul say this , they were baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus .
44019006	Then Paul placed his hands on them . The Holy Spirit was given to them , and they spoke unknown languages and prophesied .
44019007	There were about twelve men in this group .
44019008	For three months Paul went to the synagogue and talked bravely with the people about God's kingdom . He tried to win them over ,
44019009	but some of them were stubborn and refused to believe . In front of everyone they said terrible things about God's Way . Paul left and took the followers with him to the lecture hall of Tyrannus . He spoke there every day
44019010	for two years , until every Jew and Gentile in Asia had heard the Lord's message .
44019011	God gave Paul the power to work great miracles .
44019012	People even took handkerchiefs and aprons that had touched Paul's body , and they carried them to everyone who was sick . All of the sick people were healed , and the evil spirits went out .
