44019013	Some Jewish men started going around trying to force out evil spirits by using the name of the Lord Jesus . They said to the spirits , “ Come out in the name of that same Jesus that Paul preaches about ! ”
44019014	Seven sons of a high priest named Sceva were doing this ,
44019015	when an evil spirit said to them , “ I know Jesus ! And I have heard about Paul . But who are you ? ”
44019016	Then the man with the evil spirit jumped on them and beat them up . They ran out of the house , naked and bruised .
44019017	When the Jews and Gentiles in Ephesus heard about this , they were so frightened that they praised the name of the Lord Jesus .
44019018	Many who were followers now started telling everyone about the evil things they had been doing .
44019019	Some who had been practicing witchcraft even brought their books and burned them in public . These books were worth about 50,000 silver coins .
44019020	So the Lord's message spread and became even more powerful .
44019021	After all this had happened , Paul decided to visit Macedonia and Achaia on his way to Jerusalem . Paul had said , “ From there I will go on to Rome . ”
44019022	So he sent his two helpers , Timothy and Erastus , to Macedonia . But he stayed on in Asia for a while .
44019023	At that time there was serious trouble because of the Lord's Way .
44019024	A silversmith named Demetrius had a business that made silver models of the temple of the goddess Artemis . Those who worked for him earned a lot of money .
44019025	Demetrius brought together everyone who was in the same business and said :
44019028	When the workers heard this , they got angry and started shouting , “ Great is Artemis , the goddess of the Ephesians ! ”
44019029	Soon the whole city was in a riot , and some men grabbed Gaius and Aristarchus , who had come from Macedonia with Paul . Then everyone in the crowd rushed to the place where the town meetings were held .
44019030	Paul wanted to go out and speak to the people , but the Lord's followers would not let him .
44019031	A few of the local officials were friendly to Paul , and they sent someone to warn him not to go .
44019032	Some of the people in the meeting were shouting one thing , and others were shouting something else . Everyone was completely confused , and most of them did not even know why they were there .
44019033	Several of the Jewish leaders pushed a man named Alexander to the front of the crowd and started telling him what to say . He motioned with his hand and tried to explain what was going on .
44019034	But when the crowd saw that he was Jewish , they all shouted for two hours , “ Great is Artemis , the goddess of the Ephesians ! ”
44019035	Finally , a town official made the crowd be quiet . Then he said :
44019041	After saying this , he told the people to leave .
44020001	When the riot was over , Paul sent for the followers and encouraged them . He then told them goodbye and left for Macedonia .
44020002	As he traveled from place to place , he encouraged the followers with many messages . Finally , he went to Greece
44020003	and stayed there for three months . Paul was about to sail to Syria . But some of the Jewish leaders plotted against him , so he decided to return by way of Macedonia .
44020004	With him were Sopater , son of Pyrrhus from Berea , and Aristarchus and Secundus from Thessalonica . Gaius from Derbe was also with him , and so were Timothy and the two Asians , Tychicus and Trophimus .
44020005	They went on ahead to Troas and waited for us there .
44020006	After the Festival of Thin Bread , we sailed from Philippi . Five days later we met them in Troas and stayed there for a week .
44020007	On the first day of the week we met to break bread together . Paul spoke to the people until midnight because he was leaving the next morning .
44020008	In the upstairs room where we were meeting , there were a lot of lamps .
44020009	A young man by the name of Eutychus was sitting on a window sill . While Paul was speaking , the young man got very sleepy . Finally , he went to sleep and fell three floors all the way down to the ground . When they picked him up , he was dead .
44020010	Paul went down and bent over Eutychus . He took him in his arms and said , “ Don't worry ! He's alive . ”
44020011	After Paul had gone back upstairs , he broke bread , and ate with us . He then spoke until dawn and left .
44020012	Then the followers took the young man home alive and were very happy .
44020013	Paul decided to travel by land to Assos . The rest of us went on ahead by ship , and we were to take him aboard there .
44020014	When he met us in Assos , he came aboard , and we sailed on to Mitylene .
44020015	The next day we came to a place near Chios , and the following day we reached Samos . The day after that we sailed to Miletus .
44020016	Paul had decided to sail on past Ephesus , because he did not want to spend too much time in Asia . He was in a hurry and wanted to be in Jerusalem in time for Pentecost .
44020017	From Miletus , Paul sent a message for the church leaders at Ephesus to come and meet with him .
44020018	When they got there , he said :
44020036	After Paul had finished speaking , he knelt down with all of them and prayed .
44020037	Everyone cried and hugged and kissed him .
44020038	They were especially sad because Paul had told them , “ You will never see me again . ” Then they went with him to the ship .
44021001	After saying goodbye , we sailed straight to Cos . The next day we reached Rhodes and from there sailed on to Patara .
44021002	We found a ship going to Phoenicia , so we got on board and sailed off .
44021003	We came within sight of Cyprus and then sailed south of it on to the port of Tyre in Syria , where the ship was going to unload its cargo .
44021004	We found the Lord's followers and stayed with them for a week . The Holy Spirit had told them to warn Paul not to go on to Jerusalem .
44021005	But when the week was over , we started on our way again . All the men , together with their wives and children , walked with us from the town to the seashore . We knelt on the beach and prayed .
44021006	Then after saying goodbye to each other , we got into the ship , and they went back home .
44021007	We sailed from Tyre to Ptolemais , where we greeted the followers and stayed with them for a day .
44021008	The next day we went to Caesarea and stayed with Philip , the preacher . He was one of the seven men who helped the apostles ,
44021009	and he had four unmarried daughters who prophesied .
44021010	We had been in Caesarea for several days , when the prophet Agabus came to us from Judea .
44021011	He took Paul's belt , and with it he tied up his own hands and feet . Then he told us , “ The Holy Spirit says that some of the Jewish leaders in Jerusalem will tie up the man who owns this belt . They will also hand him over to the Gentiles . ”
44021012	After Agabus said this , we and the followers living there begged Paul not to go to Jerusalem .
44021013	But Paul answered , “ Why are you crying and breaking my heart ? I am not only willing to be put in jail for the Lord Jesus , but I am even willing to die for him in Jerusalem ! ”
44021014	Since we could not get Paul to change his mind , we gave up and prayed , “ Lord , please make us willing to do what you want . ”
44021015	Then we got ready to go to Jerusalem .
44021016	Some of the followers from Caesarea went with us and took us to stay in the home of Mnason . He was from Cyprus and had been a follower from the beginning .
44021017	When we arrived in Jerusalem , the Lord's followers gladly welcomed us .
44021018	Paul went with us to see James the next day , and all the church leaders were present .
44021019	Paul greeted them and told how God had used him to help the Gentiles .
44021020	Everyone who heard this praised God and said to Paul :
44021026	The next day Paul took the four men with him and got himself ready at the same time they did . Then he went into the temple and told when the final ceremony would take place and when an offering would be made for each of them .
44021027	When the period of seven days for the ceremony was almost over , some of the Jewish people from Asia saw Paul in the temple . They got a large crowd together and started attacking him .
44021028	They were shouting , “ Friends , help us ! This man goes around everywhere , saying bad things about our nation and about the Law of Moses and about this temple . He has even brought shame to this holy temple by bringing in Gentiles . ”
44021029	Some of them thought that Paul had brought Trophimus from Ephesus into the temple , because they had seen them together in the city .
44021030	The whole city was in an uproar , and the people turned into a mob . They grabbed Paul and dragged him out of the temple . Then suddenly the doors were shut .
44021031	The people were about to kill Paul when the Roman army commander heard that all Jerusalem was starting to riot .
44021032	So he quickly took some soldiers and officers and ran to where the crowd had gathered . As soon as the mob saw the commander and soldiers , they stopped beating Paul .
44021033	The army commander went over and arrested him and had him bound with two chains . Then he tried to find out who Paul was and what he had done .
44021034	Part of the crowd shouted one thing , and part of them shouted something else . But they were making so much noise that the commander could not find out a thing . Then he ordered Paul to be taken into the fortress .
44021035	As they reached the steps , the crowd became so wild that the soldiers had to lift Paul up and carry him .
44021036	The crowd followed and kept shouting , “ Kill him ! Kill him ! ”
44021037	When Paul was about to be taken into the fortress , he asked the commander , “ Can I say something to you ? ” “ How do you know Greek ? ” the commander asked .
44021038	“ Aren't you that Egyptian who started a riot not long ago and led 4,000 terrorists into the desert ? ”
44021039	“ No ! ” Paul replied . “ I am a Jew from Tarsus , an important city in Cilicia . Please let me speak to the crowd . ”
44021040	The commander told him he could speak , so Paul stood on the steps and motioned to the people . When they were quiet , he spoke to them in Aramaic :
44022001	“ My friends and leaders of our nation , listen as I explain what happened ! ”
44022002	When the crowd heard Paul speak to them in Aramaic , they became even quieter . Then Paul said :
44022022	The crowd listened until Paul said this . Then they started shouting , “ Get rid of this man ! He doesn't deserve to live . ”
44022023	They kept shouting . They waved their clothes around and threw dust into the air .
44022024	The Roman commander ordered Paul to be taken into the fortress and beaten with a whip . He did this to find out why the people were screaming at Paul .
44022025	While the soldiers were tying Paul up to be beaten , he asked the officer standing there , “ Is it legal to beat a Roman citizen before he has been tried in court ? ”
44022026	When the officer heard this , he went to the commander and said , “ What are you doing ? This man is a Roman citizen ! ”
44022027	The commander went to Paul and asked , “ Tell me , are you a Roman citizen ? ” “ Yes , ” Paul answered .
44022028	The commander then said , “ I paid a lot of money to become a Roman citizen . ” But Paul replied , “ I was born a Roman citizen . ”
44022029	The men who were about to beat and question Paul quickly backed off . And the commander himself was frightened when he realized that he had put a Roman citizen in chains .
44022030	The next day the commander wanted to know the real reason why the Jewish leaders had brought charges against Paul . So he had Paul's chains removed , and he ordered the chief priests and the whole council to meet . Then he had Paul led in and made him stand in front of them .
44023001	Paul looked straight at the council members and said , “ My friends , to this day I have served God with a clear conscience ! ”
44023002	Then Ananias the high priest ordered the men standing beside Paul to hit him on the mouth .
44023003	Paul turned to the high priest and said , “ You whitewashed wall ! God will hit you . You sit there to judge me by the Law of Moses . But at the same time you order men to break the Law by hitting me . ”
44023004	The men standing beside Paul asked , “ Don't you know you are insulting God's high priest ? ”
44023005	Paul replied , “ Oh ! I didn't know he was the high priest . The Scriptures do tell us not to speak evil about a leader of our people . ”
44023006	When Paul saw that some of the council members were Sadducees and others were Pharisees , he shouted , “ My friends , I am a Pharisee and the son of a Pharisee . I am on trial simply because I believe that the dead will be raised to life . ”
44023007	As soon as Paul said this , the Pharisees and the Sadducees got into a big argument , and the council members started taking sides .
44023008	The Sadducees do not believe in angels or spirits or that the dead will rise to life . But the Pharisees believe in all of these ,
44023009	and so there was a lot of shouting . Some of the teachers of the Law of Moses were Pharisees . Finally , they became angry and said , “ We don't find anything wrong with this man . Maybe a spirit or an angel really did speak to him . ”
44023010	The argument became fierce , and the commander was afraid that Paul would be pulled apart . So he ordered the soldiers to go in and rescue Paul . Then they took him back into the fortress .
44023011	That night the Lord stood beside Paul and said , “ Don't worry ! Just as you have told others about me in Jerusalem , you must also tell about me in Rome . ”
44023014	Then some of them went to the chief priests and the nation's leaders and said , “ We have promised God that we would not eat a thing until we have killed Paul .
44023015	You and everyone in the council must go to the commander and pretend that you want to find out more about the charges against Paul . Ask for him to be brought before your court . Meanwhile , we will be waiting to kill him before he gets there . ”
44023016	When Paul's nephew heard about the plot , he went to the fortress and told Paul about it .
44023017	So Paul said to one of the army officers , “ Take this young man to the commander . He has something to tell him . ”
44023018	The officer took him to the commander and said , “ The prisoner named Paul asked me to bring this young man to you , because he has something to tell you . ”
44023019	The commander took the young man aside and asked him in private , “ What do you want to tell me ? ”
44023020	He answered , “ Some men are planning to ask you to bring Paul down to the Jewish council tomorrow . They will claim they want to find out more about him .
44023021	But please don't do what they say . More than 40 men are going to attack Paul . They have made a vow not to eat or drink anything until they have killed him . Even now they are waiting to hear what you decide . ”
44023022	The commander sent the young man away after saying to him , “ Don't let anyone know you told me this . ”
44023023	The commander called in two of his officers and told them , “ By nine o'clock tonight have 200 soldiers ready to go to Caesarea . Take along 70 men on horseback and 200 foot soldiers with spears .
44023024	Get a horse ready for Paul and make sure he gets safely through to Felix the governor . ”
44023025	The commander wrote a letter that said :
44023031	The soldiers obeyed the commander's orders , and that same night they took Paul to the city of Antipatris .
44023032	The next day the foot soldiers returned to the fortress and let the soldiers on horseback take him the rest of the way .
44023033	When they came to Caesarea , they gave the letter to the governor and handed Paul over to him .
44023034	The governor read the letter . Then he asked Paul and found out that he was from Cilicia .
44023035	The governor said , “ I will listen to your case as soon as the people come to bring their charges against you . ” After saying this , he gave orders for Paul to be kept as a prisoner in Herod's palace .
44024001	Five days later Ananias the high priest , together with some of their leaders and a lawyer named Tertullus , went to the governor to present their case against Paul .
44024002	So Paul was called in , and Tertullus stated the case against him :
44024009	The Jewish crowd spoke up and agreed with what Tertullus had said .
44024010	The governor motioned for Paul to speak , and he began :
44024022	Felix knew a lot about the Lord's Way . But he brought the trial to an end and said , “ I will make my decision after Lysias the commander arrives . ”
44024023	He then ordered the army officer to keep Paul under guard , but not to lock him up or to stop his friends from helping him .
44024024	Several days later Felix and his wife Drusilla , who was Jewish , went to the place where Paul was kept under guard . They sent for Paul and listened while he spoke to them about having faith in Christ Jesus .
44024025	But Felix was frightened when Paul started talking to them about doing right , about self-control , and about the coming judgment . So he said to Paul , “ That's enough for now . You may go . But when I have time I will send for you . ”
44024026	After this , Felix often sent for Paul and talked with him , because he hoped that Paul would offer him a bribe .
44024027	Two years later Porcius Festus became governor in place of Felix . But since Felix wanted to do the Jewish leaders a favor , he kept Paul in jail .
44025001	Three days after Festus had become governor , he went from Caesarea to Jerusalem .
44025002	There the chief priests and some Jewish leaders told him about their charges against Paul . They also asked Festus
44025003	if he would be willing to bring Paul to Jerusalem . They begged him to do this because they were planning to attack and kill Paul on the way .
44025004	But Festus told them , “ Paul will be kept in Caesarea , and I am soon going there myself .
44025005	If he has done anything wrong , let your leaders go with me and bring charges against him there . ”
44025006	Festus stayed in Jerusalem for eight or ten more days before going to Caesarea . Then the next day he took his place as judge and had Paul brought into court .
44025007	As soon as Paul came in , the leaders from Jerusalem crowded around him and said he was guilty of many serious crimes . But they could not prove anything .
44025008	Then Paul spoke in his own defense , “ I have not broken the Law of my people . And I have not done anything against either the temple or the Emperor . ”
44025009	Festus wanted to please the leaders . So he asked Paul , “ Are you willing to go to Jerusalem and be tried by me on these charges ? ”
44025010	Paul replied , “ I am on trial in the Emperor's court , and that's where I should be tried . You know very well I have not done anything to harm the Jewish nation .
44025011	If I had done something deserving death , I would not ask to escape the death penalty . But I am not guilty of any of these crimes , and no one has the right to hand me over to these people . I now ask to be tried by the Emperor himself . ”
44025012	After Festus had talked this over with members of his council , he told Paul , “ You have asked to be tried by the Emperor , and to the Emperor you will go ! ”
44025013	A few days later King Agrippa and Bernice came to Caesarea to visit Festus .
44025014	They had been there for several days , when Festus told the king about the charges against Paul . He said :
44025022	Then Agrippa said to Festus , “ I would also like to hear what this man has to say . ” Festus answered , “ You can hear him tomorrow . ”
44025023	The next day Agrippa and Bernice made a big show as they came into the meeting room . High ranking army officers and leading citizens of the town were also there . Festus then ordered Paul to be brought in
44025024	and said :
44026001	Agrippa told Paul , “ You may now speak for yourself . ” Paul stretched out his hand and said :
44026024	Before Paul finished defending himself , Festus shouted , “ Paul , you're crazy ! Too much learning has driven you out of your mind . ”
44026025	But Paul replied , “ Honorable Festus , I am not crazy . What I am saying is true , and it makes sense .
44026026	None of these things happened off in a corner somewhere . I am sure that King Agrippa knows what I am talking about . That's why I can speak so plainly to him . ”
44026027	Then Paul said to Agrippa , “ Do you believe what the prophets said ? I know you do . ”
44026028	Agrippa asked Paul , “ In such a short time do you think you can talk me into being a Christian ? ”
44026029	Paul answered , “ Whether it takes a short time or a long time , I wish you and everyone else who hears me today would become just like me ! Except , of course , for these chains . ”
44026030	Then King Agrippa , Governor Festus , Bernice , and everyone who was with them got up .
44026031	But before they left , they said , “ This man isn't guilty of anything . He doesn't deserve to die or to be put in jail . ”
44026032	Agrippa told Festus , “ Paul could have been set free , if he had not asked to be tried by the Roman Emperor . ”
44027001	When it was time for us to sail to Rome , Captain Julius from the Emperor's special troops was put in charge of Paul and the other prisoners .
44027002	We went aboard a ship from Adramyttium that was about to sail to some ports along the coast of Asia . Aristarchus from Thessalonica in Macedonia sailed on the ship with us .
44027003	The next day we came to shore at Sidon . Captain Julius was very kind to Paul . He even let him visit his friends , so they could give him whatever he needed .
44027004	When we left Sidon , the winds were blowing against us , and we sailed close to the island of Cyprus to be safe from the wind .
44027005	Then we sailed south of Cilicia and Pamphylia until we came to the port of Myra in Lycia .
44027006	There the army captain found a ship from Alexandria that was going to Italy . So he ordered us to board that ship .
44027007	We sailed along slowly for several days and had a hard time reaching Cnidus . The wind would not let us go any farther in that direction , so we sailed past Cape Salmone , where the island of Crete would protect us from the wind .
44027008	We went slowly along the coast and finally reached a place called Fair Havens , not far from the town of Lasea .
44027009	By now we had already lost a lot of time , and sailing was no longer safe . In fact , even the Great Day of Forgiveness was past .
44027010	Then Paul spoke to the crew of the ship , “ Men , listen to me ! If we sail now , our ship and its cargo will be badly damaged , and many lives will be lost . ”
44027011	But Julius listened to the captain of the ship and its owner , rather than to Paul .
44027012	The harbor at Fair Havens wasn't a good place to spend the winter . Because of this , almost everyone agreed that we should at least try to sail along the coast of Crete as far as Phoenix . It had a harbor that opened toward the southwest and northwest , and we could spend the winter there .
44027013	When a gentle wind from the south started blowing , the men thought it was a good time to do what they had planned . So they pulled up the anchor , and we sailed along the coast of Crete .
44027014	But soon a strong wind called “ The Northeaster ” blew against us from the island .
44027015	The wind struck the ship , and we could not sail against it . So we let the wind carry the ship .
44027016	We went along the island of Cauda on the side that was protected from the wind . We had a hard time holding the lifeboat in place ,
44027017	but finally we got it where it belonged . Then the sailors wrapped ropes around the ship to hold it together . They lowered the sail and let the ship drift along , because they were afraid it might hit the sandbanks in the gulf of Syrtis .
44027018	The storm was so fierce that the next day they threw some of the ship's cargo overboard .
44027019	Then on the third day , with their bare hands they threw overboard some of the ship's gear .
44027020	For several days we could not see either the sun or the stars . A strong wind kept blowing , and we finally gave up all hope of being saved .
44027021	Since none of us had eaten anything for a long time , Paul stood up and told the men :
44027027	For 14 days and nights we had been blown around over the Mediterranean Sea . But about midnight the sailors realized we were getting near land .
44027028	They measured and found that the water was about 40 meters deep . A little later they measured again and found it was only about 30 meters .
44027029	The sailors were afraid that we might hit some rocks , and they let down four anchors from the back of the ship . Then they prayed for daylight .
44027030	The sailors wanted to escape from the ship . So they lowered the lifeboat into the water , pretending that they were letting down some anchors from the front of the ship .
44027031	But Paul said to Captain Julius and the soldiers , “ If the sailors don't stay on the ship , you won't have any chance to save your lives . ”
44027032	The soldiers then cut the ropes that held the lifeboat and let it fall into the sea .
44027033	Just before daylight Paul begged the people to eat something . He told them , “ For 14 days you have been so worried that you haven't eaten a thing .
44027034	I beg you to eat something . Your lives depend on it . Do this and not one of you will be hurt . ”
44027035	After Paul had said this , he took a piece of bread and gave thanks to God . Then in front of everyone , he broke the bread and ate some .
44027036	They all felt encouraged , and each of them ate something .
44027037	There were 276 people on the ship ,
44027038	and after everyone had eaten , they threw the cargo of wheat into the sea to make the ship lighter .
44027039	Morning came , and the ship's crew saw a coast they did not recognize . But they did see a cove with a beach . So they decided to try to run the ship aground on the beach .
44027040	They cut the anchors loose and let them sink into the sea . At the same time they untied the ropes that were holding the rudders . Next , they raised the sail at the front of the ship and let the wind carry the ship toward the beach .
44027041	But it ran aground on a sandbank . The front of the ship stuck firmly in the sand , and the rear was being smashed by the force of the waves .
44027042	The soldiers decided to kill the prisoners to keep them from swimming away and escaping .
44027043	But Captain Julius wanted to save Paul's life , and he did not let the soldiers do what they had planned . Instead , he ordered everyone who could swim to jump into the water and head for shore .
44027044	Then he told the others to hold on to planks of wood or parts of the ship . At last , everyone safely reached shore .
44028001	When we came ashore , we learned that the island was called Malta .
44028002	The local people were very friendly , and they welcomed us by building a fire , because it was rainy and cold .
44028003	After Paul had gathered some wood and had put it on the fire , the heat caused a snake to crawl out , and it bit him on the hand .
44028004	When the local people saw the snake hanging from Paul's hand , they said to each other , “ This man must be a murderer ! He didn't drown in the sea , but the goddess of justice will kill him anyway . ”
44028005	Paul shook the snake off into the fire and wasn't harmed .
44028006	The people kept thinking that Paul would either swell up or suddenly drop dead . They watched him for a long time , and when nothing happened to him , they changed their minds and said , “ This man is a god . ”
44028007	The governor of the island was named Publius , and he owned some of the land around there . Publius was very friendly and welcomed us into his home for three days .
44028008	His father was in bed , sick with fever and stomach trouble , and Paul went to visit him . Paul healed the man by praying and placing his hands on him .
44028009	After this happened , everyone on the island brought their sick people to Paul , and they were all healed .
44028010	The people were very respectful to us , and when we sailed , they gave us everything we needed .
44028011	Three months later we sailed in a ship that had been docked at Malta for the winter . The ship was from Alexandria in Egypt and was known as “ The Twin Gods . ”
44028012	We arrived in Syracuse and stayed for three days .
44028013	From there we sailed to Rhegium . The next day a south wind began to blow , and two days later we arrived in Puteoli .
44028014	There we found some of the Lord's followers , who begged us to stay with them . A week later we left for the city of Rome .
44028015	Some of the followers in Rome heard about us and came to meet us at the Market of Appius and at the Three Inns . When Paul saw them , he thanked God and was encouraged .
44028016	We arrived in Rome , and Paul was allowed to live in a house by himself with a soldier to guard him .
44028017	Three days after we got there , Paul called together some of the Jewish leaders and said :
44028021	The leaders replied , “ No one from Judea has written us a letter about you . And not one of them has come here to report on you or to say anything against you .
44028022	But we would like to hear what you have to say . We understand that people everywhere are against this new group . ”
44028023	They agreed on a time to meet with Paul , and many of them came to his house . From early morning until late in the afternoon , Paul talked to them about God's kingdom . He used the Law of Moses and the Books of the Prophets to try to win them over to Jesus .
44028024	Some of the leaders agreed with what Paul said , but others did not .
44028025	Since they could not agree among themselves , they started leaving . But Paul said , “ The Holy Spirit said the right thing when he sent Isaiah the prophet
44028026	to tell our ancestors , ‘ Go to these people and tell them : You will listen and listen , but never understand . You will look and look , but never see .
44028027	All of you have stubborn hearts . Your ears are stopped up , and your eyes are covered . You cannot see or hear or understand . If you could , you would turn to me , and I would heal you . ’ ”
44028030	For two years Paul stayed in a rented house and welcomed everyone who came to see him .
44028031	He bravely preached about God's kingdom and taught about the Lord Jesus Christ , and no one tried to stop him .
45001001	From Paul , a servant of Christ Jesus . God chose me to be an apostle , and he appointed me to preach the good news
45001002	that he promised long ago by what his prophets said in the holy Scriptures .
45001005	Jesus was kind to me and chose me to be an apostle , so that people of all nations would obey and have faith .
45001006	You are some of those people chosen by Jesus Christ .
45001007	This letter is to all of you in Rome . God loves you and has chosen you to be his very own people . I pray that God our Father and our Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
45001008	First , I thank God in the name of Jesus Christ for all of you . I do this because people everywhere in the world are talking about your faith .
45001009	God has seen how I never stop praying for you , while I serve him with all my heart and tell the good news about his Son .
45001010	In all my prayers , I ask God to make it possible for me to visit you .
45001011	I want to see you and share with you the same blessings that God's Spirit has given me . Then you will grow stronger in your faith .
45001012	What I am saying is that we can encourage each other by the faith that is ours .
45001013	My friends , I want you to know that I have often planned to come for a visit . But something has always kept me from doing it . I want to win followers to Christ in Rome , as I have done in many other places .
45001016	I am proud of the good news ! It is God's powerful way of saving all people who have faith , whether they are Jews or Gentiles .
45001017	The good news tells how God accepts everyone who has faith , but only those who have faith . It is just as the Scriptures say , “ The people God accepts because of their faith will live . ”
45001018	From heaven God shows how angry he is with all the wicked and evil things that sinful people do to crush the truth .
45001019	They know everything that can be known about God , because God has shown it all to them .
45001020	God's eternal power and character cannot be seen . But from the beginning of creation , God has shown what these are like by all he has made . That's why those people don't have any excuse .
45001021	They know about God , but they don't honor him or even thank him . Their thoughts are useless , and their stupid minds are in the dark .
45001022	They claim to be wise , but they are fools .
45001023	They don't worship the glorious and eternal God . Instead , they worship idols that are made to look like humans who cannot live forever , and like birds , animals , and reptiles .
45001024	So God let these people go their own way . They did what they wanted to do , and their filthy thoughts made them do shameful things with their bodies .
45001025	They gave up the truth about God for a lie , and they worshiped God's creation instead of God , who will be praised forever . Amen .
45001026	God let them follow their own evil desires . Women no longer wanted to have sex in a natural way , and they did things with each other that were not natural .
45001027	Men behaved in the same way . They stopped wanting to have sex with women and had strong desires for sex with other men . They did shameful things with each other , and what has happened to them is punishment for their foolish deeds .
45001028	Since these people refused even to think about God , he let their useless minds rule over them . That's why they do all sorts of indecent things .
45001029	They are evil , wicked , and greedy , as well as mean in every possible way . They want what others have , and they murder , argue , cheat , and are hard to get along with . They gossip ,
45001030	say cruel things about others , and hate God . They are proud , conceited , and boastful , always thinking up new ways to do evil . These people don't respect their parents .
45001031	They are stupid , unreliable , and don't have any love or pity for others .
45001032	They know God has said that anyone who acts this way deserves to die . But they keep on doing evil things , and they even encourage others to do them .
45002001	Some of you accuse others of doing wrong . But there is no excuse for what you do . When you judge others , you condemn yourselves , because you are guilty of doing the very same things .
45002002	We know that God is right to judge everyone who behaves in this way .
45002003	Do you really think God won't punish you , when you behave exactly like the people you accuse ?
45002004	You surely don't think much of God's wonderful goodness or of his patience and willingness to put up with you . Don't you know that the reason God is good to you is because he wants you to turn to him ?
45002005	But you are stubborn and refuse to turn to God . So you are making things even worse for yourselves on that day when he will show how angry he is and will judge the world with fairness .
45002006	God will reward each of us for what we have done .
45002007	He will give eternal life to everyone who has patiently done what is good in the hope of receiving glory , honor , and life that lasts forever .
45002008	But he will show how angry and furious he can be with every selfish person who rejects the truth and wants to do evil .
45002009	All who are wicked will be punished with trouble and suffering . It doesn't matter if they are Jews or Gentiles .
45002010	But all who do right will be rewarded with glory , honor , and peace , whether they are Jews or Gentiles .
45002011	God doesn't have any favorites !
45002012	Those people who don't know about God's Law will still be punished for what they do wrong . And the Law will be used to judge everyone who knows what it says .
45002013	God accepts those who obey his Law , but not those who simply hear it .
45002014	Some people naturally obey the Law's commands , even though they don't have the Law .
45002015	This proves that the conscience is like a law written in the human heart . And it will show whether we are forgiven or condemned ,
45002016	when God appoints Jesus Christ to judge everyone's secret thoughts , just as my message says .
45002017	Some of you call yourselves Jews . You trust in the Law and take pride in God .
45002018	By reading the Scriptures you learn how God wants you to behave , and you discover what is right .
45002019	You are sure that you are a guide for the blind and a light for all who are in the dark .
45002020	And since there is knowledge and truth in God's Law , you think you can instruct fools and teach young people .
45002021	But how can you teach others when you refuse to learn ? You preach it is wrong to steal . But do you steal ?
45002022	You say people should be faithful in marriage . But are you faithful ? You hate idols , yet you rob their temples .
45002023	You take pride in the Law , but you disobey the Law and bring shame to God .
45002024	It is just as the Scriptures tell us , “ You have made foreigners say insulting things about God . ”
45002025	Being circumcised is worthwhile , if you obey the Law . But if you don't obey the Law , you are no better off than people who are not circumcised .
45002026	In fact , if they obey the Law , they are as good as anyone who is circumcised .
45002027	So everyone who obeys the Law , but has never been circumcised , will condemn you . Even though you are circumcised and have the Law , you still don't obey its teachings .
45002028	Just because you live like a Jew and are circumcised doesn't make you a real Jew .
45002029	To be a real Jew you must obey the Law . True circumcision is something that happens deep in your heart , not something done to your body . And besides , you should want praise from God and not from humans .
45003001	What good is it to be a Jew ? What good is it to be circumcised ?
45003002	It is good in a lot of ways ! First of all , God's messages were spoken to the Jews .
45003003	It is true that some of them did not believe the message . But does this mean that God cannot be trusted , just because they did not have faith ?
45003004	No , indeed ! God tells the truth , even if everyone else is a liar . The Scriptures say about God , “ Your words will be proven true , and in court you will win your case . ”
45003005	If our evil deeds show how right God is , then what can we say ? Is it wrong for God to become angry and punish us ? What a foolish thing to ask .
45003006	But the answer is , “ No . ” Otherwise , how could God judge the world ?
45003007	Since your lies bring great honor to God by showing how truthful he is , you may ask why God still says you are a sinner .
45003008	You might as well say , “ Let's do something evil , so that something good will come of it ! ” Some people even claim that we are saying this . But God is fair and will judge them as well .
45003009	What does all this mean ? Does it mean that we Jews are better off than the Gentiles ? No , it doesn't ! Jews , as well as Gentiles , are ruled by sin , just as I have said .
45003010	The Scriptures tell us , “ No one is acceptable to God !
45003011	Not one of them understands or even searches for God .
45003012	They have all turned away and are worthless . There isn't one person who does right .
45003013	Their words are like an open pit , and their tongues are good only for telling lies . Each word is as deadly as the fangs of a snake ,
45003014	and they say nothing but bitter curses .
45003015	These people quickly become violent .
45003016	Wherever they go , they leave ruin and destruction .
45003017	They don't know how to live in peace .
45003018	They don't even fear God . ”
45003019	We know that everything in the Law was written for those who are under its power . The Law says these things to stop anyone from making excuses and to let God show that the whole world is guilty .
45003020	God doesn't accept people simply because they obey the Law . No , indeed ! All the Law does is to point out our sin .
45003021	Now we see how God does make us acceptable to him . The Law and the Prophets tell how we become acceptable , and it isn't by obeying the Law of Moses .
45003022	God treats everyone alike . He accepts people only because they have faith in Jesus Christ .
45003023	All of us have sinned and fallen short of God's glory .
45003024	But God treats us much better than we deserve , and because of Christ Jesus , he freely accepts us and sets us free from our sins .
45003027	What is left for us to brag about ? Not a thing ! Is it because we obeyed some law ? No ! It is because of faith .
45003028	We see that people are acceptable to God because they have faith , and not because they obey the Law .
45003029	Does God belong only to the Jews ? Isn't he also the God of the Gentiles ? Yes , he is !
45003030	There is only one God , and he accepts Gentiles as well as Jews , simply because of their faith .
45003031	Do we destroy the Law by our faith ? Not at all ! We make it even more powerful .
45004001	Well then , what can we say about our ancestor Abraham ?
45004002	If he became acceptable to God because of what he did , then he would have something to brag about . But he would never be able to brag about it to God .
45004003	The Scriptures say , “ God accepted Abraham because Abraham had faith in him . ”
45004004	Money paid to workers isn't a gift . It is something they earn by working .
45004005	But you cannot make God accept you because of something you do . God accepts sinners only because they have faith in him .
45004006	In the Scriptures David talks about the blessings that come to people who are acceptable to God , even though they don't do anything to deserve these blessings . David says ,
45004009	Are these blessings meant for circumcised people or for those who are not circumcised ? Well , the Scriptures say that God accepted Abraham because Abraham had faith in him .
45004010	But when did this happen ? Was it before or after Abraham was circumcised ? Of course , it was before .
45004011	Abraham let himself be circumcised to show he had been accepted because of his faith even before he was circumcised . This makes Abraham the father of all who are acceptable to God because of their faith , even though they are not circumcised .
45004012	This also makes Abraham the father of everyone who is circumcised and has faith in God , as Abraham did before he was circumcised .
45004013	God promised Abraham and his descendants that he would give them the world . This promise wasn't made because Abraham had obeyed a law , but because his faith in God made him acceptable .
45004014	If Abraham and his descendants were given this promise because they had obeyed a law , then faith would mean nothing , and the promise would be worthless .
45004015	God becomes angry when his Law is broken . But where there isn't a law , it cannot be broken .
45004016	Everything depends on having faith in God , so that God's promise is assured by his gift of undeserved grace . This promise isn't only for Abraham's descendants who have the Law . It is for all who are Abraham's descendants because they have faith , just as he did . Abraham is the ancestor of us all .
45004017	The Scriptures say that Abraham would become the ancestor of many nations . This promise was made to Abraham because he had faith in God , who raises the dead to life and creates new things .
45004018	God promised Abraham a lot of descendants . And when it all seemed hopeless , Abraham still had faith in God and became the ancestor of many nations .
45004019	Abraham's faith never became weak , not even when he was nearly 100 years old . He knew he was almost dead and that his wife Sarah could not have children .
45004020	But Abraham never doubted or questioned God's promise . His faith made him strong , and he gave all the credit to God .
45004021	Abraham was certain that God could do what he had promised .
45004022	So God accepted him ,
45004023	just as we read in the Scriptures . But these words were not written only for Abraham .
45004024	They were written for us , since we will also be accepted because of our faith in God , who raised our Lord Jesus to life .
45004025	God gave Jesus to die for our sins , and he raised him to life , so that we would be made acceptable to God .
45005001	By faith we have been made acceptable to God . And now , thanks to our Lord Jesus Christ , we have peace with God .
45005002	Christ has also introduced us to God's gift of undeserved grace on which we now take our stand . So we are happy , as we look forward to sharing in the glory of God .
45005003	But that's not all ! We gladly suffer , because we know that suffering helps us to endure .
45005004	And endurance builds character , which gives us a hope
45005005	that will never disappoint us . All of this happens because God has given us the Holy Spirit , who fills our hearts with his love .
45005006	Christ died for us at a time when we were helpless and sinful .
45005007	No one is really willing to die for an honest person , though someone might be willing to die for a truly good person .
45005008	But God showed how much he loved us by having Christ die for us , even though we were sinful .
45005009	But there is more ! Now that God has accepted us because Christ sacrificed his life's blood , we will also be kept safe from God's anger .
45005010	Even when we were God's enemies , he made peace with us , because his Son died for us . Yet something even greater than friendship is ours . Now that we are at peace with God , we will be saved by the life of his Son .
45005011	And in addition to everything else , we are happy because God sent our Lord Jesus Christ to make peace with us .
45005012	Adam sinned , and that sin brought death into the world . Now everyone has sinned , and so everyone must die .
45005013	Sin was in the world before the Law came . But no record of sin was kept , because there was no Law .
45005014	Yet death still had power over all who lived from the time of Adam to the time of Moses . This happened , though not everyone disobeyed a direct command from God , as Adam did . In some ways Adam is like Christ who came later .
45005015	But the gift of God's undeserved grace was very different from Adam's sin . That one sin brought death to many others . Yet in an even greater way , Jesus Christ alone brought God's gift of undeserved grace to many people .
45005016	There is a lot of difference between Adam's sin and God's gift . That one sin led to punishment . But God's gift made it possible for us to be acceptable to him , even though we have sinned many times .
45005017	Death ruled like a king because Adam had sinned . But that cannot compare with what Jesus Christ has done . God has treated us with undeserved grace , and he has accepted us because of Jesus . And so we will live and rule like kings .
45005018	Everyone was going to be punished because Adam sinned . But because of the good thing that Christ has done , God accepts us and gives us the gift of life .
45005019	Adam disobeyed God and caused many others to be sinners . But Jesus obeyed him and will make many people acceptable to God .
45005020	The Law came , so that the full power of sin could be seen . Yet where sin was powerful , God's gift of undeserved grace was even more powerful .
45005021	Sin ruled by means of death . But God's gift of grace now rules , and God has accepted us because of Jesus Christ our Lord . This means that we will have eternal life .
45006001	What should we say ? Should we keep on sinning , so that God's gift of undeserved grace will show up even better ?
45006002	No , we should not ! If we are dead to sin , how can we go on sinning ?
45006003	Don't you know that all who share in Christ Jesus by being baptized also share in his death ?
45006004	When we were baptized , we died and were buried with Christ . We were baptized , so we would live a new life , as Christ was raised to life by the glory of God the Father .
45006005	If we shared in Jesus' death by being baptized , we will be raised to life with him .
45006006	We know that the persons we used to be were nailed to the cross with Jesus . This was done , so our sinful bodies would no longer be the slaves of sin .
45006007	We know sin doesn't have power over dead people .
45006008	As surely as we died with Christ , we believe we will also live with him .
45006009	We know that death no longer has any power over Christ . He died and was raised to life , never again to die .
45006010	When Christ died , he died for sin once and for all . But now he is alive , and he lives only for God .
45006011	In the same way , you must think of yourselves as dead to the power of sin . But Christ Jesus has given life to you , and you live for God .
45006012	Don't let sin rule your body . After all , your body is bound to die , so don't obey its desires
45006013	or let any part of it become a slave of evil . Give yourselves to God , as people who have been raised from death to life . Make every part of your body a slave that pleases God .
45006014	Don't let sin keep ruling your lives . You are ruled by God's undeserved grace and not by the Law .
45006015	What does all this mean ? Does it mean we are free to sin , because we are ruled by God's gift of undeserved grace and not by the Law ? Certainly not !
45006016	Don't you know that you are slaves of anyone you obey ? You can be slaves of sin and die , or you can be obedient slaves of God and be acceptable to him .
45006017	You used to be slaves of sin . But I thank God that with all your heart you followed the example set forth in the teaching you received .
45006018	Now you are set free from sin and are slaves who please God .
45006019	I am using these everyday examples , because in some ways you are still weak . You used to let the different parts of your body be slaves of your evil thoughts . But now you must make every part of your body serve God , so that you will belong completely to him .
45006020	When you were slaves of sin , you didn't have to please God .
45006021	But what good did you receive from the things you did ? All you have to show for them is your shame , and they lead to death .
45006022	Now you have been set free from sin , and you are God's slaves . This will make you holy and will lead you to eternal life .
45006023	Sin pays off with death . But God's gift is eternal life given by Jesus Christ our Lord .
45007001	My friends , you surely understand enough about law to know that laws only have power over people who are alive .
45007002	For example , the Law says that a man's wife must remain his wife as long as he lives . But once her husband is dead , she is free
45007003	to marry someone else . However , if she goes off with another man while her husband is still alive , she is said to be unfaithful .
45007004	That is how it is with you , my friends . You are now part of the body of Christ and are dead to the power of the Law . You are free to belong to Christ , who was raised to life so we could serve God .
45007005	When we thought only of ourselves , the Law made us have sinful desires . It made every part of our bodies into slaves who are doomed to die .
45007006	But the Law no longer rules over us . We are like dead people , and it cannot have any power over us . Now we can serve God in a new way by obeying his Spirit , and not in the old way by obeying the written Law .
45007007	Does this mean that the Law is sinful ? Certainly not ! But if it had not been for the Law , I would not have known what sin is really like . For example , I would not have known what it means to want something that belongs to someone else , unless the Law had told me not to do this .
45007008	It was sin that used this command as a way of making me have all kinds of desires . But without the Law , sin is dead .
45007009	Before I knew about the Law , I was alive . But as soon as I heard that command , sin came to life ,
45007010	and I died . The very command that was supposed to bring life to me , instead brought death .
45007011	Sin used this command to trick me , and because of it I died .
45007012	Still , the Law and its commands are holy and correct and good .
45007013	Am I saying something good caused my death ? Certainly not ! It was sin that killed me by using something good . Now we can see how terrible and evil sin really is .
45007014	We know that the Law is spiritual . But I am merely a human , and I have been sold as a slave to sin .
45007015	In fact , I don't understand why I act the way I do . I don't do what I know is right . I do the things I hate .
45007016	Although I don't do what I know is right , I agree that the Law is good .
45007017	So I am not the one doing these evil things . The sin that lives in me is what does them .
45007018	I know that my selfish desires won't let me do anything that is good . Even when I want to do right , I cannot .
45007019	Instead of doing what I know is right , I do wrong .
45007020	And so , if I don't do what I know is right , I am no longer the one doing these evil things . The sin that lives in me is what does them .
45007021	The Law has shown me that something in me keeps me from doing what I know is right .
45007022	With my whole heart I agree with the Law of God .
45007023	But in every part of me I discover something fighting against my mind , and it makes me a prisoner of sin that controls everything I do .
45007024	What a miserable person I am . Who will rescue me from this body that is doomed to die ?
45007025	Thank God ! Jesus Christ will rescue me . So with my mind I serve the Law of God , although my selfish desires make me serve the law of sin .
45008001	If you belong to Christ Jesus , you won't be punished .
45008002	The Holy Spirit will give you life that comes from Christ Jesus and will set you free from sin and death .
45008003	The Law of Moses cannot do this , because our selfish desires make the Law weak . But God set you free when he sent his own Son to be like us sinners and to be a sacrifice for our sin . God used Christ's body to condemn sin .
45008004	He did this , so that we would do what the Law commands by obeying the Spirit instead of our own desires .
45008005	People who are ruled by their desires think only of themselves . Everyone who is ruled by the Holy Spirit thinks about spiritual things .
45008006	If our minds are ruled by our desires , we will die . But if our minds are ruled by the Spirit , we will have life and peace .
45008007	Our desires fight against God , because they do not and cannot obey God's laws .
45008008	If we follow our desires , we cannot please God .
45008009	You are no longer ruled by your desires , but by God's Spirit , who lives in you . People who don't have the Spirit of Christ in them don't belong to him .
45008010	But Christ lives in you . So you are alive because God has accepted you , even though your bodies must die because of your sins .
45008011	Yet God raised Jesus to life ! God's Spirit now lives in you , and he will raise you to life by his Spirit .
45008012	My dear friends , we must not live to satisfy our desires .
45008013	If you do , you will die . But you will live , if by the help of God's Spirit you say “ No ” to your desires .
45008014	Only those people who are led by God's Spirit are his children .
45008015	God's Spirit doesn't make us slaves who are afraid of him . Instead , we become his children and call him our Father .
45008016	God's Spirit makes us sure that we are his children .
45008017	His Spirit lets us know that together with Christ we will be given what God has promised . We will also share in the glory of Christ , because we have suffered with him .
45008018	I am sure what we are suffering now cannot compare with the glory that will be shown to us .
45008019	In fact , all creation is eagerly waiting for God to show who his children are .
45008020	Meanwhile , creation is confused , but not because it wants to be confused . God made it this way in the hope
45008021	that creation would be set free from decay and would share in the glorious freedom of his children .
45008022	We know that all creation is still groaning and is in pain , like a woman about to give birth .
45008023	The Spirit makes us sure about what we will be in the future . But now we groan silently , while we wait for God to show that we are his children . This means that our bodies will also be set free .
45008024	And this hope is what saves us . But if we already have what we hope for , there is no need to keep on hoping .
45008025	However , we hope for something we have not yet seen , and we patiently wait for it .
45008026	In certain ways we are weak , but the Spirit is here to help us . For example , when we don't know what to pray for , the Spirit prays for us in ways that cannot be put into words .
45008027	All of our thoughts are known to God . He can understand what is in the mind of the Spirit , as the Spirit prays for God's people .
45008028	We know that God is always at work for the good of everyone who loves him . They are the ones God has chosen for his purpose ,
45008029	and he has always known who his chosen ones would be . He had decided to let them become like his own Son , so his Son would be the first of many children .
45008030	God then accepted the people he had already decided to choose , and he has shared his glory with them .
45008031	What can we say about all this ? If God is on our side , can anyone be against us ?
45008032	God did not keep back his own Son , but he gave him for us . If God did this , won't he freely give us everything else ?
45008033	If God says his chosen ones are acceptable to him , can anyone bring charges against them ?
45008034	Or can anyone condemn them ? No indeed ! Christ died and was raised to life , and now he is at God's right side , speaking to him for us .
45008035	Can anything separate us from the love of Christ ? Can trouble , suffering , and hard times , or hunger and nakedness , or danger and death ?
45008036	It is exactly as the Scriptures say , “ For you we face death all day long . We are like sheep on their way to be butchered . ”
45009001	I am a follower of Christ , and the Holy Spirit is a witness to my conscience . So I tell the truth and I am not lying when I say
45009002	my heart is broken and I am in great sorrow .
45009003	I would gladly be placed under God's curse and be separated from Christ for the good of my own people .
45009004	They are the descendants of Israel , and they are also God's chosen people . God showed them his glory . He made agreements with them and gave them his Law . The temple is theirs and so are the promises that God made to them .
45009005	They have those famous ancestors , who were also the ancestors of the Christ . I pray that God , who rules over all , will be praised forever ! Amen .
45009006	It cannot be said that God broke his promise . After all , not all of the people of Israel are the true people of God .
45009009	Sarah , “ At this time next year I will return , and you will already have a son . ”
45009010	Don't forget what happened to the twin sons of Isaac and Rebekah .
45009013	That's why the Scriptures say that the Lord liked Jacob more than Esau .
45009014	Are we saying God is unfair ? Certainly not !
45009015	The Lord told Moses that he has pity and mercy on anyone he wants to .
45009016	Everything then depends on God's mercy and not on what people want or do .
45009017	In the Scriptures the Lord says to the king of Egypt , “ I let you become king , so that I could show you my power and be praised by all people on earth . ”
45009018	Everything depends on what God decides to do , and he can either have pity on people or make them stubborn .
45009019	Someone may ask , “ How can God blame us , if he makes us behave in the way he wants us to ? ”
45009020	But , my friend , I ask , “ Who do you think you are to question God ? Does the clay have the right to ask the potter why he shaped it the way he did ?
45009021	Doesn't a potter have the right to make a fancy bowl and a plain bowl out of the same lump of clay ? ”
45009022	God wanted to show his anger and reveal his power against everyone who deserved to be destroyed . But instead , he patiently put up with them .
45009023	He did this by showing how glorious he is when he has pity on the people he has chosen to share in his glory .
45009024	Whether Jews or Gentiles , we are those chosen ones ,
45009025	just as the Lord says in the book of Hosea , “ Although they are not my people , I will make them my people . I will treat with love those nations that have never been loved .
45009026	“ Once they were told , ‘ You are not my people . ’ But in that very place they will be called children of the living God . ”
45009027	And this is what the prophet Isaiah said about the people of Israel , “ The people of Israel are as many as the grains of sand along the beach . But only a few who are left will be saved .
45009028	The Lord will be quick and sure to do on earth what he has warned he will do . ”
45009029	Isaiah also said , “ If the Lord All-Powerful had not spared some of our descendants , we would have been destroyed like the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah . ”
45009030	What does all of this mean ? It means that the Gentiles were not trying to be acceptable to God , but they found that he would accept them if they had faith .
45009033	just as God says in the Scriptures , “ Look ! I am placing in Zion a stone to make people stumble and fall . But those who have faith in that one will never be disappointed . ”
45010001	Dear friends , my greatest wish and my prayer to God is for the people of Israel to be saved .
45010002	I know they love God , but they don't understand
45010003	what makes people acceptable to him . So they refuse to trust God , and they try to be acceptable by obeying the Law .
45010004	But Christ makes the Law no longer necessary for those who become acceptable to God by faith .
45010005	Moses said a person could become acceptable to God by obeying the Law . He did this when he wrote , “ If you want to live , you must do all the Law commands . ”
45010006	But people whose faith makes them acceptable to God will never ask , “ Who will go up to heaven to bring Christ down ? ”
45010007	Neither will they ask , “ Who will go down into the world of the dead to raise him to life ? ”
45010008	All who are acceptable because of their faith simply say , “ The message is as near as your mouth or your heart . ” And this is the same message we preach about faith .
45010009	So you will be saved , if you honestly say , “ Jesus is Lord , ” and if you believe with all your heart that God raised him from death .
45010010	God will accept you and save you , if you truly believe this and tell it to others .
45010011	The Scriptures say no one who has faith will be disappointed ,
45010012	no matter if that person is a Jew or a Gentile . There is only one Lord , and he is generous to everyone who asks for his help .
45010013	All who call out to the Lord will be saved .
45010014	How can people have faith in the Lord and ask him to save them , if they have never heard about him ? And how can they hear , unless someone tells them ?
45010015	And how can anyone tell them without being sent by the Lord ? The Scriptures say it is a beautiful sight to see even the feet of someone coming to preach the good news .
45010016	Yet not everyone has believed the message . For example , the prophet Isaiah asked , “ Lord , has anyone believed what we said ? ”
45010017	No one can have faith without hearing the message about Christ .
45010018	But am I saying that the people of Israel did not hear ? No , I am not ! The Scriptures say , “ The message was told everywhere on earth . It was announced all over the world . ” “ I will make Israel jealous of people who are a nation of nobodies . I will make them angry with people who don't understand a thing . ” “ I was found by people who were not looking for me . I appeared to the ones who were not asking about me . ” “ All day long the Lord has reached out to people who are stubborn and refuse to obey . ”
45011001	Am I saying that God has turned his back on his people ? Certainly not ! I am one of the people of Israel , and I myself am a descendant of Abraham from the tribe of Benjamin .
45011002	God did not turn his back on his chosen people . Don't you remember reading in the Scriptures how Elijah complained to God about the people of Israel ?
45011003	He said , “ Lord , they killed your prophets and destroyed your altars . I am the only one left , and now they want to kill me . ”
45011004	But the Lord told Elijah , “ I still have 7,000 followers who have not worshiped Baal . ”
45011005	It is the same way now . God treated the people of Israel with undeserved grace , and so a few of them are still his followers .
45011006	This happened because of God's undeserved kindness and not because of anything they have done . It could not have happened except for God's gift of undeserved grace .
45011007	This means that only a chosen few of the people of Israel found what all of them were searching for . And the rest of them were stubborn ,
45011008	just as the Scriptures say , “ God made them so stupid that their eyes are blind , and their ears are still deaf . ”
45011009	Then David said , “ Turn their meals into bait for a trap , so that they will stumble and be given what they deserve .
45011010	Blindfold their eyes ! Don't let them see . Bend their backs beneath a burden that will never be lifted . ”
45011011	Do I mean that the people of Israel fell , never to get up again ? Certainly not ! Their failure made it possible for the Gentiles to be saved , and this will make the people of Israel jealous .
45011012	But if the rest of the world's people were helped so much by their sin and loss , they will be helped even more by their full return .
45011013	I am now speaking to you Gentiles , and as long as I am an apostle to you , I will take pride in my work .
45011014	I hope in this way to make some of my own people jealous enough to be saved .
45011015	When Israel rejected God , the rest of the people in the world were able to turn to him . So when God makes friends with Israel , it will be like bringing the dead back to life .
45011016	If part of a batch of dough is made holy by being offered to God , then all of the dough is holy . If the roots of a tree are holy , the rest of the tree is holy too .
45011017	You Gentiles are like branches of a wild olive tree made to be part of a cultivated olive tree . You have taken the place of some branches that were cut away from it . And because of this , you enjoy the blessings that come from being part of that cultivated tree .
45011018	But don't think you are better than the branches that were cut away . Just remember you are not supporting the roots of this tree . Its roots are supporting you .
45011019	Maybe you think those branches were cut away , so you could be put in their place .
45011020	That's true enough . But they were cut away because they did not have faith , and you are where you are because you do have faith . So don't be proud , but be afraid .
45011021	If God cut away those natural branches , couldn't he do the same to you ?
45011022	Now you see both how kind and how hard God can be . He was hard on those who fell , but he was kind to you . And he will keep on being kind to you , if you keep on trusting in his kindness . Otherwise , you will be cut away too .
45011023	If those other branches will start having faith , they will be made a part of that tree again . God has the power to put them back .
45011024	After all , it wasn't natural for branches to be cut from a wild olive tree and to be made part of a cultivated olive tree . So it is much more likely that God will join the natural branches back to the cultivated olive tree .
45011025	My friends , I don't want you Gentiles to be too proud of yourselves . So I will explain the mystery of what has happened to the people of Israel . Some of them have become stubborn , and they will stay like that until the complete number of you Gentiles has come in .
45011026	In this way all of Israel will be saved , as the Scriptures say , “ From Zion someone will come to rescue us . Then Jacob's descendants will stop being evil .
45011027	This is what the Lord has promised to do when he forgives their sins . ”
45011028	The people of Israel are treated as God's enemies , so the good news can come to you Gentiles . But they are still the chosen ones , and God loves them because of their famous ancestors .
45011029	God doesn't take back the gifts he has given or disown the people he has chosen .
45011030	At one time you Gentiles rejected God . But now Israel has rejected God , and you have been shown mercy .
45011031	And because of the mercy shown to you , they will also be shown mercy .
45011032	All people have disobeyed God , and that's why he treats them as prisoners . But he does this , so that he can have mercy on all of them .
45011033	Who can measure the wealth and wisdom and knowledge of God ? Who can understand his decisions or explain what he does ?
45011034	“ Has anyone known the thoughts of the Lord or given him advice ?
45011035	Has anyone loaned something to the Lord that must be repaid ? ”
45012001	Dear friends , God is good . So I beg you to offer your bodies to him as a living sacrifice , pure and pleasing . That's the most sensible way to serve God .
45012002	Don't be like the people of this world , but let God change the way you think . Then you will know how to do everything that is good and pleasing to him .
45012003	I realize God has treated me with undeserved grace , and so I tell each of you not to think you are better than you really are . Use good sense and measure yourself by the amount of faith that God has given you .
45012004	A body is made up of many parts , and each of them has its own use .
45012005	That's how it is with us . There are many of us , but we each are part of the body of Christ , as well as part of one another .
45012006	God has also given each of us different gifts to use . If we can prophesy , we should do it according to the amount of faith we have .
45012007	If we can serve others , we should serve . If we can teach , we should teach .
45012008	If we can encourage others , we should encourage them . If we can give , we should be generous . If we are leaders , we should do our best . If we are good to others , we should do it cheerfully .
45012009	Be sincere in your love for others . Hate everything that is evil and hold tight to everything that is good .
45012010	Love each other as brothers and sisters and honor others more than you do yourself .
45012011	Never give up . Eagerly follow the Holy Spirit and serve the Lord .
45012012	Let your hope make you glad . Be patient in time of trouble and never stop praying .
45012013	Take care of God's needy people and welcome strangers into your home .
45012014	Ask God to bless everyone who mistreats you . Ask him to bless them and not to curse them .
45012015	When others are happy , be happy with them , and when they are sad , be sad .
45012016	Be friendly with everyone . Don't be proud and feel that you know more than others . Make friends with ordinary people .
45012017	Don't mistreat someone who has mistreated you . But try to earn the respect of others ,
45012018	and do your best to live at peace with everyone .
45012019	Dear friends , don't try to get even . Let God take revenge . In the Scriptures the Lord says , “ I am the one to take revenge and pay them back . ” “ If your enemies are hungry , give them something to eat . And if they are thirsty , give them something to drink . This will be the same as piling burning coals on their heads . ”
45013001	Obey the rulers who have authority over you . Only God can give authority to anyone , and he puts these rulers in their places of power .
45013002	People who oppose the authorities are opposing what God has done , and they will be punished .
45013003	Rulers are a threat to evil people , not to good people . There is no need to be afraid of the authorities . Just do right , and they will praise you for it .
45013004	After all , they are God's servants , and it is their duty to help you . If you do something wrong , you ought to be afraid , because these rulers have the right to punish you . They are God's servants who punish criminals to show how angry God is .
45013005	But you should obey the rulers because you know it is the right thing to do , and not just because of God's anger .
45013006	You must also pay your taxes . The authorities are God's servants , and it is their duty to take care of these matters .
45013007	Pay all that you owe , whether it is taxes and fees or respect and honor .
45013008	Let love be your only debt ! If you love others , you have done all that the Law demands .
45013009	In the Law there are many commands , such as , “ Be faithful in marriage . Do not murder . Do not steal . Do not want what belongs to others . ” But all of these are summed up in the command that says , “ Love others as much as you love yourself . ”
45013010	No one who loves others will harm them . So love is all that the Law demands .
45013011	You know what sort of times we live in , and so you should live properly . It is time to wake up . You know that the day when we will be saved is nearer now than when we first put our faith in the Lord .
45013012	Night is almost over , and day will soon appear . We must stop behaving as people do in the dark and be ready to live in the light .
45013013	So behave properly , as people do in the day . Don't go to wild parties or get drunk or be vulgar or indecent . Don't quarrel or be jealous .
45013014	Let the Lord Jesus Christ be as near to you as the clothes you wear . Then you won't try to satisfy your selfish desires .
45014001	Welcome all the Lord's followers , even those whose faith is weak . Don't criticize them for having beliefs that are different from yours .
45014002	Some think it is all right to eat anything , while those whose faith is weak will eat only vegetables .
45014003	But you should not criticize others for eating or for not eating . After all , God welcomes everyone .
45014004	What right do you have to criticize someone else's servants ? Only their Lord can decide if they are doing right , and the Lord will make sure that they do right .
45014005	Some of the Lord's followers think one day is more important than another . Others think all days are the same . But each of you should make up your own mind .
45014006	Any followers who count one day more important than another day do it to honor their Lord . And any followers who eat meat give thanks to God , just like the ones who don't eat meat .
45014007	Whether we live or die , it must be for God , rather than for ourselves .
45014008	Whether we live or die , it must be for the Lord . Alive or dead , we still belong to the Lord .
45014009	This is because Christ died and rose to life , so that he would be the Lord of the dead and of the living .
45014010	Why do you criticize other followers of the Lord ? Why do you look down on them ? The day is coming when God will judge all of us .
45014011	In the Scriptures God says , “ I swear by my very life that everyone will kneel down and praise my name ! ”
45014013	We must stop judging others . We must also make up our minds not to upset anyone's faith .
45014014	The Lord Jesus has made it clear to me that God considers all foods fit to eat . But if you think some foods are unfit to eat , then for you they are not fit .
45014015	If you are hurting others by the foods you eat , you are not guided by love . Don't let your appetite destroy someone Christ died for .
45014016	Don't let your right to eat bring shame to Christ .
45014017	God's kingdom isn't about eating and drinking . It is about pleasing God , about living in peace , and about true happiness . All this comes from the Holy Spirit .
45014018	If you serve Christ in this way , you will please God and be respected by people .
45014019	We should try to live at peace and help each other have a strong faith .
45014020	Don't let your appetite destroy what God has done . All foods are fit to eat , but it is wrong to cause problems for others by what you eat .
45014021	It is best not to eat meat or drink wine or do anything else that causes problems for other followers of the Lord .
45014022	What you believe about these things should be kept between you and God . You are fortunate , if your actions don't make you have doubts .
45014023	But if you do have doubts about what you eat , you are going against your beliefs . And you know that is wrong , because anything you do against your beliefs is sin .
45015001	If our faith is strong , we should be patient with the Lord's followers whose faith is weak . We should try to please them instead of ourselves .
45015002	We should think of their good and try to help them by doing what pleases them .
45015003	Even Christ did not try to please himself . But as the Scriptures say , “ The people who insulted you also insulted me . ”
45015004	And the Scriptures were written to teach and encourage us by giving us hope .
45015005	God is the one who makes us patient and cheerful . I pray that he will help you live at peace with each other , as you follow Christ .
45015006	Then all of you together will praise God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ .
45015007	Honor God by accepting each other , as Christ has accepted you .
45015008	I tell you that Christ came as a servant of the Jews to show that God has kept the promises he made to their famous ancestors . Christ also came ,
45015009	so that the Gentiles would praise God for being kind to them . It is just as the Scriptures say , “ I will tell the nations about you , and I will sing praises to your name . ”
45015010	The Scriptures also say to the Gentiles , “ Come and celebrate with God's people . ”
45015011	Again the Scriptures say , “ Praise the Lord , all you Gentiles . All you nations , come and worship him . ”
45015012	Isaiah says , “ Someone from David's family will come to power . He will rule the nations , and they will put their hope in him . ”
45015013	I pray that God , who gives hope , will bless you with complete happiness and peace because of your faith . And may the power of the Holy Spirit fill you with hope .
45015014	My friends , I am sure that you are very good and that you have all the knowledge you need to teach each other .
45015015	But I have spoken to you plainly and have tried to remind you of some things . God treated me with undeserved grace !
45015016	He chose me to be a servant of Christ Jesus for the Gentiles and to do the work of a priest in the service of his good news . God did this so that the Holy Spirit could make the Gentiles into a holy offering , pleasing to him .
45015017	Because of Christ Jesus , I can take pride in my service for God .
45015018	In fact , all I will talk about is how Christ let me speak and work , so that the Gentiles would obey him .
45015019	Indeed , I will tell how Christ worked miracles and wonders by the power of the Holy Spirit . I have preached the good news about him all the way from Jerusalem to Illyricum .
