45015020	But I have always tried to preach where people have never heard about Christ . I am like a builder who doesn't build on someone else's foundation .
45015021	It is just as the Scriptures say , “ All who haven't been told about him will see him , and those who haven't heard about him will understand . ”
45015022	My work has always kept me from coming to see you .
45015023	Now there is nothing left for me to do in this part of the world , and for years I have wanted to visit you .
45015024	So I plan to stop off on my way to Spain . Then after a short , but refreshing , visit with you , I hope you will quickly send me on .
45015027	This is something they really wanted to do . But sharing their money with the Jews was also like paying back a debt , because the Jews had already shared their spiritual blessings with the Gentiles .
45015028	After I have safely delivered this money , I will visit you and then go on to Spain .
45015029	And when I do arrive in Rome , I know it will be with the full blessings of Christ .
45015030	My friends , by the power of the Lord Jesus Christ and by the love that comes from the Holy Spirit , I beg you to pray sincerely with me and for me .
45015031	Pray that God will protect me from the unbelievers in Judea , and that his people in Jerusalem will be pleased with what I am doing .
45015032	Ask God to let me come to you and have a pleasant and refreshing visit .
45015033	I pray that God , who gives peace , will be with all of you . Amen .
45016001	I have good things to say about Phoebe , who is a leader in the church at Cenchreae .
45016002	Welcome her in a way that is proper for someone who has faith in the Lord and is one of God's own people . Help her in any way you can . After all , she has proved to be a respected leader for many others , including me .
45016003	Give my greetings to Priscilla and Aquila . They have not only served Christ Jesus together with me ,
45016004	but they have even risked their lives for me . I am grateful for them and so are all the Gentile churches .
45016005	Greet the church that meets in their home . Greet my dear friend Epaenetus , who was the first person in Asia to have faith in Christ .
45016006	Greet Mary , who has worked so hard for you .
45016007	Greet my relatives Andronicus and Junia , who were in jail with me . They are highly respected by the apostles and were followers of Christ before I was .
45016008	Greet Ampliatus , my dear friend whose faith is in the Lord .
45016009	Greet Urbanus , who serves Christ along with us . Greet my dear friend Stachys .
45016010	Greet Apelles , a faithful servant of Christ . Greet Aristobulus and his family .
45016011	Greet Herodion , who is a relative of mine . Greet Narcissus and the others in his family , who have faith in the Lord .
45016012	Greet Tryphaena and Tryphosa , who work hard for the Lord . Greet my dear friend Persis . She also works hard for the Lord .
45016013	Greet Rufus , that special servant of the Lord , and greet his mother , who has been like a mother to me .
45016014	Greet Asyncritus , Phlegon , Hermes , Patrobas , and Hermas , as well as our friends who are with them .
45016015	Greet Philologus , Julia , Nereus and his sister , and Olympas , and all of God's people who are with them .
45016016	Be sure to give each other a warm greeting . All of Christ's churches greet you .
45016017	My friends , I beg you to watch out for anyone who causes trouble and divides the church by refusing to do what all of you were taught . Stay away from them !
45016018	They want to serve themselves and not Christ the Lord . Their flattery and fancy talk fool people who don't know any better .
45016019	I am glad that everyone knows how well you obey the Lord . But still , I want you to understand what is good and not have anything to do with evil .
45016020	Then God , who gives peace , will soon crush Satan under your feet . I pray that our Lord Jesus will be kind to you .
45016021	Timothy , who works with me , sends his greetings , and so do my relatives , Lucius , Jason , and Sosipater .
45016022	I , Tertius , also send my greetings . I am a follower of the Lord , and I wrote this letter .
45016025	Praise God ! He can make you strong by means of my good news , which is the message about Jesus Christ . For ages and ages this message was kept secret ,
45016026	but now at last it has been told . The eternal God commanded his prophets to write about the good news , so that all nations would obey and have faith .
45016027	And now , because of Jesus Christ , we can praise the only wise God forever ! Amen .
46001001	From Paul , chosen by God to be an apostle of Christ Jesus , and from Sosthenes , who is also a follower .
46001002	To God's church in Corinth . Christ Jesus chose you to be his very own people , and you worship in his name , as we and all others do who call him Lord .
46001003	My prayer is that God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
46001004	I never stop thanking my God for treating you with undeserved grace by giving you Christ Jesus ,
46001005	who helps you speak and understand so well .
46001006	Now you are certain that everything we told you about our Lord Christ Jesus is true .
46001007	You are not missing out on any blessings , as you wait for him to return .
46001008	And until the day Christ does return , he will keep you completely innocent .
46001009	God can be trusted , and he chose you to be partners with his Son , our Lord Jesus Christ .
46001010	My dear friends , as a follower of our Lord Jesus Christ , I beg you to get along with each other . Don't take sides . Always try to agree in what you think .
46001011	Several people from Chloe's family have already reported to me that you keep arguing with each other .
46001012	They have said that some of you claim to follow me , while others claim to follow Apollos or Peter or Christ .
46001013	Has Christ been divided up ? Was I nailed to a cross for you ? Were you baptized in my name ?
46001014	I thank God that I didn't baptize any of you except Crispus and Gaius .
46001015	Not one of you can say that you were baptized in my name .
46001016	I did baptize the family of Stephanas , but I don't remember if I baptized anyone else .
46001017	Christ did not send me to baptize . He sent me to tell the good news without using words that sound wise and would make the cross of Christ lose its power .
46001018	The message about the cross doesn't make any sense to lost people . But for those of us who are being saved , it is God's power at work .
46001019	As God says in the Scriptures , “ I will destroy the wisdom of all who claim to be wise . I will confuse those who think they know so much . ”
46001020	What happened to those wise people ? What happened to those experts in the Scriptures ? What happened to the ones who think they have all the answers ? Didn't God show that the wisdom of this world is foolish ?
46001021	God was wise and decided not to let the people of this world use their wisdom to learn about him . Instead , God chose to save only those who believe the foolish message we preach .
46001022	Jews ask for miracles , and Greeks want something that sounds wise .
46001023	But we preach that Christ was nailed to a cross . Most Jews have problems with this , and most Gentiles think it is foolish .
46001024	Our message is God's power and wisdom for the Jews and the Greeks that he has chosen .
46001025	Even when God is foolish , he is wiser than everyone else , and even when God is weak , he is stronger than everyone else .
46001026	My dear friends , remember what you were when God chose you . The people of this world didn't think that many of you were wise . Only a few of you were in places of power , and not many of you came from important families .
46001027	But God chose the foolish things of this world to put the wise to shame . He chose the weak things of this world to put the powerful to shame .
46001028	What the world thinks is worthless , useless , and nothing at all is what God has used to destroy what the world considers important .
46001029	God did all this to keep anyone from bragging to him .
46001030	You are God's children . He sent Christ Jesus to save us and to make us wise , acceptable , and holy .
46001031	So if you want to brag , do what the Scriptures say and brag about the Lord .
46002001	Friends , when I came and told you the mystery that God had shared with us , I didn't use big words or try to sound wise .
46002002	In fact , while I was with you , I made up my mind to speak only about Jesus Christ , who had been nailed to a cross .
46002003	At first , I was weak and trembling with fear .
46002004	When I talked with you or preached , I didn't try to prove anything by sounding wise . I simply let God's Spirit show his power .
46002005	That way you would have faith because of God's power and not because of human wisdom .
46002006	We do use wisdom when speaking to people who are mature in their faith . But it isn't the wisdom of this world or of its rulers , who will soon disappear .
46002007	We speak of God's hidden and mysterious wisdom that God decided to use for our glory long before the world began .
46002008	The rulers of this world didn't know anything about this wisdom . If they had known about it , they would not have nailed the glorious Lord to a cross .
46002009	But it is just as the Scriptures say , “ What God has planned for people who love him is more than eyes have seen or ears have heard . It has never even entered our minds ! ”
46002010	God's Spirit has shown you everything . His Spirit finds out everything , even what is deep in the mind of God .
46002011	You are the only one who knows what is in your own mind , and God's Spirit is the only one who knows what is in God's mind .
46002012	But God has given us his Spirit . This is why we don't think the same way that the people of this world think . This is also why we can recognize the blessings God has given us .
46002013	Every word we speak was taught to us by God's Spirit , not by human wisdom . And this same Spirit helps us teach spiritual things to spiritual people .
46002014	This is why only someone who has God's Spirit can understand spiritual blessings . Anyone who doesn't have God's Spirit thinks these blessings are foolish .
46002015	People who are guided by the Spirit can make all kinds of judgments , but they cannot be judged by others .
46002016	The Scriptures ask , “ Has anyone ever known the thoughts of the Lord or given him advice ? ”
46003001	My friends , you are acting like the people of this world . That's why I could not speak to you as spiritual people . You are like babies as far as your faith in Christ is concerned .
46003002	So I had to treat you like babies and feed you milk . You could not take solid food , and you still cannot ,
46003003	because you are not yet spiritual . You are jealous and argue with each other . This proves you are not spiritual and you are acting like the people of this world .
46003004	Some of you say you follow me , and others claim to follow Apollos . Isn't this how ordinary people behave ?
46003005	Apollos and I are merely servants who helped you to have faith . It was the Lord who made it all happen .
46003006	I planted the seeds , Apollos watered them , but God made them sprout and grow .
46003007	What matters isn't those who planted or watered , but God who made the plants grow .
46003008	The one who plants is just as important as the one who waters . And each one will be paid for what they do .
46003009	Apollos and I work together for God , and you are God's garden and God's building .
46003010	God treated me with undeserved grace and let me become an expert builder . I laid a foundation on which others have built . But we must each be careful how we build ,
46003011	because Christ is the only foundation .
46003014	We will be rewarded if our building is left standing .
46003015	But if it is destroyed by the fire , we will lose everything . Yet we ourselves will be saved , like someone escaping from flames .
46003016	All of you surely know you are God's temple and his Spirit lives in you .
46003017	Together you are God's holy temple , and God will destroy anyone who destroys his temple .
46003018	Don't fool yourselves ! If any of you think you are wise in the things of this world , you will have to become foolish before you can be truly wise .
46003019	This is because God considers the wisdom of this world to be foolish . It is just as the Scriptures say , “ God catches the wise when they try to outsmart him . ”
46003020	The Scriptures also say , “ The Lord knows that the plans made by wise people are useless . ”
46003023	and you belong to Christ , and Christ belongs to God .
46004001	Think of us as servants of Christ who have been given the work of explaining God's mysterious ways .
46004002	And since our first duty is to be faithful to the one we work for ,
46004003	it doesn't matter to me if I am judged by you or even by a court of law . In fact , I don't judge myself .
46004004	I don't know of anything against me , but this doesn't prove I am right . The Lord is my judge .
46004005	So don't judge anyone until the Lord returns . He will show what is hidden in the dark and what is in everyone's heart . Then God will be the one who praises each of us .
46004006	Friends , I have used Apollos and myself as examples to teach you the meaning of the saying , “ Follow the rules . ” I want you to stop saying one of us is better than the other .
46004007	What is so special about you ? What do you have that you were not given ? And if it was given to you , how can you brag ?
46004008	Are you already satisfied ? Are you now rich ? Have you become kings while we are still nobodies ? I wish you were kings . Then we could have a share in your kingdom .
46004009	It seems to me that God has put us apostles in the worst possible place . We are like prisoners on their way to death . Angels and the people of this world just laugh at us .
46004010	Because of Christ we are thought of as fools , but Christ has made you wise . We are weak and hated , but you are powerful and respected .
46004011	Even today we go hungry and thirsty and don't have anything to wear except rags . We are mistreated and don't have a place to live .
46004012	We work hard with our own hands , and when people abuse us , we wish them well . When we suffer , we are patient .
46004013	When someone curses us , we answer with kind words . Until now we are thought of as nothing more than the trash and garbage of this world .
46004014	I am not writing to embarrass you . I want to help you , just as parents help their own dear children .
46004015	Ten thousand people may teach you about Christ , but I am your only father . You became my children when I told you about Christ Jesus ,
46004016	and I want you to be like me .
46004017	This is why I sent Timothy to you . I love him like a son , and he is a faithful servant of the Lord . Timothy will tell you what I do to follow Christ and how it agrees with what I always teach about Christ in every church .
46004018	Some of you think I am not coming for a visit , and so you are bragging .
46004019	But if the Lord lets me come , I will soon be there . Then I will find out if the ones who are doing all this bragging really have any power .
46004020	God's kingdom isn't just a lot of words . It is power .
46004021	What do you want me to do when I arrive ? Do you want me to be hard on you or to be kind and gentle ?
46005001	I have heard terrible things about some of you . In fact , you are behaving worse than Gentiles . A man is even sleeping with his own stepmother .
46005002	You are proud , when you ought to feel bad enough to chase away anyone who acts like this .
46005005	You must then hand that man over to Satan . His body will be destroyed , but his spirit will be saved when the Lord Jesus returns .
46005006	Stop being proud ! Don't you know how a little yeast can spread through the whole batch of dough ?
46005007	Get rid of the old yeast ! Then you will be like fresh bread made without yeast , and this is what you are . Our Passover lamb is Christ , who has already been sacrificed .
46005008	So don't celebrate the festival by being evil and sinful , which is like serving bread made with yeast . Be pure and truthful and celebrate by using bread made without yeast .
46005009	In my other letter I told you not to have anything to do with immoral people .
46005010	But I wasn't talking about the people of this world . You would have to leave this world to get away from everyone who is immoral or greedy or who cheats or worships idols .
46005011	I was talking about your own people who are immoral or greedy or worship idols or curse others or get drunk or cheat . Don't even eat with them !
46005012	Why should I judge outsiders ? Aren't we supposed to judge only church members ?
46005013	God judges everyone else . The Scriptures say , “ Chase away any of your own people who are evil . ”
46006001	When one of you has a complaint against another , do you take your complaint to a court of sinners ? Or do you take it to God's people ?
46006002	Don't you know that God's people will judge the world ? And if you are going to judge the world , can't you settle small problems ?
46006003	Don't you know we will judge angels ? And if this is so , we can surely judge everyday matters .
46006004	Why do you take everyday complaints to judges who are not respected by the church ?
46006005	I say this to your shame . Aren't any of you wise enough to act as a judge between one follower and another ?
46006006	Why should one of you take another to be tried by unbelievers ?
46006007	When one of you takes another to court , all of you lose . It would be better to let yourselves be cheated and robbed .
46006008	But instead , you cheat and rob other followers .
46006009	Don't you know that evil people won't have a share in the blessings of God's kingdom ? Don't fool yourselves ! No one who is immoral or worships idols or is unfaithful in marriage or is a pervert or behaves like a homosexual
46006010	will share in God's kingdom . Neither will any thief or greedy person or drunkard or anyone who curses and cheats others .
46006011	Some of you used to be like that . But now the name of our Lord Jesus Christ and the power of God's Spirit have washed you and made you holy and acceptable to God .
46006012	Some of you say , “ We can do anything we want to . ” But I tell you not everything is good for us . So I refuse to let anything have power over me .
46006013	You also say , “ Food is meant for our bodies , and our bodies are meant for food . ” But I tell you that God will destroy them both . We are not supposed to do indecent things with our bodies . We are to use them for the Lord who is in charge of our bodies .
46006014	God will raise us from death by the same power he used when he raised our Lord to life .
46006015	Don't you know that your bodies are part of the body of Christ ? Is it right for me to join part of the body of Christ to a prostitute ? No , it isn't !
46006016	Don't you know that a man who does that becomes part of her body ? The Scriptures say , “ The two of them will be like one person . ”
46006017	But anyone who is joined to the Lord is one in spirit with him .
46006018	Don't be immoral in matters of sex . That is a sin against your own body in a way no other sin is .
46006019	You surely know that your body is a temple where the Holy Spirit lives . The Spirit is in you and is a gift from God . You are no longer your own .
46006020	God paid a great price for you . So use your body to honor God .
46007001	Now I will answer the questions you asked in your letter . You asked , “ Is it best for people not to marry ? ”
46007002	Well , having your own husband or wife should keep you from doing something immoral .
46007003	Husbands and wives should be fair with each other about having sex .
46007004	A wife belongs to her husband instead of to herself , and a husband belongs to his wife instead of to himself .
46007005	So don't refuse sex to each other , unless you agree not to have sex for a little while , in order to spend time in prayer . Then Satan won't be able to tempt you because of your lack of self-control .
46007006	In my opinion that is what should be done , though I don't know of anything the Lord said about this matter .
46007007	I wish all of you were like me , but God has given different gifts to each of us .
46007008	My advice for the unmarried and for widows is that it is acceptable for them to remain single , just as I am .
46007009	But if you don't have enough self-control , then go ahead and get married . After all , it is better to marry than to burn with desire .
46007010	I instruct married couples to stay together , and this is exactly what the Lord himself taught . A wife who leaves her husband
46007011	should either stay single or go back to her husband . And a husband should not leave his wife .
46007012	I don't know of anything else the Lord said about marriage . All I can do is to give you my own advice . If your wife isn't a follower of the Lord , but is willing to stay with you , don't divorce her .
46007013	If your husband isn't a follower , but is willing to stay with you , don't divorce him .
46007014	Your husband or wife who isn't a follower is made holy by having you as a partner . This also makes your children holy and keeps them from being unclean in God's sight .
46007015	If your husband or wife isn't a follower of the Lord and decides to divorce you , then you should agree to it . You are no longer bound to that person . After all , God chose you and wants you to live at peace .
46007016	And besides , how do you know if you will be able to save your husband or wife who isn't a follower ?
46007017	In every church I tell the people to stay as they were when the Lord Jesus chose them and God called them to be his own . Now I say the same thing to you .
46007018	If you are already circumcised , don't try to change it . If you are not circumcised , don't get circumcised .
46007019	Being circumcised or uncircumcised isn't really what matters . The important thing is to obey God's commands .
46007020	So don't try to change what you were when God chose you .
46007021	Are you a slave ? Don't let that bother you . But if you can win your freedom , you should .
46007022	When the Lord chooses slaves , they become his free people . And when he chooses free people , they become slaves of Christ .
46007023	God paid a great price for you . So don't become slaves of anyone else .
46007024	Stay what you were when God chose you .
46007025	I don't know of anything the Lord said about people who have never been married . But I will tell you what I think . And you can trust me , because the Lord has treated me with kindness .
46007026	We are now going through hard times , and I think it is best for you to stay as you are .
46007027	If you are married , stay married . If you are not married , don't try to get married .
46007028	It isn't wrong to marry , even if you have never been married before . But those who marry will have a lot of trouble , and I want to protect you from this .
46007029	My friends , what I mean is that the Lord will soon come , and it won't matter if you are married or not .
46007030	It will be all the same if you are crying or laughing , or if you are buying or are completely broke .
46007031	It won't make any difference how much good you are getting from this world or how much you like it . This world as we know it is now passing away .
46007032	I want all of you to be free from worry . An unmarried man worries about how to please the Lord .
46007033	But a married man has more worries . He must worry about the things of this world , because he wants to please his wife .
46007034	So he is pulled in two directions . Unmarried women and women who have never been married worry only about pleasing the Lord , and they keep their bodies and minds pure . But a married woman worries about the things of this world , because she wants to please her husband .
46007035	What I am saying is for your own good — it isn't to limit your freedom . I want to help you to live right and to love the Lord above all else .
46007036	But suppose you are engaged to someone old enough to be married , and you want her so much that all you can think about is getting married . Then go ahead and marry . There is nothing wrong with that .
46007037	But it is better to have self-control and to make up your mind not to marry .
46007038	It is perfectly all right to marry , but it is better not to get married at all .
46007039	A wife should stay married to her husband until he dies . Then she is free to marry again , but only to a man who is a follower of the Lord .
46007040	However , I think I am obeying God's Spirit when I say she would be happier to stay single .
46008001	In your letter you asked me about food offered to idols . All of us know something about this subject . But knowledge makes us proud of ourselves , while love makes us helpful to others .
46008002	In fact , people who think they know so much don't know anything at all .
46008003	But God has no doubts about who loves him .
46008004	Even though food is offered to idols , we know that none of the idols in this world are alive . After all , there is only one God .
46008005	Many things in heaven and on earth are called gods and lords , but none of them really are gods or lords .
46008006	We have only one God , and he is the Father . He created everything , and we live for him . Jesus Christ is our only Lord . Everything was made by him , and by him life was given to us .
46008007	Not everyone knows these things . In fact , many people have grown up with the belief that idols have life in them . So when they eat meat offered to idols , they are bothered by a weak conscience .
46008008	But food doesn't bring us any closer to God . We are no worse off if we don't eat , and we are no better off if we do .
46008009	Don't cause problems for someone with a weak conscience , just because you have the right to eat anything .
46008010	You know all this , and so it doesn't bother you to eat in the temple of an idol . But suppose a person with a weak conscience sees you and decides to eat food that has been offered to idols .
46008011	Then what you know has destroyed someone Christ died for .
46008012	When you sin by hurting a follower with a weak conscience , you sin against Christ .
46008013	So if I hurt one of the Lord's followers by what I eat , I will never eat meat as long as I live .
46009001	I am free . I am an apostle . I have seen the Lord Jesus and have led you to have faith in him .
46009002	Others may think that I am not an apostle , but you are proof that I am an apostle to you .
46009003	When people question me , I tell them
46009004	that Barnabas and I have the right to our food and drink .
46009005	We each have the right to marry one of the Lord's followers and to take her along with us , just as the other apostles and the Lord's brothers and Peter do .
46009006	Are we the only ones who have to support ourselves by working at another job ?
46009007	Do soldiers pay their own salaries ? Don't people who raise grapes eat some of what they grow ? Don't shepherds get milk from their own goats ?
46009010	No , he wasn't ! He was talking about us . This was written in the Scriptures so that all who plow and all who grind the grain will look forward to sharing in the harvest .
46009011	When we told the message to you , it was like planting spiritual seed . So we have the right to accept material things as our harvest from you .
46009012	If others have the right to do this , we have an even greater right . But we haven't used this right of ours . We are willing to put up with anything to keep from causing trouble for the message about Christ .
46009013	Don't you know that people who work in the temple make their living from what is brought to the temple ? Don't you know that a person who serves at the altar is given part of what is offered ?
46009014	In the same way , the Lord wants everyone who preaches the good news to make a living from preaching this message .
46009015	But I have never used these privileges of mine , and I am not writing this because I want to start now . I would rather die than have someone rob me of the right to take pride in this .
46009016	I don't have any reason to brag about preaching the good news . Preaching is something God told me to do , and if I don't do it , I am doomed .
46009017	If I preach because I want to , I will be paid . But even if I don't want to , it is still something God has sent me to do .
46009018	What pay am I given ? It is the chance to preach the good news free of charge and not to use the privileges that are mine because I am a preacher .
46009019	I am not anyone's slave . But I have become a slave to everyone , so I can win as many people as possible .
46009020	When I am with the Jews , I live like a Jew to win Jews . They are ruled by the Law of Moses , and I am not . But I live by the Law to win them .
46009021	And when I am with people who are not ruled by the Law , I forget about the Law to win them . Of course , I never really forget about the law of God . In fact , I am ruled by the law of Christ .
46009022	When I am with people whose faith is weak , I live as they do to win them . I do everything I can to win everyone I possibly can .
46009023	I do all this for the good news , because I want to share in its blessings .
46009024	You know that many runners enter a race , and only one of them wins the prize . So run to win !
46009025	Athletes work hard to win a crown that cannot last , but we do it for a crown that will last forever .
46009026	I don't run without a goal . And I don't box by beating my fists in the air .
46009027	I keep my body under control and make it my slave , so I won't lose out after telling the good news to others .
46010001	Friends , I want to remind you that all our ancestors walked under the cloud and went through the sea .
46010002	This was like being baptized and becoming followers of Moses .
46010003	All of them also ate the same spiritual food
46010004	and drank the same spiritual drink , which flowed from the spiritual rock that followed them . That rock was Christ .
46010005	But most of them did not please God . So they died , and their bodies were scattered all over the desert .
46010006	What happened to them is a warning to keep us from wanting to do the same evil things .
46010007	They worshiped idols , just as the Scriptures say , “ The people sat down to eat and drink . Then they got up to dance around . ” So don't worship idols .
46010008	Some of those people did shameful things , and in a single day about 23,000 died . Don't do shameful things as they did .
46010009	And don't try to test Christ , as some of them did and were later bitten by poisonous snakes .
46010010	Don't even grumble , as some of them did and were killed by the destroying angel .
46010011	These things happened to them as a warning to us . All this was written in the Scriptures to teach us who live in these last days .
46010012	Even if you think you can stand up to temptation , be careful not to fall .
46010013	You are tempted in the same way that everyone else is tempted . But God can be trusted not to let you be tempted too much , and he will show you how to escape from your temptations .
46010014	My friends , you must keep away from idols .
46010015	I am speaking to you as people who have enough sense to know what I am talking about .
46010016	When we drink from the cup we ask God to bless , isn't that sharing in the blood of Christ ? When we eat the bread we break , isn't that sharing in the body of Christ ?
46010017	By sharing in the same loaf of bread , we become one body , even though there are many of us .
46010018	Aren't the people of Israel sharing in the worship when they gather around the altar and eat the sacrifices offered there ?
46010019	Am I saying that either the idols or the food sacrificed to them is anything at all ?
46010020	No , I am not ! This food is really sacrificed to demons and not to God . I don't want you to have anything to do with demons .
46010021	You cannot drink from the cup of demons and still drink from the Lord's cup . You cannot eat at the table of demons and still eat at the Lord's table .
46010022	We would make the Lord jealous if we did this . And we are not stronger than the Lord .
46010023	Some of you say , “ We can do whatever we want to ! ” But I tell you not everything may be good or helpful .
46010024	We should think about others and not about ourselves .
46010025	However , when you buy meat in the market , go ahead and eat it . Keep your conscience clear by not asking where the meat came from .
46010026	The Scriptures say , “ The earth and everything in it belong to the Lord . ”
46010027	If an unbeliever invites you to dinner , and you want to go , then go . Eat whatever you are served . Don't cause a problem for someone's conscience by asking where the food came from .
46010030	If I give thanks for what I eat , why should anyone accuse me of doing wrong ?
46010031	When you eat or drink or do anything else , always do it to honor God .
46010032	Don't cause problems for Jews or Greeks or anyone else who belongs to God's church .
46010033	I always try to please others instead of myself , in the hope that many of them will be saved .
46011002	I am proud of you , because you always remember me and obey the teachings I gave you .
46011003	Now I want you to know that Christ is the head of all men , and a man is the head of a woman . But God is the head of Christ .
46011004	This means that any man who prays or prophesies with something on his head brings shame to his head .
46011005	But any woman who prays or prophesies without something on her head brings shame to her head . In fact , she may as well shave her head .
46011006	A woman should wear something on her head . It is a disgrace for a woman to shave her head or cut her hair . But if she refuses to wear something on her head , let her cut off her hair .
46011007	Men were created to be like God and to bring honor to God . This means a man should not wear anything on his head . Women were created to bring honor to men .
46011008	It was the woman who was made from a man , and not the man who was made from a woman .
46011009	He wasn't created for her . She was created for him .
46011010	And so , because of this , and also because of the angels , a woman ought to wear something on her head , as a sign of her authority .
46011011	As far as the Lord is concerned , men and women need each other .
46011012	It is true that the first woman came from a man , but all other men have been given birth by women . Yet God is the one who created everything .
46011013	Ask yourselves if it is proper for a woman to pray without something on her head .
46011014	Isn't it unnatural and disgraceful for men to have long hair ?
46011015	But long hair is a beautiful way for a woman to cover her head .
46011016	This is how things are done in all of God's churches , and this is why none of you should argue about what I have said .
46011017	Your worship services do you more harm than good . I am certainly not going to praise you for this .
46011018	I am told you can't get along with each other when you worship , and I am sure that some of what I have heard is true .
46011019	You are bound to argue with each other , but it is easy to see which of you have God's approval .
46011020	When you meet together , you don't really celebrate the Lord's Supper .
46011021	You even start eating before everyone gets to the meeting , and some of you go hungry , while others get drunk .
46011022	Don't you have homes where you can eat and drink ? Do you hate God's church ? Do you want to embarrass people who don't have anything ? What can I say to you ? I certainly cannot praise you .
46011023	I have already told you what the Lord Jesus did on the night he was betrayed . And it came from the Lord himself .
46011026	The Lord meant that when you eat this bread and drink from this cup , you tell about his death until he comes .
46011027	But if you eat the bread and drink the wine in a way that isn't worthy of the Lord , you sin against his body and blood .
46011028	This is why you must examine the way you eat and drink .
46011029	If you fail to understand that you are the body of the Lord , you will condemn yourselves by the way you eat and drink .
46011030	This is why many of you are sick and weak and why a lot of others have died .
46011031	If we carefully judge ourselves , we won't be punished .
46011032	But when the Lord judges and punishes us , he does it to keep us from being condemned with the rest of the world .
46011033	My dear friends , you should wait until everyone gets there before you start eating .
46011034	If you really are hungry , you can eat at home . Then you won't condemn yourselves when you meet together . After I arrive , I will instruct you about the other matters .
46012001	My friends , you asked me about spiritual gifts .
46012002	I want you to remember that before you became followers of the Lord , you were led in all the wrong ways by idols that cannot even talk .
46012003	Now I want you to know that if you are led by God's Spirit , you will say that Jesus is Lord , and you will never curse Jesus .
46012004	There are different kinds of spiritual gifts , but they all come from the same Spirit .
46012005	There are different ways to serve the same Lord ,
46012006	and we can each do different things . Yet the same God works in all of us and helps us in everything we do .
46012007	The Spirit has given each of us a special way of serving others .
46012008	Some of us can speak with wisdom , while others can speak with knowledge , but these gifts come from the same Spirit .
46012009	To others the Spirit has given great faith or the power to heal the sick
46012010	or the power to work mighty miracles . Some of us are prophets , and some of us recognize when God's Spirit is present . Others can speak different kinds of languages , and still others can tell what these languages mean .
46012011	But it is the Spirit who does all this and decides which gifts to give to each of us .
46012012	The body of Christ has many different parts , just as any other body does .
46012013	Some of us are Jews , and others are Gentiles . Some of us are slaves , and others are free . But God's Spirit baptized each of us and made us part of the body of Christ . Now we each drink from that same Spirit .
46012014	Our bodies don't have just one part . They have many parts .
46012015	Suppose a foot says , “ I'm not a hand , and so I'm not part of the body . ” Wouldn't the foot still belong to the body ?
46012016	Or suppose an ear says , “ I'm not an eye , and so I'm not part of the body . ” Wouldn't the ear still belong to the body ?
46012017	If our bodies were only an eye , we couldn't hear a thing . And if they were only an ear , we couldn't smell a thing .
46012018	But God has put all parts of our body together in the way that he decided is best .
46012019	A body isn't really a body , unless there is more than one part .
46012020	It takes many parts to make a single body .
46012021	That's why the eyes cannot say they don't need the hands . That's also why the head cannot say it doesn't need the feet .
46012022	In fact , we cannot get along without the parts of the body that seem to be the weakest .
46012023	We take special care to dress up some parts of our bodies . We are modest about our personal parts ,
46012024	but we don't have to be modest about other parts . God put our bodies together in such a way that even the parts that seem the least important are valuable .
46012025	He did this to make all parts of the body work together smoothly , with each part caring about the others .
46012026	If one part of our body hurts , we hurt all over . If one part of our body is honored , the whole body will be happy .
46012027	Together you are the body of Christ . Each one of you is part of his body .
46012028	First , God chose some people to be apostles and prophets and teachers for the church . But he also chose some to work miracles or heal the sick or help others or be leaders or speak different kinds of languages .
46012029	Not everyone is an apostle . Not everyone is a prophet . Not everyone is a teacher . Not everyone can work miracles .
46012030	Not everyone can heal the sick . Not everyone can speak different kinds of languages . Not everyone can tell what these languages mean .
46012031	I want you to desire the best gifts . So I will show you a much better way .
46013001	What if I could speak all languages of humans and even of angels ? If I did not love others , I would be nothing more than a noisy gong or a clanging cymbal .
46013002	What if I could prophesy and understand all mysteries and all knowledge ? And what if I had faith that moved mountains ? I would be nothing , unless I loved others .
46013003	What if I gave away all that I owned and let myself be burned alive ? I would gain nothing , unless I loved others .
46013004	Love is patient and kind , never jealous , boastful , proud , or
46013005	rude . Love isn't selfish or quick tempered . It doesn't keep a record of wrongs that others do .
46013006	Love rejoices in the truth , but not in evil .
46013007	Love is always supportive , loyal , hopeful , and trusting .
46013008	Love never fails ! Everyone who prophesies will stop , and unknown languages will no longer be spoken . All that we know will be forgotten .
46013009	We don't know everything , and our prophecies are not complete .
46013010	But what is perfect will someday appear , and what isn't perfect will then disappear .
46013011	When we were children , we thought and reasoned as children do . But when we grew up , we quit our childish ways .
46013012	Now all we can see of God is like a cloudy picture in a mirror . Later we will see him face to face . We don't know everything , but then we will , just as God completely understands us .
46013013	For now there are faith , hope , and love . But of these three , the greatest is love .
46014001	Love should be your guide . Be eager to have the gifts that come from the Holy Spirit , especially the gift of prophecy .
46014002	If you speak languages that others don't know , God will understand what you are saying , though no one else will know what you mean . You will be talking about mysteries that only the Spirit understands .
46014003	But when you prophesy , you will be understood , and others will be helped . They will be encouraged and made to feel better .
46014004	By speaking languages that others don't know , you help only yourself . But by prophesying you help everyone in the church .
46014005	I am glad for you to speak unknown languages , although I prefer that you would prophesy . In fact , prophesying does much more good than speaking unknown languages , unless someone can help the church by explaining what you mean .
46014006	My friends , what good would it do , if I came and spoke unknown languages to you and didn't explain what I meant ? How would I help you , unless I told you what God had shown me or gave you some knowledge or prophecy or teaching ?
46014007	If all musical instruments sounded alike , how would you know the difference between a flute and a harp ?
46014008	If a bugle call isn't clear , how would you know to get ready for battle ?
46014009	This is how it is when you speak unknown languages . If no one can understand what you are talking about , you will only be talking to the wind .
46014010	There are many different languages in this world , and all of them make sense .
46014011	But if I don't understand the language that someone is using , we will be like foreigners to each other .
46014012	If you really want spiritual gifts , choose the ones that will be most helpful to the church .
46014013	When we speak languages that others don't know , we should pray for the power to explain what we mean .
46014014	For example , if I use an unknown language in my prayers , my spirit prays but my mind is useless .
46014015	Then what should I do ? There are times when I should pray with my spirit , and times when I should pray with my mind . Sometimes I should sing with my spirit , and at other times I should sing with my mind .
46014016	Suppose some strangers are in your worship service , when you are praising God with your spirit . If they don't understand you , how will they know to say , “ Amen ” ?
46014017	You may be worshiping God in a wonderful way , but no one else will be helped .
46014018	I thank God that I speak unknown languages more than any of you .
46014019	But words that make sense can help the church . This is why in church I would rather speak five words that make sense than to speak 10,000 words in a language that others don't know .
46014020	My friends , stop thinking like children . Think like mature people and be as innocent as tiny babies .
46014021	In the Scriptures the Lord says , “ I will use strangers who speak unknown languages to talk to my people . They will speak to them in foreign languages , but still my people won't listen to me . ”
46014022	Languages others don't know may mean something to unbelievers , but not to the Lord's followers . Prophecy , on the other hand , is for followers , not for unbelievers .
46014023	Suppose everyone in your worship service started speaking unknown languages , and some outsiders or some unbelievers come in . Won't they think you are crazy ?
46014024	But suppose all of you are prophesying when those unbelievers and outsiders come in . They will realize that they are sinners , and they will want to change their ways because of what you are saying .
46014025	They will tell what is hidden in their hearts . Then they will kneel down and say to God , “ We are certain that you are with these people . ”
46014026	My friends , when you meet to worship , you must do everything for the good of everyone there . That's how it should be when someone sings or teaches or tells what God has said or speaks an unknown language or explains what the language means .
46014027	No more than two or three of you should speak unknown languages during the meeting . You must take turns , and someone should always be there to explain what you mean .
46014028	If no one can explain , you must keep silent in church and speak only to yourself and to God .
46014029	Two or three persons may prophesy , and everyone else must listen carefully .
46014030	If someone sitting there receives a message from God , the speaker must stop and let the other person speak .
46014031	Let only one person speak at a time , then all of you will learn something and be encouraged .
46014032	A prophet should be willing to stop and let someone else speak .
46014033	God wants everything to be done peacefully and in order . When God's people meet in church ,
46014034	the women must not be allowed to speak . They must keep quiet and listen , as the Law of Moses teaches .
46014035	If there is something they want to know , they can ask their husbands when they get home . It is disgraceful for women to speak in church .
46014036	God's message did not start with you people , and you are not the only ones it has reached .
46014037	If you think of yourself as a prophet or a spiritual person , you will know I am writing only what the Lord has commanded .
46014038	So don't pay attention to anyone who ignores what I am writing .
46014039	My friends , be eager to prophesy and don't stop anyone from speaking languages that others don't know .
46014040	But do everything properly and in order .
46015001	My friends , I want you to remember the message I preached and that you believed and trusted .
46015002	You will be saved by this message , if you hold firmly to it . But if you don't , your faith was all for nothing .
46015003	I told you the most important part of the message exactly as it was told to me . This part is : Christ died for our sins , as the Scriptures say .
46015004	He was buried , and three days later he was raised to life , as the Scriptures say .
46015005	Christ appeared to Peter , then to the twelve .
46015006	After this , he appeared to more than five hundred other followers . Most of them are still alive , but some have died .
46015007	He also appeared to James , then to all of the apostles .
46015008	Finally , he appeared to me , even though I am like someone who was born at the wrong time .
46015009	I am the least important of all the apostles . In fact , I caused so much trouble for God's church that I don't even deserve to be called an apostle .
46015010	But God treated me with undeserved grace ! He made me what I am , and his grace wasn't wasted . I worked much harder than any of the other apostles , although it was really God's grace at work and not me .
46015011	But it doesn't matter if I preached or if they preached . All of you believed the message just the same .
46015012	If we preach that Christ was raised from death , how can some of you say the dead will not be raised to life ?
46015013	If they won't be raised to life , Christ himself wasn't raised to life .
46015014	And if Christ wasn't raised to life , our message is worthless , and so is your faith .
46015015	If the dead won't be raised to life , we have told lies about God by saying he raised Christ to life , when he really did not .
46015016	So if the dead won't be raised to life , Christ wasn't raised to life .
46015017	Unless Christ was raised to life , your faith is useless , and you are still living in your sins .
46015018	And those people who died after putting their faith in him are completely lost .
46015019	If our hope in Christ is good only for this life , we are worse off than anyone else .
46015020	But Christ has been raised to life ! And he makes us certain that others will also be raised to life .
46015021	Just as we will die because of Adam , we will be raised to life because of Christ .
46015022	Adam brought death to all of us , and Christ will bring life to all of us .
46015023	But we must each wait our turn . Christ was the first to be raised to life , and his people will be raised to life when he returns .
46015024	Then after Christ has destroyed all powers and forces , the end will come , and he will give the kingdom to God the Father .
46015025	Christ will rule until he puts all his enemies under his power ,
46015026	and the last enemy he destroys will be death .
46015027	When the Scriptures say he will put everything under his power , they don't include God . It was God who put everything under the power of Christ .
46015028	After everything is under the power of God's Son , he will put himself under the power of God , who put everything under his Son's power . Then God will mean everything to everyone .
46015029	If the dead are not going to be raised to life , what will people do who are being baptized for them ? Why are they being baptized for those dead people ?
46015030	And why do we always risk our lives
46015031	and face death every day ? The pride that I have in you because of Christ Jesus our Lord is what makes me say this .
46015032	What do you think I gained by fighting wild animals in Ephesus ? If the dead are not raised to life , “ Let's eat and drink . Tomorrow we die . ”
46015035	Some of you have asked , “ How will the dead be raised to life ? What kind of bodies will they have ? ”
46015036	Don't be foolish . A seed must die before it can sprout from the ground .
46015037	Wheat seeds and all other seeds look different from the sprouts that come up .
46015038	This is because God gives everything the kind of body he wants it to have .
46015039	People , animals , birds , and fish are each made of flesh , but none of them are alike .
46015040	Everything in the heavens has a body , and so does everything on earth . But each one is very different from all the others .
46015041	The sun isn't like the moon , the moon isn't like the stars , and each star is different .
46015042	That's how it will be when our bodies are raised to life . These bodies will die , but the bodies that are raised will live forever .
46015043	These ugly and weak bodies will become beautiful and strong .
46015044	As surely as there are physical bodies , there are spiritual bodies . And our physical bodies will be changed into spiritual bodies .
46015045	The first man was named Adam , and the Scriptures tell us that he was a living person . But Jesus , who may be called the last Adam , is a life-giving spirit .
46015046	We see that the one with a spiritual body did not come first . He came after the one who had a physical body .
46015047	The first man was made from the dust of the earth , but the second man came from heaven .
46015048	Everyone on earth has a body like the body of the one who was made from the dust of the earth . And everyone in heaven has a body like the body of the one who came from heaven .
46015049	Just as we are like the one who was made out of earth , we will be like the one who came from heaven .
46015050	My friends , I want you to know that our bodies of flesh and blood will decay . This means they cannot share in God's kingdom , which lasts forever .
46015051	I will explain a mystery to you . Not every one of us will die , but we will all be changed .
46015052	It will happen suddenly , quicker than the blink of an eye . At the sound of the last trumpet the dead will be raised . We will all be changed , so we will never die again .
46015053	Our dead and decaying bodies will be changed into bodies that won't die or decay .
46015054	The bodies we now have are weak and can die . But they will be changed into bodies that are eternal . Then the Scriptures will come true , “ Death has lost the battle !
46015055	Where is its victory ? Where is its sting ? ”
46015058	My dear friends , stand firm and don't be shaken . Always keep busy working for the Lord . You know that everything you do for him is worthwhile .
46016001	When you collect money for God's people , I want you to do exactly what I told the churches in Galatia to do .
46016002	That is , each Sunday each of you must put aside part of what you have earned . If you do this , you won't have to take up a collection when I come .
46016003	Choose some followers to take the money to Jerusalem . I will send them on with the money and with letters which show that you approve of them .
46016004	If you think I should go along , they can go with me .

46016006	and visit with you for a while . I may even stay all winter , so that you can help me on my way to wherever I will be going next .

46016008	I will stay in Ephesus until Pentecost ,
