46016021	I am signing this letter myself : PAUL .
46016022	I pray that God will put a curse on everyone who doesn't love the Lord . And may the Lord come soon .
46016023	I pray the Lord Jesus will be kind to you .
46016024	I love everyone who belongs to Christ Jesus .
47001001	From Paul , chosen by God to be an apostle of Jesus Christ , and from Timothy , who is also a follower . To God's church in Corinth and to all of God's people in Achaia .
47001002	I pray that God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
47001003	Praise God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ ! The Father is a merciful God , who always gives us comfort .
47001004	He comforts us when we are in trouble , so that we can share this same comfort with others in trouble .
47001005	We share in the terrible sufferings of Christ , but also in the wonderful comfort he gives .
47001006	We suffer in the hope that you will be comforted and saved . And because we are comforted , you will also be comforted , as you patiently endure suffering like ours .
47001007	You never disappoint us . You suffered as much as we did , and we know that you will be comforted as we were .
47001008	My friends , I want you to know what a hard time we had in Asia . Our sufferings were so horrible and so unbearable that death seemed certain .
47001009	In fact , we felt sure we were going to die . But this made us stop trusting in ourselves and start trusting God , who raises the dead to life .
47001010	God saved us from the threat of death , and we are sure that he will do it again and again .
47001011	Please help us by praying for us . Then many people will give thanks for the blessings we receive in answer to all these prayers .
47001012	We can be proud of our clear conscience . We have always lived honestly and sincerely , especially when we were with you . And we were guided by God's gift of undeserved grace instead of by the wisdom of this world .
47001013	I am not writing anything you cannot read and understand . I hope you will understand it completely ,
47001014	just as you already partly understand us . Then when our Lord Jesus returns , you can be as proud of us as we are of you .
47001015	I was so sure of your pride in us that I had planned to visit you first of all . In this way you would have the blessing of two visits from me
47001016	once on my way to Macedonia and again on my return from there . Then you could send me on to Judea .
47001017	Do you think I couldn't make up my mind about what to do ? Or do I seem like someone who says “ Yes ” or “ No ” simply to please others ?
47001018	God can be trusted , and so can I , when I say our answer to you has always been “ Yes ” and never “ No . ”
47001019	This is because Jesus Christ the Son of God is always “ Yes ” and never “ No . ” And he is the one Silas , Timothy , and I told you about .
47001020	Christ says “ Yes ” to all God's promises . This is why we have Christ to say “ Amen ” for us to the glory of God .
47001021	And so God makes it possible for you and us to stand firmly together with Christ . God is also the one who chose us
47001022	and put his Spirit in our hearts to show that we belong only to him .
47001023	God is my witness that I stayed away from Corinth , just to keep from being hard on you .
47001024	We are not bosses who tell you what to believe . We are working with you to make you glad , because your faith is strong .
47002001	I have decided not to make my next visit with you so painful .
47002002	If I make you feel bad , who would be left to cheer me up , except the people I had made to feel bad ?
47002003	The reason I want to be happy is to make you happy . I wrote as I did because I didn't want to visit you and be made to feel bad , when you should make me feel happy .
47002004	At the time I wrote , I was suffering terribly . My eyes were full of tears , and my heart was broken . But I didn't want to make you feel bad . I only wanted to let you know how much I cared for you .
47002005	I don't want to be hard on you . But if one of you has made someone feel bad , I am not really the one who has been made to feel bad . Some of you are the ones .
47002006	Most of you have already pointed out the wrong that person did , and this is punishment enough for what was done .
47002007	When people sin , you should forgive and comfort them , so they won't give up in despair .
47002008	You should make them sure of your love for them .
47002009	I also wrote because I wanted to test you and find out if you would follow my instructions .
47002010	I will forgive anyone you forgive . Yes , for your sake and with Christ as my witness , I have forgiven whatever needed to be forgiven .
47002011	I have done this to keep Satan from getting the better of us . We all know what goes on in his mind .
47002012	When I went to Troas to preach the good news about Christ , I found that the Lord had already prepared the way .
47002013	But I was worried when I didn't find my friend Titus there . So I left the other followers and went on to Macedonia .
47002014	I am grateful that God always makes it possible for Christ to lead us to victory . God also helps us spread the knowledge about Christ everywhere , and this knowledge is like the smell of perfume .
47002017	A lot of people try to get rich from preaching God's message . But we are God's sincere messengers , and by the power of Christ we speak our message with God as our witness .
47003001	Are we once again bragging about ourselves ? Do we need letters to you or from you to tell others about us ? Some people do need letters telling about them .
47003002	But you are our letter , and you are in our hearts for everyone to read and understand .
47003003	You are like a letter written by Christ and delivered by us . But you are not written with pen and ink or on tablets made of stone . You are written in our hearts by the Spirit of the living God .
47003004	We are sure about all this . Christ makes us sure in the very presence of God .
47003005	We don't have the right to claim that we have done anything on our own . God gives us what it takes to do all we do .
47003006	He makes us worthy to be the servants of his new agreement that comes from the Holy Spirit and not from a written Law . After all , the Law brings death , but the Spirit brings life .
47003007	The Law of Moses brought only the promise of death , even though it was carved on stones and given in a wonderful way . Still the Law made Moses' face shine so brightly the people of Israel could not look at it , even though it was a fading glory .
47003008	So won't the agreement the Spirit brings to us be even more wonderful ?
47003009	If something that brings the death sentence is glorious , won't something that makes us acceptable to God be even more glorious ?
47003010	In fact , the new agreement is so wonderful that the Law is no longer glorious at all .
47003011	The Law was given with a glory that faded away . But the glory of the new agreement is much greater , because it will never fade away .
47003012	This wonderful hope makes us feel like speaking freely .
47003013	We are not like Moses . His face was shining , but he covered it to keep the people of Israel from seeing the brightness fade away .
47003014	The people were stubborn , and something still keeps them from seeing the truth when the Law is read . Only Christ can take away the covering that keeps them from seeing .
47003015	When the Law of Moses is read , they have their minds covered over
47003016	with a covering that is removed only for those who turn to the Lord .
47003017	The Lord and the Spirit are one and the same , and the Lord's Spirit sets us free .
47003018	So our faces are not covered . They show the bright glory of the Lord , as the Lord's Spirit makes us more and more like our glorious Lord .
47004001	God has been kind enough to trust us with this work . This is why we never give up .
47004002	We don't do shameful things that must be kept secret . And we don't try to fool anyone or twist God's message around . God is our witness that we speak only the truth , so others will be sure we can be trusted .
47004003	If there is anything hidden about our message , it is hidden only to someone who is lost .
47004004	The god who rules this world has blinded the minds of unbelievers . They cannot see the light , which is the good news about our glorious Christ , who shows what God is like .
47004005	We are not preaching about ourselves . Our message is that Jesus Christ is Lord . He also sent us to be your servants .
47004006	The Scriptures say , “ God commanded light to shine in the dark . ” Now God is shining in our hearts to let you know that his glory is seen in Jesus Christ .
47004007	We are like clay jars in which this treasure is stored . The real power comes from God and not from us .
47004008	We often suffer , but we are never crushed . Even when we don't know what to do , we never give up .
47004009	In times of trouble , God is with us , and when we are knocked down , we get up again .
47004012	This means that death is working in us , but life is working in you .
47004013	In the Scriptures it says , “ I spoke because I had faith . ” We have this same kind of faith . So we speak
47004014	because we know that God raised the Lord Jesus to life . And just as God raised Jesus , he will also raise us to life . Then he will bring us into his presence together with you .
47004015	All of this has been done for you , so more and more people will know how kind God is and will praise and honor him .
47004016	We never give up . Our bodies are gradually dying , but we ourselves are being made stronger each day .
47004017	These little troubles are getting us ready for an eternal glory that will make all our troubles seem like nothing .
47004018	Things that are seen don't last forever , but things that are not seen are eternal . This is why we keep our minds on the things that cannot be seen .
47005001	Our bodies are like tents that we live in here on earth . But when these tents are destroyed , we know that God will give each of us a place to live . These homes will not be buildings someone has made , but they are in heaven and will last forever .
47005002	While we are here on earth , we sigh because we want to live in that heavenly home .
47005003	We want to put it on like clothes and not be naked .
47005004	These tents we now live in are like a heavy burden , and we groan . But we don't do this just because we want to leave these bodies that will die . It is because we want to change them for bodies that will never die .
47005005	God is the one who makes all this possible . He has given us his Spirit to make us certain he will do it .
47005006	So always be cheerful ! As long as we are in these bodies , we are away from the Lord .
47005007	But we live by faith , not by what we see .
47005008	We should be cheerful , because we would rather leave these bodies and be at home with the Lord .
47005009	But whether we are at home with the Lord or away from him , we still try our best to please him .
47005010	After all , Christ will judge each of us for the good or the bad that we do while living in these bodies .
47005011	We know what it means to respect the Lord , and we encourage everyone to turn to him . God himself knows what we are like , and I hope you also know what kind of people we are .
47005012	We are not trying once more to brag about ourselves . But we want you to be proud of us , when you are with those who are not sincere and brag about what others think of them .
47005013	If we seem out of our minds , it is between God and us . But if we are in our right minds , it is for your good .
47005014	We are ruled by Christ's love for us . We are certain that if one person died for everyone else , then all of us have died .
47005015	And Christ did die for all of us . He died so we would no longer live for ourselves , but for the one who died and was raised to life for us .
47005016	We are careful not to judge people by what they seem to be , though we once judged Christ in this way .
47005017	Anyone who belongs to Christ is a new person . The past is forgotten , and everything is new .
47005018	God has done it all ! He sent Christ to make peace between himself and us , and he has given us the work of making peace between himself and others .
47005019	What we mean is that God was in Christ , offering peace and forgiveness to the people of this world . And he has given us the work of sharing his message about peace .
47005020	We were sent to speak for Christ , and God is begging you to listen to our message . We speak for Christ and sincerely ask you to make peace with God .
47005021	Christ never sinned ! But God treated him as a sinner , so Christ could make us acceptable to God .
47006001	We work together with God , and we beg you to make good use of God's gift of undeserved grace .
47006002	In the Scriptures God says , “ When the time came , I listened to you , and when you needed help , I came to save you . ”
47006003	We don't want anyone to find fault with our work , and so we try hard not to cause problems .
47006004	But in everything and in every way we show we truly are God's servants . We have always been patient , though we have had a lot of trouble , suffering , and hard times .
47006005	We have been beaten , put in jail , and hurt in riots . We have worked hard and have gone without sleep or food .
47006006	But we have kept ourselves pure and have been understanding , patient , and kind . The Holy Spirit has been with us , and our love has been real .
47006007	We have spoken the truth , and God's power has worked in us . In all our struggles we have said and done only what is right .
47006008	Whether we were honored or dishonored or praised or cursed , we always told the truth about ourselves . But some people said we did not .
47006009	We are unknown to others , but well known to you . We seem to be dying , and yet we are still alive . We have been punished , but never killed ,
47006010	and we are always happy , even in times of suffering . Although we are poor , we have made many people rich . And though we own nothing , everything is ours .
47006011	Friends in Corinth , we are telling the truth when we say there is room in our hearts for you .
47006012	We are not holding back on our love for you , but you are holding back on your love for us .
47006013	I speak to you as I would speak to my own children . Please make room in your hearts for us .
47006014	Stay away from people who are not followers of the Lord ! Can someone who is good get along with someone who is evil ? Are light and darkness the same ?
47006015	Is Christ a friend of Satan ? Can people who follow the Lord have anything in common with those who don't ?
47006016	Do idols belong in the temple of God ? We are the temple of the living God , as God himself says , “ I will live with these people and walk among them . I will be their God , and they will be my people . ”
47006017	The Lord also says , “ Leave them and stay away ! Don't touch anything that isn't clean . Then I will welcome you
47006018	and be your Father . You will be my sons and my daughters , as surely as I am God , the All-Powerful . ”
47007001	My friends , God has made us these promises . So we should stay away from everything that keeps our bodies and spirits from being clean . We should honor God and try to be completely like him .
47007002	Make a place for us in your hearts ! We haven't mistreated or hurt anyone . We haven't cheated anyone .
47007003	I am not saying this to be hard on you . But , as I have said before , you will always be in our thoughts , whether we live or die .
47007004	I trust you completely . I am always proud of you , and I am greatly encouraged . In all my trouble I am still very happy .
47007005	After we came to Macedonia , we didn't have any chance to rest . We were faced with all kinds of problems . We were troubled by enemies and troubled by fears .
47007006	But God cheers up people in need , and this is what he did when he sent Titus to us .
47007007	Of course , we were glad to see Titus , but what really made us glad is the way you cheered him up . He told how sorry you were and how concerned you were about me . And this made me even happier .
47007008	I don't feel bad anymore , even though my letter hurt your feelings . I did feel bad at first , but I don't now . I know that the letter hurt you for a while .
47007009	Now I am happy , but not because I hurt your feelings . It is because God used your hurt feelings to make you turn back to him , and none of you were harmed by us .
47007010	When God makes you feel sorry enough to turn to him and be saved , you don't have anything to feel bad about . But when this world makes you feel sorry , it can cause your death .
47007011	Just look what God has done by making you feel sorry ! You sincerely want to prove you are innocent . You are angry . You are shocked . You are eager to see that justice is done . You have proved that you were completely right in this matter .
47007012	When I wrote you , it wasn't to accuse the one who was wrong or to take up for the one who was hurt . I wrote , so God would show you how much you do care for us .
47007013	And we were greatly encouraged . Although we were encouraged , we felt even better when we saw how happy Titus was , because you had shown he had nothing to worry about .
47007014	We had told him how much we thought of you , and you did not disappoint us . Just as we have always told you the truth , so everything we told him about you has also proved to be true .
47007015	Titus loves all of you very much , especially when he remembers how you obeyed him and how you trembled with fear when you welcomed him .
47007016	It makes me really glad to know I can depend on you .
47008001	My friends , we want you to know that the churches in Macedonia have shown others God's gift of undeserved grace .
47008002	Although they were going through hard times and were very poor , they were glad to give generously .
47008003	They gave as much as they could afford and even more , simply because they wanted to .
47008004	They even asked and begged us to let them have the joy of giving their money for God's people .
47008005	And they did more than we had hoped . They gave themselves first to the Lord and then to us , just as God wanted them to do .
47008006	Titus was the one who got you started doing this good thing , so we begged him to help you finish what you had begun .
47008007	You do everything better than anyone else . You have stronger faith . You speak better and know more . You are eager to give , and you love us better . Now you must give more generously than anyone else .
47008008	I am not ordering you to do this . I am simply testing how real your love is by comparing it with the concern that others have shown .
47008009	You know our Lord Jesus Christ treated us with undeserved grace by giving up all his riches , so you could become rich .
47008010	A year ago you were the first ones to give , and you gave because you wanted to . So listen to my advice .
47008011	I think you should finish what you started . If you give according to what you have , you will prove you are as eager to give as you were to think about giving .
47008012	It doesn't matter how much you have . What matters is how much you are willing to give from what you have .
47008013	I am not trying to make life easier for others by making life harder for you . But it is only fair
47008014	for you to share with them when you have so much , and they have so little . Later , when they have more than enough , and you are in need , they can share with you . Then everyone will have a fair share ,
47008015	just as the Scriptures say , “ Those who gathered too much had nothing left . Those who gathered only a little had all they needed . ”
47008016	I am grateful that God made Titus care as much about you as we do .
47008017	When we begged Titus to visit you , he said he would . He wanted to because he cared so much for you .
47008018	With Titus we are also sending one of the Lord's followers who is well known in every church for spreading the good news .
47008019	The churches chose this follower to travel with us while we carry this gift that will bring praise to the Lord and show how much we hope to help .
47008020	We don't want anyone to find fault with the way we handle your generous gift .
47008021	But we want to do what pleases the Lord and what people think is right .
47008022	We are also sending someone else with Titus and the other follower . We approve of this man . In fact , he has already shown us many times that he wants to help . And now he wants to help even more than ever , because he trusts you so much .
47008023	Titus is my partner , who works with me to serve you . The other two followers are sent by the churches , and they bring honor to Christ .
47008024	Treat them in such a way that the churches will see your love and will know why we bragged about you .
47009001	I don't need to write you about the money you plan to give for God's people .
47009002	I know how eager you are to give . And I have proudly told the Lord's followers in Macedonia that you people in Achaia have been ready for a whole year . Now your desire to give has made them want to give .
47009003	This is why I am sending Titus and the two others to you . I want you to be ready , just as I promised . This will prove we were not wrong to brag about you .
47009004	Some followers from Macedonia may come with me , and I want them to find that you have the money ready . If you don't , I would be embarrassed for trusting you to do this . But you would be embarrassed even more .
47009005	So I have decided to ask Titus and the others to spend some time with you before I arrive . This way they can arrange to collect the money you have promised . Then you will have the chance to give because you want to , and not because you feel forced to .
47009006	Remember this saying , “ A few seeds make a small harvest , but a lot of seeds make a big harvest . ”
47009007	Each of you must make up your own mind about how much to give . But don't feel sorry that you must give and don't feel you are forced to give . God loves people who love to give .
47009008	God can bless you with everything you need , and you will always have more than enough to do all kinds of good things for others .
47009009	The Scriptures say , “ God freely gives his gifts to the poor , and always does right . ”
47009012	What you are doing is much more than a service that supplies God's people with what they need . It is something that will make many others thank God .
47009013	The way in which you have proved yourselves by this service will bring honor and praise to God . You believed the message about Christ , and you obeyed it by sharing generously with God's people and with everyone else .
47009014	Now they are praying for you and want to see you , because God used you to bless them so very much .
47009015	Thank God for his gift that is too wonderful for words !
47010001	Do you think I am a coward when I am with you and brave when I am far away ? Well , I ask you to listen , because Christ himself was humble and gentle .
47010002	Some people have said we act like the people of this world . So when I arrive , I expect I will have to be firm and forceful in what I say to them . Please don't make me treat you that way .
47010003	We live in this world , but we don't act like its people
47010004	or fight our battles with the weapons of this world . Instead , we use God's power that can destroy fortresses . We destroy arguments
47010005	and every bit of pride that keeps anyone from knowing God . We capture people's thoughts and make them obey Christ .
47010006	And when you completely obey him , we will punish anyone who refuses to obey .
47010007	You judge by appearances . If any of you think you are the only ones who belong to Christ , then think again . We belong to Christ as much as you do .
47010008	Maybe I brag a little too much about the authority that the Lord gave me to help you and not to hurt you . Yet I am not embarrassed to brag .
47010009	And I am not trying to scare you with my letters .
47010010	Some of you are saying , “ Paul's letters are harsh and powerful . But in person , he is a weakling and has nothing worth saying . ”
47010011	Those people had better understand that when I am with you , I will do exactly what I say in my letters .
47010012	We won't dare compare ourselves with those who think so much of themselves . But they are foolish to compare themselves with themselves .
47010013	We won't brag about something we don't have a right to brag about . We will only brag about the work God has sent us to do , and you are part of that work .
47010014	We are not bragging more than we should . After all , we did bring the message about Christ to you .
47010015	We don't brag about what others have done , as if we had done those things ourselves . But I hope as you become stronger in your faith , we will be able to reach many more of the people around you . That has always been our goal .
47010016	Then we will be able to preach the good news in other lands where we cannot take credit for work someone else has already done .
47010017	The Scriptures say , “ If you want to brag , then brag about the Lord . ”
47010018	You may brag about yourself , but the only approval that counts is the Lord's approval .
47011001	Please put up with a little of my foolishness .
47011002	I am as concerned about you as God is . You were like a virgin bride I had chosen only for Christ .
47011003	But now I fear that you will be tricked , just as Eve was tricked by that lying snake . I am afraid that you might stop thinking about Christ in an honest and sincere way .
47011004	We told you about Jesus , and you received the Holy Spirit and accepted our message . But you let some people tell you about another Jesus . Now you are ready to receive another spirit and accept a different message .
47011005	I think I am as good as any of those super apostles .
47011006	I may not speak as well as they do , but I know as much . And this has already been made perfectly clear to you .
47011007	Was it wrong for me to lower myself and honor you by preaching God's message free of charge ?
47011008	I robbed other churches by taking money from them to serve you .
47011009	Even when I was in need , I still didn't bother you . In fact , some of the Lord's followers from Macedonia brought me what I needed . I have not been a burden to you in the past , and I will never be a burden .
47011010	As surely as I speak the truth about Christ , no one in Achaia can stop me from bragging about this .
47011011	And it isn't because I don't love you . God himself knows how much I do love you .
47011012	I plan to go on doing just what I have always done . Then those people won't be able to brag about doing the same things we are doing .
47011013	Anyway , they are no more than false apostles and dishonest workers . They only pretend to be apostles of Christ .
47011014	And it is no wonder . Even Satan tries to make himself look like an angel of light .
47011015	So why does it seem strange for Satan's servants to pretend to do what is right ? Someday they will get exactly what they deserve .
47011016	I don't want any of you to think I am a fool . But if you do , then let me be a fool and brag a little .
47011017	When I do all this bragging , I do it as a fool and not for the Lord .
47011018	Yet if others want to brag about what they have done , so will I .
47011019	And since you are so smart , you will gladly put up with a fool .
47011020	In fact , you let people make slaves of you and cheat you and steal from you . Why , you even let them strut around and slap you in the face .
47011021	I am ashamed to say we are too weak to behave in such a way . If they can brag , so can I , but it is a foolish thing to do .
47011022	Are they Hebrews ? So am I . Are they Jews ? So am I . Are they from the family of Abraham ? Well , so am I .
47011023	Are they servants of Christ ? I am a fool to talk this way , but I serve him better than they do . I have worked harder and have been put in jail more times . I have been beaten with whips more and have been in danger of death more often .
47011024	Five times my own people gave me 39 lashes with a whip .
47011025	Three times the Romans beat me with a big stick , and once my enemies stoned me . I have been shipwrecked three times , and I even had to spend a night and a day in the sea .
47011026	During my many travels , I have been in danger from rivers , robbers , my own people , and foreigners . My life has been in danger in cities , in deserts , at sea , and with people who only pretended to be the Lord's followers .
47011027	I have worked and struggled and spent many sleepless nights . I have gone hungry and thirsty and often had nothing to eat . I have been cold from not having enough clothes to keep me warm .
47011028	Besides everything else , each day I am burdened down , worrying about all the churches .
47011029	When others are weak , I am weak too . When others are tricked into sin , I get angry .
47011030	If I have to brag , I will brag about how weak I am .
47011031	God , the Father of our Lord Jesus , knows I am not lying . And God is to be praised forever !
47011032	The governor of Damascus at the time of King Aretas had the city gates guarded , so he could capture me .
47011033	But I escaped by being let down in a basket through a window in the city wall .
47012001	I have to brag . There is nothing to be gained by it , but I must brag about the visions and other things that the Lord has shown me .
47012002	I know about one of Christ's followers who was taken up into the third heaven 14 years ago . I don't know if the man was still in his body when it happened , but God certainly knows .
47012003	As I said , only God really knows if this man was in his body at the time .
47012004	But he was taken up into paradise , where he heard things too wonderful to tell .
47012005	I will brag about that man , but not about myself , except to say how weak I am .
47012006	Yet even if I did brag , I would not be foolish . I would simply be speaking the truth . But I will try not to say too much . That way , none of you will think more highly of me than you should because of what you have seen me do and say .
47012007	Of course , I am now referring to the wonderful things I saw . One of Satan's angels was sent to make me suffer terribly , so that I would not feel too proud .
47012008	Three times I begged the Lord to make this suffering go away .
47012009	But he replied , “ My gift of undeserved grace is all you need . My power is strongest when you are weak . ” So if Christ keeps giving me his power , I will gladly brag about how weak I am .
47012010	Yes , I am glad to be weak or insulted or mistreated or to have troubles and sufferings , if it is for Christ . Because when I am weak , I am strong .
47012011	I have been making a fool of myself . But you forced me to do it , when you should have been speaking up for me . I may be nothing at all , but I am as good as those super apostles .
47012012	When I was with you , I was patient and worked all the powerful miracles and signs and wonders of a true apostle .
47012013	You missed out on only one blessing the other churches received . That is , you didn't have to support me . Forgive me for doing you wrong .
47012014	I am planning to visit you for the third time . But I still won't make a burden of myself . What I really want is you , and not what you have . Children are not supposed to save up for their parents , but parents are supposed to take care of their children .
47012015	So I will gladly give all I have and all I am . Will you love me less for loving you too much ?
47012016	You agree that I wasn't a burden to you . Maybe that's because I was trying to catch you off guard and trick you .

47012021	I am afraid God will make me ashamed when I visit you again . I will feel like crying because many of you have never given up your old sins . You are still doing things that are immoral , indecent , and shameful .
47013001	I am on my way to visit you for the third time . And as the Scriptures say , “ Any charges must be proved true by at least two or three witnesses . ”
47013002	During my second visit I warned you that I would punish you and anyone else who doesn't stop sinning . I am far away from you now , but I give you the same warning .
47013003	This should prove to you that I am speaking for Christ . When he corrects you , he won't be weak . He will be powerful !
47013004	Although he was weak when he was nailed to the cross , he now lives by the power of God . We are weak , just as Christ was . But you will see that we will live by the power of God , just as Christ does .
47013005	Test yourselves and find out if you really are true to your faith . If you pass the test , you will discover that Christ is living in you . But if Christ isn't living in you , you have failed .
47013006	I hope you will discover we have not failed .
47013007	We pray you will stop doing evil things . We don't pray like this to make ourselves look good , but to get you to do right , even if we are failures .
47013008	All we can do is to follow the truth and not fight against it .
47013009	Even though we are weak , we are glad that you are strong , and we pray you will do even better .

48001013	You know how I used to live as a Jew . I was cruel to God's church and even tried to destroy it .

They even gave Barnabas and me a friendly handshake . This was to show that we would work with Gentiles and that they would work with Jews .
48002010	They only asked us to remember the poor , and this was something I had always been eager to do .

48003001	You stupid Galatians ! I told you exactly how Jesus Christ was nailed to a cross . Has someone now put an evil spell on you ?

48003004	Have you gone through all of this for nothing ? Is it all really for nothing ?
48003005	God gives you his Spirit and works miracles in you . But does he do this because you obey the Law of Moses or because you have heard about Christ and have faith in him ?
48003006	The Scriptures say that God accepted Abraham because Abraham had faith .
48003007	And so , you should understand that everyone who has faith is a child of Abraham .
48003008	Long ago the Scriptures said God would accept the Gentiles because of their faith . This is why God told Abraham the good news that all nations would be blessed because of him .
48003009	This means everyone who has faith will share in the blessings given to Abraham because of his faith .
48003010	Anyone who tries to please God by obeying the Law is under a curse . The Scriptures say , “ Everyone who doesn't obey everything in the Law is under a curse . ”
48003011	No one can please God by obeying the Law . The Scriptures also say , “ The people God accepts because of their faith will live . ”
48003012	The Law isn't based on faith . It promises life only to people who obey its commands .
48003013	But Christ rescued us from the Law's curse , when he became a curse in our place . This is because the Scriptures say that anyone who is nailed to a tree is under a curse .
48003014	And because of what Jesus Christ has done , the blessing promised to Abraham was taken to the Gentiles . This happened so that by faith we would be given the promised Holy Spirit .
48003015	My friends , I will use an everyday example to explain what I mean . Once someone agrees to something , no one else can change or cancel the agreement .
48003016	That is how it is with the promises God made to Abraham and his descendant . The promises were not made to many descendants , but only to one , and that one is Christ .
48003017	What I am saying is that the Law cannot change or cancel God's promise made 430 years before the Law was given .
48003018	If we have to obey the Law in order to receive God's blessings , those blessings don't really come to us because of God's promise . But God was kind to Abraham and made him a promise .
48003019	What is the use of the Law ? It was given later to show that we sin . But it was only supposed to last until the coming of that descendant who was given the promise . In fact , angels gave the Law to Moses , and he gave it to the people .
48003020	There is only one God , and the Law did not come directly from him .
48003021	Does the Law disagree with God's promises ? No , it doesn't ! If any law could give life to us , we could become acceptable to God by obeying that law .
48003022	But the Scriptures say that sin controls everyone , so that God's promises will be for anyone who has faith in Jesus Christ .
48003023	The Law controlled us and kept us under its power until the time came when we would have faith .
48003024	In fact , the Law was to be our teacher until Christ came . Then we could have faith and be acceptable to God .
48003025	But once a person has learned to have faith , there is no more need to have the Law as a teacher .

48003028	Faith in Christ Jesus is what makes each of you equal with each other , whether you are a Jew or a Greek , a slave or a free person , a man or a woman .
48003029	So if you belong to Christ , you are now part of Abraham's family , and you will be given what God has promised .

49005002	Let love be your guide . Christ loved us and offered his life for us as a sacrifice that pleases God .
49005003	You are God's people , so don't let it be said that any of you are immoral or indecent or greedy .
49005004	Don't use dirty or foolish or filthy words . Instead , say how thankful you are .
49005005	Being greedy , indecent , or immoral is just another way of worshiping idols . You can be sure people who behave in this way will never be part of the kingdom that belongs to Christ and to God .
49005006	Don't let anyone trick you with foolish talk . God punishes everyone who disobeys him and says foolish things .
49005007	So don't have anything to do with anyone like that .
49005008	You used to be like people living in the dark , but now you are people of the light because you belong to the Lord . So act like people of the light
49005009	and make your light shine . Be good and honest and truthful ,
49005010	as you try to please the Lord .
49005011	Don't take part in doing those worthless things that are done in the dark . Instead , show how wrong they are .
49005012	It is disgusting even to talk about what is done in the dark .
49005013	But the light will show what these things are really like .
49005014	Light shows up everything , just as the Scriptures say , “ Wake up from your sleep and rise from death . Then Christ will shine on you . ”
49005015	Act like people with good sense and not like fools .
49005016	These are evil times , so make every minute count .
49005017	Don't be stupid . Instead , find out what the Lord wants you to do .
49005018	Don't destroy yourself by getting drunk , but let the Spirit fill your life .
49005019	When you meet together , sing psalms , hymns , and spiritual songs , as you praise the Lord with all your heart .
49005020	Always use the name of our Lord Jesus Christ to thank God the Father for everything .
49005021	Honor Christ and put others first .
49005022	A wife should put her husband first , as she does the Lord .
49005023	A husband is the head of his wife , as Christ is the head and the Savior of the church , which is his own body .
49005024	Wives should always put their husbands first , as the church puts Christ first .
49005025	A husband should love his wife as much as Christ loved the church and gave his life for it .
49005026	He made the church holy by the power of his word , and he made it pure by washing it with water .
49005027	Christ did this , so he would have a glorious and holy church , without faults or spots or wrinkles or any other flaws .
49005028	In the same way , a husband should love his wife as much as he loves himself . A husband who loves his wife shows he loves himself .
49005029	None of us hate our own bodies . We provide for them and take good care of them , just as Christ does for the church ,
49005030	because we are each part of his body .
49005031	As the Scriptures say , “ A man leaves his father and mother to get married , and he becomes like one person with his wife . ”
49005032	This is a great mystery , but I understand it to mean Christ and his church .
49005033	So each husband should love his wife as much as he loves himself , and each wife should respect her husband .
49006001	Children , you belong to the Lord , and you do the right thing when you obey your parents . The first commandment with a promise says ,
49006002	“ Obey your father and your mother ,
49006003	and you will have a long and happy life . ”
49006004	Parents , don't be hard on your children . Raise them properly . Teach them and instruct them about the Lord .
49006005	Slaves , you must obey your earthly masters . Show them great respect and be as loyal to them as you are to Christ .
49006006	Try to please them at all times , and not just when you think they are watching . You are slaves of Christ , so with your whole heart you must do what God wants you to do .
49006007	Gladly serve your masters , as though they were the Lord himself , and not simply people .
49006008	You know that you will be rewarded for any good things you do , whether you are slaves or free .
49006009	Slave owners , you must treat your slaves with this same respect . Don't threaten them . They have the same Master in heaven that you do , and he doesn't have favorites .
49006010	Finally , let the mighty strength of the Lord make you strong .
49006011	Put on all the armor that God gives , so you can defend yourself against the devil's tricks .
49006012	We are not fighting against humans . We are fighting against forces and authorities and against rulers of darkness and powers in the spiritual world .
49006013	So put on all the armor that God gives . Then when that evil day comes , you will be able to defend yourself . And when the battle is over , you will still be standing firm .
49006014	Be ready ! Let the truth be like a belt around your waist , and let God's justice protect you like armor .
49006015	Your desire to tell the good news about peace should be like shoes on your feet .
49006016	Let your faith be like a shield , and you will be able to stop all the flaming arrows of the evil one .
49006017	Let God's saving power be like a helmet , and for a sword use God's message that comes from the Spirit .
49006018	Never stop praying , especially for others . Always pray by the power of the Spirit . Stay alert and keep praying for God's people .
49006019	Pray that I will be given the message to speak and that I may fearlessly explain the mystery about the good news .
49006020	I was sent to do this work , and this is the reason I am in jail . So pray that I will be brave and will speak as I should .
49006023	I pray that God the Father and the Lord Jesus Christ will give peace , love , and faith to every follower !
49006024	May God be kind to everyone who keeps on loving our Lord Jesus Christ .
50001001	From Paul and Timothy , servants of Christ Jesus . To all God's people who belong to Christ Jesus at Philippi and to all your bishops and deacons .
50001002	I pray that God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
50001003	Every time I think of you , I thank my God .
50001004	And whenever I mention you in my prayers , it makes me happy .
50001005	This is because you have taken part with me in spreading the good news from the first day you heard about it .
50001006	God is the one who began this good work in you , and I am certain that he won't stop before it is complete on the day that Christ Jesus returns .
50001007	You have a special place in my heart . So it is only natural for me to feel the way I do . All of you have helped in the work God has given me , as I defend the good news and tell about it here in jail .
50001008	God himself knows how much I want to see you . He knows I care for you in the same way Christ Jesus does .
50001009	I pray that your love will keep on growing and you will fully know and understand
50001010	how to make the right choices . Then you will still be pure and innocent when Christ returns . And until that day ,
50001011	Jesus Christ will keep you busy doing good deeds that bring glory and praise to God .
50001012	My dear friends , I want you to know that what has happened to me has helped to spread the good news .
50001013	The Roman guards and all the others know I am here in jail because I serve Christ .
50001014	Now most of the Lord's followers have become brave and are fearlessly telling the message .
50001015	Some are preaching about Christ because they are jealous and envious of us . Others are preaching because they want to help .
50001016	They love Christ and know I am here to defend the good news about him .
50001017	But the ones who are jealous of us are not sincere . They just want to cause trouble for me while I am in jail .
50001018	But that doesn't matter . All that matters is that people are telling about Christ , whether they are sincere or not . This is what makes me glad . I will keep on being glad ,
50001019	because I know that your prayers and the help that comes from the Spirit of Christ Jesus will keep me safe .
50001020	I honestly expect and hope I will never do anything to be ashamed of . Whether I live or die , I always want to be as brave as I am now and bring honor to Christ .
50001021	If I live , it will be for Christ , and if I die , I will gain even more .
50001022	I don't know what to choose . I could keep on living and doing something useful .
50001023	It is a hard choice to make . I want to die and be with Christ , because this would be much better .
50001026	Then , when I visit you again , you will have good reason to take great pride in Christ Jesus because of me .
50001027	Above all else , you must live in a way that brings honor to the good news about Christ . Then , whether I visit you or not , I will hear that all of you think alike . I will know that you are working together and are struggling side by side to get others to believe the good news .
50001028	Be brave when you face your enemies . Your courage will show them that they are going to be destroyed , and it will show you that you will be saved . God will make all of this happen ,
50001029	and he has blessed you . Not only do you have faith in Christ , but you suffer for him .
50001030	You saw me suffer , and you still hear about my troubles . Now you must suffer in the same way .
50002001	Christ encourages you , and his love comforts you . God's Spirit unites you , and you are concerned for others .
50002002	Now make me completely happy ! Live in harmony by showing love for each other . Be united in what you think , as if you were only one person .
50002003	Don't be jealous or proud , but be humble and consider others more important than yourselves .
50002004	Care about them as much as you care about yourselves
50002005	and think the same way that Christ Jesus thought :
50002006	Christ was truly God . But he did not try to remain equal with God .
50002007	Instead he gave up everything and became a slave , when he became like one of us .
50002008	Christ was humble . He obeyed God and even died on a cross .
50002009	Then God gave Christ the highest place and honored his name above all others .
50002010	So at the name of Jesus everyone will bow down , those in heaven , on earth , and under the earth .
50002011	And to the glory of God the Father everyone will openly agree , “ Jesus Christ is Lord ! ”
50002012	My dear friends , you always obeyed when I was with you . Now that I am away , you should obey even more . So work with fear and trembling to discover what it really means to be saved .
50002013	God is working in you to make you willing and able to obey him .
50002014	Do everything without grumbling or arguing .
50002015	Then you will be the pure and innocent children of God . You live among people who are crooked and evil , but you must not do anything they can say is wrong . Try to shine as lights among the people of this world ,
50002016	as you hold firmly to the message that gives life . Then on the day when Christ returns , I can take pride in you . I can also know that my work and efforts were not useless .
50002017	Your faith in the Lord and your service are like a sacrifice offered to him . And my own blood may have to be poured out with the sacrifice . If this happens , I will be glad and rejoice with you .
50002018	In the same way , you should be glad and rejoice with me .
50002019	I want to be encouraged by news about you . So I hope the Lord Jesus will soon let me send Timothy to you .
50002020	I don't have anyone else who cares about you as much as he does .
50002021	The others think only about what interests them and not about what concerns Christ Jesus .
50002022	But you know what kind of person Timothy is . He has worked with me like a son in spreading the good news .
50002023	I hope to send him to you , as soon as I find out what is going to happen to me .
50002024	And I feel sure the Lord will also let me come soon .
50002025	I think I ought to send my dear friend Epaphroditus back to you . He is a follower and a worker and a soldier of the Lord , just as I am . You sent him to look after me ,
50002026	but now he is eager to see you . He is worried , because you heard he was sick .
50002027	In fact , he was very sick and almost died . But God was kind to him , and also to me , and he kept me from being burdened down with sorrow .
50002028	Now I am more eager than ever to send Epaphroditus back again . You will be glad to see him , and I won't have to worry any longer .
50002029	Be sure to give him a cheerful welcome , just as people who serve the Lord deserve .
50002030	He almost died working for Christ , and he risked his own life to do for me what you could not .
50003001	Finally , my dear friends , be glad that you belong to the Lord . It doesn't bother me to write the same things to you that I have written before . In fact , it is for your own good .
50003002	Watch out for those people who behave like dogs ! They are evil and want to do more than just circumcise you .
50003003	But we are the ones who are truly circumcised , because we worship by the power of God's Spirit and take pride in Christ Jesus . We don't brag about what we have done ,
50003004	although I could . Others may brag about themselves , but I have more reason to brag than anyone else .
50003005	I was circumcised when I was eight days old , and I am from the nation of Israel and the tribe of Benjamin . I am a true Hebrew . As a Pharisee , I strictly obeyed the Law of Moses .
50003006	And I was so eager I even made trouble for the church . I did everything the Law demands in order to please God .
50003007	But Christ has shown me that what I once thought was valuable is worthless .
50003008	Nothing is as wonderful as knowing Christ Jesus my Lord . I have given up everything else and count it all as garbage . All I want is Christ
50003009	and to know that I belong to him . I could not make myself acceptable to God by obeying the Law of Moses . God accepted me simply because of my faith in Christ .
50003010	All I want is to know Christ and the power that raised him to life . I want to suffer and die as he did ,
50003011	so that somehow I also may be raised to life .
50003012	I have not yet reached my goal , and I am not perfect . But Christ has taken hold of me . So I keep on running and struggling to take hold of the prize .
50003013	My friends , I don't feel I have already arrived . But I forget what is behind , and I struggle for what is ahead .
50003014	I run toward the goal , so I can win the prize of being called to heaven . This is the prize God offers because of what Christ Jesus has done .
50003015	All of us who are mature should think in this same way . And if any of you think differently , God will make it clear to you .
50003016	But we must keep going in the direction that we are now headed .
50003017	My friends , I want you to follow my example and learn from others who closely follow the example we set for you .
50003018	I often warned you that many people are living as enemies of the cross of Christ . And now with tears in my eyes , I warn you again
50003019	that they are headed for hell ! They worship their stomachs and brag about the disgusting things they do . All they can think about are the things of this world .
50003020	But we are citizens of heaven and are eagerly waiting for our Savior to come from there . Our Lord Jesus Christ
50003021	has power over everything , and he will make these poor bodies of ours like his own glorious body .
50004001	Dear friends , I love you and long to see you . Please keep on being faithful to the Lord . You are my pride and joy .
50004002	Euodia and Syntyche , you belong to the Lord , so I beg you to stop arguing with each other .
50004003	And , my true partner , I ask you to help them . These women have worked together with me and with Clement and with the others in spreading the good news . Their names are now written in the book of life .
50004004	Always be glad because of the Lord ! I will say it again : Be glad .
50004005	Always be gentle with others . The Lord will soon be here .
50004006	Don't worry about anything , but pray about everything . With thankful hearts offer up your prayers and requests to God .
50004007	Then , because you belong to Christ Jesus , God will bless you with peace that no one can completely understand . And this peace will control the way you think and feel .
50004008	Finally , my friends , keep your minds on whatever is true , pure , right , holy , friendly , and proper . Don't ever stop thinking about what is truly worthwhile and worthy of praise .
50004009	You know the teachings I gave you , and you know what you heard me say and saw me do . So follow my example . And God , who gives peace , will be with you .
50004010	The Lord has made me very grateful that at last you have thought about me once again . Actually , you were thinking about me all along , but you didn't have any chance to show it .
50004011	I am not complaining about having too little . I have learned to be satisfied with whatever I have .
50004012	I know what it is to be poor or to have plenty , and I have lived under all kinds of conditions . I know what it means to be full or to be hungry , to have too much or too little .
50004013	Christ gives me the strength to face anything .
50004014	It was good of you to help me when I was having such a hard time .
50004015	My friends at Philippi , you remember what it was like when I started preaching the good news in Macedonia . After I left there , you were the only church that became my partner by giving blessings and by receiving them in return .
50004016	Even when I was in Thessalonica , you helped me more than once .
50004017	I am not trying to get something from you , but I want you to receive the blessings that come from giving .
50004018	I have been paid back everything , and with interest . I am completely satisfied with the gifts you sent with Epaphroditus . They are like a sweet-smelling offering or like the right kind of sacrifice that pleases God .
50004019	I pray that God will take care of all your needs with the wonderful blessings that come from Christ Jesus !

51001001	From Paul , chosen by God to be an apostle of Christ Jesus , and from Timothy , who is also a follower .

51001003	Each time we pray for you , we thank God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ .
51001004	We have heard of your faith in Christ and of your love for all God's people ,
51001005	because what you hope for is kept safe for you in heaven . You first heard about this hope when you believed the true message , which is the good news .
51001006	The good news is spreading all over the world with great success . It has spread in this same way among you , ever since the first day you learned the truth about God's wonderful kindness
51001007	from our good friend Epaphras . He works together with us for Christ and is a faithful worker for you .
51001008	He is also the one who told us about the love that God's Spirit has given you .
51001009	We have not stopped praying for you since the first day we heard about you . In fact , we always pray that God will show you everything he wants you to do and that you may have all the wisdom and understanding his Spirit gives .
51001010	Then you will live a life that honors the Lord , and you will always please him by doing good deeds . You will come to know God even better .
51001011	His glorious power will make you patient and strong enough to endure anything , and you will be truly happy .
51001012	I pray that you will be grateful to God for letting you have part in what he has promised his people in the kingdom of light .
51001013	God rescued us from the dark power of Satan and brought us into the kingdom of his dear Son ,
51001014	who forgives our sins and sets us free .
51001015	Christ is exactly like God , who cannot be seen . He is the first-born Son , superior to all creation .
51001016	Everything was created by him , everything in heaven and on earth , everything seen and unseen , including all forces and powers , and all rulers and authorities . All things were created by God's Son , and everything was made for him .
51001017	God's Son was before all else , and by him everything is held together .
51001018	He is the head of his body , which is the church . He is the very beginning , the first to be raised from death , so that he would be above all others .
51001019	God himself was pleased to live fully in his Son .
51001020	And God was pleased for him to make peace by sacrificing his blood on the cross , so that all beings in heaven and on earth would be brought back to God .
51001021	You used to be far from God . Your thoughts made you his enemies , and you did evil things .
51001022	But his Son became a human and died . So God made peace with you , and now he lets you stand in his presence as people who are holy and faultless and innocent .
51001023	But you must stay deeply rooted and firm in your faith . You must not give up the hope you received when you heard the good news . It was preached to everyone on earth , and I myself have become a servant of this message .
51001024	I am glad I can suffer for you . I am pleased also that in my own body I can continue the suffering of Christ for his body , the church .
51001025	God's plan was to make me a servant of his church and to send me to preach his complete message to you .
51001026	For ages and ages this message was kept secret from everyone , but now it has been explained to God's people .
51001027	God did this because he wanted you Gentiles to understand his wonderful and glorious mystery . And the mystery is that Christ lives in you , and he is your hope of sharing in God's glory .
51001028	We announce the message about Christ , and we use all our wisdom to warn and teach everyone , so all of Christ's followers will grow and become mature .
51001029	This is why I work so hard and use the mighty power he gives me .
51002001	I want you to know what a struggle I am going through for you , for God's people at Laodicea , and for all of those followers who have never met me .
51002002	I do it to encourage them . Then as their hearts are joined together in love , they will be wonderfully blessed with complete understanding . And they will truly know Christ . Not only is he the key to God's mystery ,
51002003	but all wisdom and knowledge are hidden away in him .
51002004	I tell you these things to keep you from being fooled by fancy talk .
51002005	Even though I am not with you , I keep thinking about you . I am glad to know that you are living as you should and your faith in Christ is strong .
51002006	You have accepted Christ Jesus as your Lord . Now keep on following him .
51002007	Plant your roots in Christ and let him be the foundation for your life . Be strong in your faith , just as you were taught . And be grateful .
51002008	Don't let anyone fool you by using senseless arguments . These arguments may sound wise , but they are only human teachings . They come from the powers of this world and not from Christ .
51002009	God lives fully in Christ .
51002010	And you are fully grown because you belong to Christ , who is over every power and authority .
51002011	Christ has also taken away your selfish desires , just as circumcision removes flesh from the body .
51002012	And when you were baptized , it was the same as being buried with Christ . Then you were raised to life because you had faith in the power of God , who raised Christ from death .
51002013	You were dead , because you were sinful and were not God's people . But God let Christ make you alive , when he forgave all our sins .
51002014	God wiped out the charges that were against us for disobeying the Law of Moses . He took them away and nailed them to the cross .
51002015	There Christ defeated all powers and forces . He let the whole world see them being led away as prisoners when he celebrated his victory .
51002016	Don't let anyone tell you what you must eat or drink . Don't let them say you must celebrate the New Moon festival , the Sabbath , or any other festival .
51002017	These things are only a shadow of what was to come . But Christ is real !
51002018	Don't be cheated by people who make a show of acting humble and who worship angels . They brag about seeing visions . But it is all nonsense , because their minds are filled with selfish desires .
51002019	They are no longer part of Christ , who is the head of the whole body . Christ gives the body its strength , and he uses its joints and muscles to hold it together , as it grows by the power of God .
51002020	You died with Christ . Now the forces of the universe don't have any power over you . Why do you live as if you had to obey such rules as ,
51002021	“ Don't handle this . Don't taste that . Don't touch this . ” ?
51002022	After these things are used , they are no longer good for anything . So why be bothered with the rules that humans have made up ?
51002023	Obeying these rules may seem to be the smart thing to do . They appear to make you love God more and to be very humble and to have control over your body . But they don't really have any power over our desires .
51003001	You have been raised to life with Christ . Now set your heart on what is in heaven , where Christ rules at God's right side .
51003002	Think about what is up there , not about what is here on earth .
51003003	You died , which means that your life is hidden with Christ , who sits beside God .
51003004	Christ gives meaning to your life , and when he appears , you will also appear with him in glory .
51003005	Don't be controlled by your body . Kill every desire for the wrong kind of sex . Don't be immoral or indecent or have evil thoughts . Don't be greedy , which is the same as worshiping idols .
51003006	God is angry with people who disobey him by doing these things .
51003007	And this is exactly what you did , when you lived among people who behaved in this way .
51003008	But now you must stop doing such things . You must quit being angry , hateful , and evil . You must no longer say insulting or cruel things about others .
51003009	And stop lying to each other . You have given up your old way of life with its habits .
51003010	Each of you is now a new person . You are becoming more and more like your Creator , and you will understand him better .
51003011	It doesn't matter if you are a Greek or a Jew , or if you are circumcised or not . You may even be a barbarian or a Scythian , and you may be a slave or a free person . Yet Christ is all that matters , and he lives in all of us .
51003012	God loves you and has chosen you as his own special people . So be gentle , kind , humble , meek , and patient .
51003013	Put up with each other , and forgive anyone who does you wrong , just as Christ has forgiven you .
51003014	Love is more important than anything else . It is what ties everything completely together .
51003015	Each one of you is part of the body of Christ , and you were chosen to live together in peace . So let the peace that comes from Christ control your thoughts . And be grateful .
51003016	Let the message about Christ completely fill your lives , while you use all your wisdom to teach and instruct each other . With thankful hearts , sing psalms , hymns , and spiritual songs to God .
51003017	Whatever you say or do should be done in the name of the Lord Jesus , as you give thanks to God the Father because of him .
51003018	A wife must put her husband first . This is her duty as a follower of the Lord .
51003019	A husband must love his wife and not abuse her .
51003020	Children must always obey their parents . This pleases the Lord .
51003021	Parents , don't be hard on your children . If you are , they might give up .
51003022	Slaves , you must always obey your earthly masters . Try to please them at all times , and not just when you think they are watching . Honor the Lord and serve your masters with your whole heart .
51003023	Do your work willingly , as though you were serving the Lord himself , and not just your earthly master .
51003024	In fact , the Lord Christ is the one you are really serving , and you know he will reward you .
51003025	But Christ has no favorites ! He will punish evil people , just as they deserve .
51004001	Slave owners , be fair and honest with your slaves . Don't forget that you have a Master in heaven .
51004002	Never give up praying . And when you pray , keep alert and be thankful .
51004003	Be sure to pray that God will make a way for us to spread his message and explain the mystery about Christ , even though I am in jail for doing this .

52001006	So , when you accepted the message , you followed our example and the example of the Lord . You suffered , but the Holy Spirit made you glad .
52001007	You became an example for all the Lord's followers in Macedonia and Achaia .
52001008	And because of you , the Lord's message has spread everywhere in those regions . Now the news of your faith in God is known all over the world , and we don't have to say a thing about it .
52001009	Everyone is talking about how you welcomed us and how you turned away from idols to serve the true and living God .
52001010	They also tell how you are waiting for his Son Jesus to come from heaven . God raised him from death , and on the day of judgment Jesus will save us from God's anger .
52002001	My friends , you know our time with you wasn't wasted .
52002002	As you remember , we had been mistreated and insulted at Philippi . But God gave us the courage to tell you the good news about him , even though many people caused us trouble .
52002003	We didn't have any hidden motives when we won you over , and we didn't try to fool or trick anyone .
52002004	God was pleased to trust us with his message . We didn't speak to please people , but to please God who knows our motives .
52002005	You also know we didn't try to flatter anyone . God himself knows what we did wasn't a cover-up for greed .
52002006	We were not trying to get you or anyone else to praise us .
52002007	But as apostles , we could have demanded help from you . After all , Christ is the one who sent us . We chose to be like children or like a mother nursing her baby .
52002008	We cared so much for you , and you became so dear to us , that we were willing to give our lives for you when we gave you God's message .
52002009	My dear friends , you surely haven't forgotten our hard work and hardships . You remember how night and day we struggled to make a living , so we could tell you God's message without being a burden to anyone .
52002010	Both you and God are witnesses that we were pure and honest and innocent in our dealings with you followers of the Lord .
52002011	You also know we did everything for you that parents would do for their own children .
52002012	We begged , encouraged , and urged each of you to live in a way that would honor God . He is the one who chose you to share in his own kingdom and glory .
52002013	We always thank God that you believed the message we preached . It came from him , and it isn't something made up by humans . You accepted it as God's message , and now he is working in you .
52002014	My friends , you did just like God's churches in Judea and like the other followers of Christ Jesus there . And so , you were mistreated by your own people , in the same way they were mistreated by their people .
52002015	Those evil people killed the Lord Jesus and the prophets , and they even chased us away . God doesn't like what they do and neither does anyone else .
52002016	They keep us from speaking his message to the Gentiles and from leading them to be saved . They have always gone too far with their sins . Now God has finally become angry and will punish them .
52002017	My friends , we were kept from coming to you for a while , but we never stopped thinking about you . We were eager to see you and tried our best to visit you in person .
52002018	We really wanted to come . I myself tried several times , but Satan always stopped us .
52002019	After all , when the Lord Jesus appears , who else but you will give us hope and joy and be like a glorious crown for us ?
52002020	You alone are our glory and joy !
52003001	Finally , we couldn't stand it any longer . We decided to stay in Athens by ourselves
52003002	and send our friend Timothy to you . He works with us as God's servant and preaches the good news about Christ . We wanted him to make you strong in your faith and to encourage you .
52003003	We didn't want any of you to be discouraged by all these troubles . You knew we would have to suffer ,
52003004	because when we were with you , we told you this would happen . And we did suffer , as you well know .
52003005	At last , when I could not wait any longer , I sent Timothy to find out about your faith . I hoped Satan had not tempted you and made all our work useless .
52003006	Timothy has now come back from his visit with you and has told us about your faith and love . He also said that you always have happy memories of us and that you want to see us as much as we want to see you .
52003007	My friends , even though we have a lot of trouble and suffering , your faith makes us feel better about you .
52003008	Your strong faith in the Lord is like a breath of new life .
52003009	How can we possibly thank God enough for all the happiness you have brought us ?
52003010	Day and night we sincerely pray that we will see you again and help you to have an even stronger faith .
52003011	We pray that God our Father and our Lord Jesus will let us visit you .
52003012	May the Lord make your love for each other and for everyone else grow by leaps and bounds . This is how our love for you has grown .
52003013	And when our Lord comes with all his people , I pray he will make your hearts pure and innocent in the sight of God the Father .
52004001	Finally , my dear friends , since you belong to the Lord Jesus , we beg and urge you to live as we taught you . Then you will please God . You are already living that way , but try even harder .
52004002	Remember the instructions we gave you as followers of the Lord Jesus .
52004003	God wants you to be holy , so don't be immoral in matters of sex .
52004004	Respect and honor your wife .
52004005	Don't be a slave of your desires or live like people who don't know God .
52004006	You must not cheat any of the Lord's followers in matters of sex . Remember , we warned you that he punishes everyone who does such things .
52004007	God didn't choose you to be filthy , but to be pure .
52004008	So if you don't obey these rules , you are not really disobeying us . Instead , you are disobeying God , who gives you his Holy Spirit .
52004009	We don't have to write you about the need to love each other . God has taught you to do this ,
52004010	and you already have shown your love for all his people in Macedonia . But , my dear friends , we ask you to do even more .
52004011	Try your best to live quietly , to mind your own business , and to work hard , just as we taught you to do .
52004012	Then you will be respected by people who are not followers of the Lord , and you won't have to depend on anyone .
52004013	My friends , we want you to understand how it will be for those followers who have already died . Then you won't grieve over them and be like people who don't have any hope .
52004014	We believe Jesus died and was raised to life . We also believe that when God brings Jesus back again , he will bring with him all who had faith in Jesus before they died .
52004015	Our Lord Jesus told us that when he comes , we won't go up to meet him ahead of his followers who have already died .
52004016	With a loud command and with the shout of the chief angel and a blast of God's trumpet , the Lord will return from heaven . Then those who had faith in Christ before they died will be raised to life .
52004017	Next , all of us who are still alive will be taken up into the clouds together with them to meet the Lord in the sky . From that time on we will all be with the Lord forever .
52004018	Encourage each other with these words .
52005001	I don't need to write you about the time or date when all this will happen .
52005002	You surely know that the Lord's return will be as a thief coming at night .
52005003	People will think they are safe and secure . But destruction will suddenly strike them like the pains of a woman about to give birth . And they won't escape .
52005004	My dear friends , you don't live in darkness , and so that day won't surprise you like a thief .
52005005	You belong to the light and live in the day . We don't live in the night or belong to the dark .
52005006	Others may sleep , but we should stay awake and be alert .
52005007	People sleep during the night , and some even get drunk .
52005008	But we belong to the day . So we must stay sober and let our faith and love be like a suit of armor . Our firm hope that we will be saved is our helmet .
52005009	God doesn't intend to punish us , but wants us to be saved by our Lord Jesus Christ .
52005010	Christ died for us , so we could live with him , whether we are alive or dead when he comes .
52005011	This is why you must encourage and help each other , just as you are already doing .
52005012	My friends , we ask you to be thoughtful of your leaders who work hard and tell you how to live for the Lord .
52005013	Show them great respect and love because of their work . Try to get along with each other .
52005014	My friends , we beg you to warn anyone who isn't living right . Encourage anyone who feels left out , help all who are weak , and be patient with everyone .
52005015	Don't be hateful to people , just because they are hateful to you . Rather , be good to each other and to everyone else .
52005016	Always be joyful
52005017	and never stop praying .
52005018	Whatever happens , keep thanking God because of Jesus Christ . This is what God wants you to do .
52005019	Don't turn away God's Spirit
52005020	or ignore prophecies .
52005021	Put everything to the test . Accept what is good
52005022	and don't have anything to do with evil .
52005023	I pray that God , who gives peace , will make you completely holy . And may your spirit , soul , and body be kept healthy and faultless until our Lord Jesus Christ returns .
52005024	The one who chose you can be trusted , and he will do this .
52005025	Friends , please pray for us .
52005026	Give the Lord's followers a warm greeting .
52005027	In the name of the Lord I beg you to read this letter to all his followers .
52005028	I pray that our Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you !
53001001	From Paul , Silas , and Timothy . To the church in Thessalonica , the people of God our Father and of the Lord Jesus Christ .
53001002	I pray that God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
53001003	My dear friends , we always have good reason to thank God for you , because your faith in God and your love for each other keep growing all the time .
53001004	This is why we brag about you to all of God's churches . We tell them how patient you are and how you keep on having faith , even though you are going through a lot of trouble and suffering .
53001005	All this shows that God judges fairly and is making you fit to share in his kingdom for which you are suffering .
53001006	It is only right for God to punish everyone who is causing you trouble ,
53001007	but he will give you relief from your troubles . God will do the same for us , when the Lord Jesus comes from heaven with his powerful angels
53001008	and with a flaming fire . Our Lord Jesus will punish anyone who doesn't know God and won't obey his message .
53001009	Their punishment will be eternal destruction , and they will be kept far from the presence of our Lord and his glorious strength .
53001010	This will happen on the day when the Lord returns to be praised and honored by all who have faith in him and belong to him . This includes you , because you believed what we said .
53001011	God chose you , and we keep praying that God will make you worthy of being his people . We pray for God's power to help you do all the good things you hope to do and your faith makes you want to do .
53001012	Then , because of the undeserved grace of God and our Lord Jesus Christ , you will bring honor to the name of our Lord Jesus , and he will bring honor to you .
53002001	When our Lord Jesus returns , we will be gathered up to meet him . So I ask you , my friends ,
53002002	not to be easily upset or disturbed by people who claim the Lord has already come . They may say they heard this directly from the Holy Spirit , or from someone else , or even that they read it in one of our letters .
53002003	But don't be fooled ! People will rebel against God . Then before the Lord returns , the wicked one who is doomed to be destroyed will appear .
53002004	He will brag and oppose everything holy or sacred . He will even sit in God's temple and claim to be God .
53002005	Don't you remember I told you this while I was still with you ?
53002006	You already know what is holding this wicked one back until it is time for him to come .
53002007	His mysterious power is already at work , but someone is holding him back . And the wicked one won't appear until this someone is out of the way .
53002008	Then he will appear , but the Lord Jesus will kill him simply by breathing on him . He will be completely destroyed by the Lord's glorious return .
53002009	When the wicked one appears , Satan will pretend to work all kinds of miracles , wonders , and signs .
53002010	Lost people will be fooled by his evil deeds . They could be saved , but they will refuse to love the truth and accept it .
53002011	So God will make sure they are fooled into believing a lie .
53002012	All of them will be punished , because they would rather do evil than believe the truth .
53002013	My friends , the Lord loves you , and it is only natural for us to thank God for you . God chose you to be the first ones to be saved . His Spirit made you holy , and you put your faith in the truth .
53002014	God used our preaching as his way of inviting you to share in the glory of our Lord Jesus Christ .
53002015	My friends , this is why you must remain faithful and follow closely what we taught you in person and by our letters .
