53002016	God our Father loves us . He treats us with undeserved grace and has given us eternal comfort and a wonderful hope . We pray that our Lord Jesus Christ and God our Father
53002017	will encourage you and help you always to do and say the right thing .
53003001	Finally , our friends , please pray for us . This will help the message about the Lord to spread quickly , and others will respect it , just as you do .
53003002	Pray that we may be kept safe from worthless and evil people . After all , not everyone has faith .
53003003	But the Lord can be trusted to make you strong and protect you from harm .
53003004	He has made us sure that you are obeying what we taught you and that you will keep on obeying .
53003005	I pray that the Lord will guide you to be as loving as God and as patient as Christ .
53003006	My dear friends , in the name of the Lord Jesus , I beg you not to have anything to do with any of your people who loaf around and refuse to obey the instructions we gave you .
53003007	You surely know that you should follow our example . We didn't waste our time loafing ,
53003008	and we didn't accept food from anyone without paying for it . We didn't want to be a burden to any of you , so night and day we worked as hard as we could .
53003009	We had the right not to work , but we wanted to set an example for you .
53003010	We also gave you this rule : If you don't work , you don't eat .
53003011	Now we learn that some of you just loaf around and won't do any work , except the work of a busybody .
53003012	So , for the sake of our Lord Jesus Christ , we ask and beg these people to settle down and start working for a living .
53003013	Dear friends , you must never become tired of doing right .
53003014	Be on your guard against any followers who refuse to obey what we have written in this letter . Put them to shame by not having anything to do with them .
53003015	Don't consider them your enemies . Instead , speak kindly to them as you would to any other follower .
53003016	I pray that the Lord , who gives peace , will always bless you with peace . May the Lord be with all of you .
53003017	I always sign my letters as I am now doing : PAUL .
53003018	I pray that our Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to all of you .
54001001	From Paul . God our Savior and Christ Jesus commanded me to be an apostle of Christ Jesus , who gives us hope .
54001002	Timothy , because of our faith , you are like a son to me . I pray that God our Father and our Lord Jesus Christ will be kind and merciful to you . May they bless you with peace !
54001003	When I was leaving for Macedonia , I asked you to stay on in Ephesus and warn certain people there to stop spreading their false teachings .
54001004	You needed to warn them to stop wasting their time on senseless stories and endless lists of ancestors . Such things only cause arguments . They don't help anyone to do God's work that can only be done by faith .
54001005	You must teach people to have genuine love , as well as a good conscience and true faith .
54001006	There are some who have given up these for nothing but empty talk .
54001007	They want to be teachers of the Law of Moses . But they don't know what they are talking about , even though they think they do .
54001008	We know the Law is good , if it is used in the right way .
54001009	We also understand it wasn't given to control people who please God , but to control lawbreakers , criminals , godless people , and sinners . It is for wicked and evil people , and for murderers , who would even kill their own parents .
54001010	The Law was written for people who are sexual perverts or who live as homosexuals or are kidnappers or liars or won't tell the truth in court . It is for anything else that opposes the correct teaching
54001011	of the good news the glorious and wonderful God has given me .
54001012	I thank Christ Jesus our Lord , who has given me the strength for my work because he knew he could trust me .
54001013	I used to say terrible and insulting things about him , and I was cruel . But Christ had mercy on me because I didn't know what I was doing , and I had not yet put my faith in him .
54001014	Christ Jesus our Lord treated me with undeserved grace and has greatly blessed my life with faith and love just like his own .
54001015	“ Christ Jesus came into the world to save sinners . ” This saying is true , and it can be trusted . I was the worst sinner of all !
54001016	But since I was worse than anyone else , God had mercy on me and let me be an example of the endless patience of Christ Jesus . He did this so that others would put their faith in Christ and have eternal life .
54001017	I pray that honor and glory will always be given to the only God , who lives forever and is the invisible and eternal King ! Amen .
54001018	Timothy , my son , the instructions I am giving you are based on what some prophets once said about you . If you follow these instructions , you will fight like a good soldier .
54001019	You will be faithful and have a clear conscience . Some people have made a mess of their faith because they didn't listen to their consciences .
54001020	Two of them are Hymenaeus and Alexander . I have given these men over to the power of Satan , so they will learn not to oppose God .
54002001	First of all , I ask you to pray for everyone . Ask God to help and bless them all , and tell God how thankful you are for each of them .
54002002	Pray for kings and others in power , so we may live quiet and peaceful lives as we worship and honor God .
54002003	This kind of prayer is good , and it pleases God our Savior .
54002004	God wants everyone to be saved and to know the whole truth , which is ,
54002005	There is only one God , and Christ Jesus is the only one who can bring us to God . Jesus was truly human , and he gave himself to rescue all of us .
54002006	God showed us this at the right time .
54002008	I want everyone everywhere to lift innocent hands toward heaven and pray , without being angry or arguing with each other .
54002009	I would like for women to wear modest and sensible clothes . They should not have fancy hairdos , or wear expensive clothes , or put on jewelry made of gold or pearls .
54002010	Women who claim to love God should do helpful things for others ,
54002011	and they should learn by being quiet and paying attention .
54002012	They should be silent and not be allowed to teach or to tell men what to do .
54002013	After all , Adam was created before Eve ,
54002014	and the man Adam wasn't the one who was fooled . It was the woman Eve who was completely fooled and sinned .
54002015	But women will be saved by having children , if they stay faithful , loving , holy , and modest .
54003001	It is true that anyone who desires to be a church official wants to be something worthwhile .
54003002	That's why officials must have a good reputation and be faithful in marriage . They must be self-controlled , sensible , well-behaved , friendly to strangers , and able to teach .
54003003	They must not be heavy drinkers or troublemakers . Instead , they must be kind and gentle and not love money .
54003004	Church officials must be in control of their own families , and they must see that their children are obedient and always respectful .
54003005	If they don't know how to control their own families , how can they look after God's people ?
54003006	They must not be new followers of the Lord . If they are , they might become proud and be doomed along with the devil .
54003007	Finally , they must be well-respected by people who are not followers . Then they won't be trapped and disgraced by the devil .
54003008	Church officers should be serious . They must not be liars , heavy drinkers , or greedy for money .
54003009	And they must have a clear conscience and hold firmly to what God has shown us about our faith .
54003010	They must first prove themselves . Then if no one has anything against them , they can serve as officers .
54003011	Women must also be serious . They must not gossip or be heavy drinkers , and they must be faithful in everything they do .
54003012	Church officers must be faithful in marriage . They must be in full control of their children and everyone else in their home .
54003013	Those who serve well as officers will earn a good reputation and will be highly respected for their faith in Christ Jesus .
54003014	I hope to visit you soon . But I am writing these instructions ,
54003015	so if I am delayed , you will know how everyone who belongs to God's family ought to behave . After all , the church of the living God is the strong foundation of truth .
54003016	Here is the great mystery of our religion : Christ came as a human . The Spirit proved that he pleased God , and he was seen by angels . Christ was preached to the nations . People in this world put their faith in him , and he was taken up to glory .
54004001	God's Spirit clearly says that in the last days many people will turn from their faith . They will be fooled by evil spirits and by teachings that come from demons .
54004002	They will also be fooled by the false claims of liars whose consciences have lost all feeling . These liars
54004003	will forbid people to marry or to eat certain foods . But God created these foods to be eaten with thankful hearts by his followers who know the truth .
54004004	Everything God created is good . And if you give thanks , you may eat anything .
54004005	What God has said and your prayer will make it fit to eat .
54004006	If you teach these things to other followers , you will be a good servant of Christ Jesus . You will show you have grown up on the teachings about our faith and on the good instructions you have obeyed .
54004007	Don't have anything to do with worthless , senseless stories . Work hard to be truly religious .
54004011	Teach these things and tell everyone to do what you say .
54004012	Don't let anyone make fun of you , just because you are young . Set an example for other followers by what you say and do , as well as by your love , faith , and purity .
54004013	Until I arrive , be sure to keep on reading the Scriptures in worship , and don't stop preaching and teaching .
54004014	Use the gift you were given when the prophets spoke and the group of church leaders blessed you by placing their hands on you .
54004015	Remember these things and think about them , so everyone can see how well you are doing .
54004016	Be careful about the way you live and about what you teach . Keep on doing this , and you will save not only yourself , but the people who hear you .
54005001	Don't correct an older man . Encourage him , as you would your own father . Treat younger men as you would your own brother ,
54005002	and treat older women as you would your own mother . Show the same respect to younger women that you would to your sister .
54005003	Take care of any widow who is really in need .
54005004	But if a widow has children or grandchildren , they should learn to serve God by taking care of her , as she once took care of them . This is what God wants them to do .
54005005	A widow who is really in need is one who doesn't have any relatives . She has faith in God , and she keeps praying to him night and day , asking for his help .
54005006	A widow who thinks only about having a good time is already dead , even though she is still alive .
54005007	Tell all this to everyone , so they will do the right thing .
54005008	People who don't take care of their relatives , and especially their own families , have given up their faith . They are worse than someone who doesn't have faith in the Lord .
54005009	For a widow to be put on the list of widows , she must be at least 60 years old , and she must have been faithful in marriage .
54005010	She must also be well-known for doing all sorts of good things , such as raising children , giving food to strangers , welcoming God's people into her home , helping people in need , and always making herself useful .
54005011	Don't put young widows on the list . They may later have a strong desire to get married . Then they will turn away from Christ
54005012	and become guilty of breaking their promise to him .
54005013	Besides , they will become lazy and get into the habit of going from house to house . Next , they will start gossiping and become busybodies , talking about things that are none of their business .
54005014	I would prefer that young widows get married , have children , and look after their families . Then the enemy won't have any reason to say insulting things about us .
54005015	Look what's already happened to some of the young widows ! They have turned away to follow Satan .
54005016	If a woman who is a follower has any widows in her family , she should help them . This will keep the church from having that burden , and then the church can help widows who are really in need .
54005017	Church leaders who do their job well deserve to be paid twice as much , especially if they work hard at preaching and teaching .
54005018	It is just as the Scriptures say , “ Don't muzzle an ox when you are using it to grind grain . ” You also know the saying , “ Workers are worth their pay . ”
54005019	Don't listen to any charge against a church leader , unless at least two or three people bring the same charges .
54005020	But if any of the leaders should keep on sinning , they must be corrected in front of the whole group , as a warning to everyone else .
54005021	In the presence of God and Christ Jesus and their chosen angels , I order you to follow my instructions ! Be fair with everyone , and don't have any favorites .
54005022	Don't be too quick to accept people into the service of the Lord by placing your hands on them . Don't sin because others do , but stay close to God .
54005023	Stop drinking only water . Take a little wine to help your stomach trouble and the other illnesses you often have .
54005024	Some people get caught in their sins almost at once , even before the time of judgment . But other people's sins don't show up until later .
54005025	It is the same with good deeds . Some are easily seen , but none of them can be hidden .
54006001	If you are a slave , you should respect and honor your owner . This will keep people from saying bad things about God and about our teaching .
54006002	If any of you slaves have owners who are followers , you should show them respect . After all , they are also followers of Christ , and he loves them . So you should serve and help them the best you can . These are the things you must teach and tell the people to do .
54006003	Anyone who teaches something different disagrees with the correct and godly teaching of our Lord Jesus Christ .
54006004	Those people who disagree are proud of themselves , but they don't really know a thing . Their minds are sick , and they like to argue over words . They cause jealousy , disagreements , unkind words , evil suspicions ,
54006005	and nasty quarrels . They have wicked minds and have missed out on the truth . These people think religion is supposed to make you rich .
54006006	And religion does make your life rich , by making you content with what you have .
54006007	We didn't bring anything into this world , and we won't take anything with us when we leave .
54006008	So we should be satisfied just to have food and clothes .
54006009	People who want to be rich fall into all sorts of temptations and traps . They are caught by foolish and harmful desires that drag them down and destroy them .
54006010	The love of money causes all kinds of trouble . Some people want money so much they have given up their faith and caused themselves a lot of pain .
54006011	Timothy , you belong to God , so keep away from all these evil things . Try your best to please God and to be like him . Be faithful , loving , dependable , and gentle .
54006012	Fight a good fight for the faith and claim eternal life . God offered it to you when you clearly told about your faith , while so many people listened .
54006013	Now I ask you to make a promise . Make it in the presence of God , who gives life to all , and in the presence of Christ Jesus , who openly told Pontius Pilate about his faith .
54006014	Promise to obey completely and fully all that you have been told until our Lord Jesus Christ returns .
54006015	The glorious God is the only Ruler , the King of kings and Lord of lords . At the time that God has already decided , he will send Jesus Christ back again .
54006016	Only God lives forever ! And he lives in light that no one can come near . No human has ever seen God or ever can see him . God will be honored , and his power will last forever . Amen .
54006017	Warn the rich people of this world not to be proud or to trust in wealth that is easily lost . Tell them to have faith in God , who is rich and blesses us with everything we need to enjoy life .
54006018	Instruct them to do as many good deeds as they can and to help everyone . Remind the rich to be generous and share what they have .
54006019	This will lay a solid foundation for the future , so they will know what true life is like .
54006020	Timothy , guard what God has placed in your care ! Don't pay any attention to godless and stupid talk that sounds smart but really isn't .
54006021	Some people have even lost their faith by believing this talk . I pray that the Lord will be kind to all of you !
55001001	From Paul , an apostle of Christ Jesus . God himself chose me to be an apostle , and he gave me the promised life that Jesus Christ makes possible .
55001002	Timothy , you are like a dear child to me . I pray that God our Father and our Lord Christ Jesus will be kind and merciful to you and will bless you with peace !
55001003	Night and day I mention you in my prayers . I am always grateful for you , as I pray to the God my ancestors and I have served with a clear conscience .
55001004	I remember how you cried , and I want to see you , because this would make me truly happy .
55001005	I also remember the genuine faith of your mother Eunice . Your grandmother Lois had the same sort of faith , and I am sure you have it as well .
55001006	So I ask you to make full use of the gift God gave you when I placed my hands on you . Use it well .
55001007	God's Spirit doesn't make cowards out of us . The Spirit gives us power , love , and self-control .
55001008	Don't be ashamed to speak for our Lord . And don't be ashamed of me , just because I am in jail for serving him . Use the power that comes from God and join with me in suffering for telling the good news .
55001009	God saved us and chose us to be his holy people . We did nothing to deserve this , but God planned it because he is so kind . Even before time began God planned for Christ Jesus to show kindness to us .
55001010	Now Christ Jesus has come to offer us God's gift of undeserved grace . Christ our Savior defeated death and brought us the good news . It shines like a light and offers life that never ends .
55001011	My work is to be a preacher , an apostle , and a teacher .
55001012	This is why I am suffering now . But I am not ashamed ! I know the one I have faith in , and I am sure he can guard until the last day what he has trusted me with .
55001013	Now follow the example of the correct teaching I gave you , and let the faith and love of Christ Jesus be your model .
55001014	You have been trusted with a wonderful treasure . Guard it with the help of the Holy Spirit , who lives within us .
55001015	You know that everyone in Asia has turned against me , especially Phygelus and Hermogenes .
55001016	I pray that the Lord will be kind to the family of Onesiphorus . He often cheered me up and wasn't ashamed of me when I was put in jail .
55001017	Then after he arrived in Rome , he searched everywhere until he found me .
55001018	I pray that the Lord Jesus will ask God to show mercy to Onesiphorus on the day of judgment . You know how much he helped me in Ephesus .
55002001	Timothy , my child , you must let Christ Jesus make you strong by his gift of undeserved grace .
55002002	You have often heard me teach . Now I want you to tell these same things to followers who can be trusted to tell others .
55002003	As a good soldier of Christ Jesus you must endure your share of suffering .
55002004	Soldiers on duty don't work at outside jobs . They try only to please their commanding officer .
55002005	No one wins an athletic contest without obeying the rules .
55002006	And farmers who work hard are the first to eat what grows in their field .
55002007	If you keep in mind what I have told you , the Lord will help you understand completely .
55002008	Keep your mind on Jesus Christ ! He was from the family of David and was raised from death , just as my good news says .
55002009	And because of this message , I am locked up in jail and treated like a criminal . But God's good news isn't locked in jail ,
55002010	and so I am willing to put up with anything . Then God's special people will be saved and given eternal glory because they belong to Christ Jesus .
55002011	Here is a true message : “ If we died with Christ , we will live with him .
55002012	If we don't give up , we will rule with him . If we deny that we know him , he will deny that he knows us .
55002013	If we are not faithful , he will still be faithful . Christ cannot deny who he is . ”
55002014	Don't let anyone forget these things . And with God as your witness , you must warn them not to argue about words . These arguments don't help anyone . In fact , they ruin everyone who listens to them .
55002015	Do your best to win God's approval as a worker who doesn't need to be ashamed and who teaches only the true message .
55002016	Keep away from worthless and useless talk . It only leads people farther away from God .
55002017	That sort of talk is like a sore that won't heal . And Hymenaeus and Philetus have been talking this way
55002018	by teaching that the dead have already been raised to life . This is far from the truth , and it is destroying the faith of some people .
55002019	But the foundation God has laid is solid . On it is written , “ The Lord knows who his people are . So everyone who worships the Lord must turn away from evil . ”
55002020	In a large house some dishes are made of gold or silver , while others are made of wood or clay . Some of these are special , and others are not .
55002021	This is also how it is with people . The ones who stop doing evil and make themselves pure will become special . Their lives will be holy and pleasing to their Master , and they will be able to do all kinds of good deeds .
55002022	Run from temptations that capture young people . Always do the right thing . Be faithful , loving , and easy to get along with . Worship with people whose hearts are pure .
55002023	Stay away from stupid and senseless arguments . These only lead to trouble ,
55002024	and God's servants must not be troublemakers . They must be kind to everyone , and they must be good teachers and very patient .
55002025	Be humble when you correct people who oppose you . Maybe God will lead them to turn to him and learn the truth .
55002026	They have been trapped by the devil , and he makes them obey him , but God may help them escape .
55003001	You can be certain that in the last days there will be some very hard times .
55003002	People will love only themselves and money . They will be proud , stuck-up , rude , and disobedient to their parents . They will also be ungrateful , godless ,
55003003	heartless , and hateful . Their words will be cruel , and they will have no self-control or pity . These people will hate everything good .
55003004	They will be sneaky , reckless , and puffed up with pride . Instead of loving God , they will love pleasure .
55003005	Even though they will make a show of being religious , their religion won't be real . Don't have anything to do with such people .
55003006	Some men fool whole families , just to get power over those women who are slaves of sin and are controlled by all sorts of desires .
55003007	These women always want to learn something new , but they never can discover the truth .
55003008	Just as Jannes and Jambres opposed Moses , these people are enemies of the truth . Their minds are sick , and their faith isn't real .
55003009	But they won't get very far with their foolishness . Soon everyone will know the truth about them , just as Jannes and Jambres were found out .
55003010	Timothy , you know what I teach and how I live . You know what I want to do and what I believe . You have seen how patient and loving I am , and how in the past I put up with
55003011	trouble and suffering in the cities of Antioch , Iconium , and Lystra . Yet the Lord rescued me from all those terrible troubles .
55003012	In fact , anyone who belongs to Christ Jesus and wants to live right will have trouble from others .
55003013	But evil people who pretend to be what they are not will become worse than ever , as they fool others and are fooled themselves .
55003014	Keep on being faithful to what you were taught and to what you believed . After all , you know who taught you these things .
55003015	Since childhood , you have known the Holy Scriptures that are able to make you wise enough to have faith in Christ Jesus and be saved .
55003016	Everything in the Scriptures is God's Word . All of it is useful for teaching and helping people and for correcting them and showing them how to live .
55003017	The Scriptures train God's servants to do all kinds of good deeds .
55004001	When Christ Jesus comes as king , he will be the judge of everyone , whether they are living or dead . So with God and Christ as witnesses , I command you
55004002	to preach God's message . Do it willingly , even if it isn't the popular thing to do . You must correct people and point out their sins . But also cheer them up , and when you instruct them , always be patient .
55004003	The time is coming when people won't listen to good teaching . Instead , they will look for teachers who will please them by telling them only what they are itching to hear .
55004004	They will turn from the truth and eagerly listen to senseless stories .
55004005	But you must stay calm and be willing to suffer . You must work hard , telling the good news and to do your job well .
55004006	Now the time has come for me to die . My life is like a drink offering being poured out on the altar .
55004007	I have fought well . I have finished the race , and I have been faithful .
55004008	So a crown will be given to me for pleasing the Lord . He judges fairly , and on the day of judgment he will give a crown to me and to everyone else who wants him to appear with power .
55004009	Come to see me as soon as you can .
55004010	Demas loves the things of this world so much that he left me and went to Thessalonica . Crescens has gone to Galatia , and Titus has gone to Dalmatia .
55004011	Only Luke has stayed with me . Mark can be very helpful to me , so please find him and bring him with you .
55004012	I sent Tychicus to Ephesus .
55004013	When you come , bring the coat I left at Troas with Carpus . Don't forget to bring the scrolls , especially the ones made of leather .
55004014	Alexander , the metalworker , has hurt me in many ways . But the Lord will pay him back for what he has done .
55004015	Alexander opposes what we preach , so you had better watch out for him .
55004016	When I was first put on trial , no one helped me . In fact , everyone deserted me . I hope it won't be held against them .
55004017	But the Lord stood beside me . He gave me the strength to tell his full message , so that all Gentiles would hear it . And I was kept safe from hungry lions .
55004018	The Lord will always keep me from being harmed by evil , and he will bring me safely into his heavenly kingdom . Praise him forever and ever ! Amen .
55004019	Give my greetings to Priscilla and Aquila and to the family of Onesiphorus .
55004020	Erastus stayed at Corinth . Trophimus was sick when I left him at Miletus .
55004021	Do your best to come before winter . Eubulus , Pudens , Linus , and Claudia send you their greetings , and so do the rest of the Lord's followers .
55004022	I pray that the Lord will bless your life and will be kind to you .
56001001	From Paul , a servant of God and an apostle of Jesus Christ . I encourage God's own people to have more faith and to understand the truth about religion .
56001002	Then they will have the hope of eternal life God promised long ago . And God never tells a lie !
56001003	So , at the proper time , God our Savior gave this message and told me to announce what he had said .
56001004	Titus , because of our faith , you are like a son to me . I pray that God our Father and Christ Jesus our Savior will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
56001005	I left you in Crete to do what had been left undone and to appoint leaders for the churches in each town . As I told you ,
56001006	they must have a good reputation and be faithful in marriage . Their children must be followers of the Lord and not have a reputation for being wild and disobedient .
56001007	Church officials are in charge of God's work , and so they must also have a good reputation . They must not be bossy , quick-tempered , heavy drinkers , bullies , or dishonest in business .
56001008	Instead , they must be friendly to strangers and enjoy doing good things . They must also be sensible , fair , pure , and self-controlled .
56001009	They must stick to the true message they were taught , so their good teaching can help others and correct everyone who opposes it .
56001010	There are many who don't respect authority , and they fool others by talking nonsense . This is especially true of some Jewish followers .
56001011	But you must make them be quiet . They are after money , and they upset whole families by teaching what they should not .
56001012	It is like one of their own prophets once said , “ The people of Crete always tell lies . They are greedy and lazy like wild animals . ”
56001013	This surely is a true saying . And you should be hard on such people , so you can help them grow stronger in their faith .
56001014	Don't pay any attention to any of those senseless Jewish stories and human commands . These are made up by people who won't obey the truth .
56001015	Everything is pure for someone whose heart is pure . But nothing is pure for an unbeliever with a dirty mind . That person's mind and conscience are destroyed .
56001016	Such people claim to know God , but their actions prove they really don't . They are disgusting . They won't obey God , and they are too worthless to do anything good .
56002001	Titus , you must teach only what is correct .
56002002	Tell the older men to have self-control and to be serious and sensible . Their faith , love , and patience must never fail .
56002003	Tell the older women to behave as those who love the Lord should . They must not gossip about others or be slaves of wine . They must teach what is proper ,
56002004	so the younger women will be loving wives and mothers .
56002005	Each of the younger women must be sensible and kind , as well as a good homemaker , who puts her own husband first . Then no one can say insulting things about God's message .
56002006	Tell the young men to have self-control in everything .
56002007	Always set a good example for others . Be sincere and serious when you teach .
56002008	Use clean language that no one can criticize . Do this , and your enemies will be too ashamed to say anything against you .
56002009	Tell slaves always to please their owners by obeying them in everything . Slaves must not talk back to their owners
56002010	or steal from them . They must be completely honest and trustworthy . Then everyone will show great respect for what is taught about God our Savior .
56002011	God has shown us undeserved grace by coming to save all people .
56002012	He taught us to give up our wicked ways and our worldly desires and to live decent and honest lives in this world .
56002013	We are filled with hope , as we wait for the glorious return of our great God and Savior Jesus Christ .
56002014	He gave himself to rescue us from everything evil and to make our hearts pure . He wanted us to be his own people and to be eager to do right .
56002015	Teach these things , as you use your full authority to encourage and correct people . Make sure you earn everyone's respect .
56003001	Remind your people to obey the rulers and authorities and not to be rebellious . They must always be ready to do something helpful
56003002	and not say cruel things or argue . They should be gentle and kind to everyone .
56003003	We used to be stupid , disobedient , and foolish , as well as slaves of all sorts of desires and pleasures . We were evil and jealous . Everyone hated us , and we hated everyone .
56003004	God our Savior showed us how good and kind he is .
56003005	He saved us because of his mercy , and not because of any good things we have done . God washed us by the power of the Holy Spirit . He gave us new birth and a fresh beginning .
56003006	God sent Jesus Christ our Savior to give us his Spirit .
56003007	Jesus treated us much better than we deserve . He made us acceptable to God and gave us the hope of eternal life . These teachings are useful and helpful for everyone . I want you to insist that the people follow them , so that all who have faith in God will be sure to do good deeds .
56003009	But don't have anything to do with stupid arguments about ancestors . And stay away from disagreements and quarrels about the Law of Moses . Such arguments are useless and senseless .
56003010	Warn troublemakers once or twice . Then don't have anything else to do with them .
56003011	You know their minds are twisted , and their own sins show how guilty they are .
56003012	I plan to send Artemas or Tychicus to you . After he arrives , please try your best to meet me at Nicopolis . I have decided to spend the winter there .
56003013	When Zenas the lawyer and Apollos get ready to leave , help them as much as you can , so they won't have need of anything .
56003014	Our people should learn to spend their time doing something useful and worthwhile .
56003015	Greetings to you from everyone here . Greet all of our friends who share in our faith . I pray that the Lord will be kind to all of you !
57001001	From Paul , who is in jail for serving Christ Jesus , and from Timothy , who is like a brother because of our faith . Philemon , you work with us and are very dear to us . This letter is to you
57001002	and to the church that meets in your home . It is also to our dear friend Apphia and to Archippus , who serves the Lord as we do .
57001003	I pray that God our Father and our Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you and will bless you with peace !
57001004	Philemon , each time I mention you in my prayers , I thank God .
57001005	I hear about your faith in our Lord Jesus and about your love for all God's people .
57001006	As you share your faith with others , I pray they may come to know all the blessings Christ has given us .
57001007	My friend , your love has made me happy and has greatly encouraged me . It has also cheered the hearts of God's people .
57001008	Christ gives me the courage to tell you what to do .
57001009	But I would rather ask you to do it simply because of love . Yes , as someone in jail for Christ ,
57001010	I beg you to help Onesimus ! He is like a son to me because I led him to Christ here in jail .
57001011	Before this , he was useless to you , but now he is useful both to you and to me .
57001012	Sending Onesimus back to you makes me very sad .
57001013	I would like to keep him here with me , where he could take your place in helping me while I am here in prison for preaching the good news .
57001014	But I won't do anything unless you agree to it first . I want your act of kindness to come from your heart , and not be something you feel forced to do .
57001015	Perhaps Onesimus was taken from you for a little while so you could have him back for good ,
57001016	but not as a slave . Onesimus is much more than a slave . To me he is a dear friend , but to you he is even more , both as a person and as a follower of the Lord .
57001017	If you consider me a friend because of Christ , then welcome Onesimus as you would welcome me .
57001018	If he has cheated you or owes you anything , charge it to my account .
57001019	With my own hand I write : I , PAUL , WILL PAY YOU BACK . But don't forget you owe me your life .
57001020	My dear friend and follower of Christ our Lord , please cheer me up by doing this for me .
57001021	I am sure you will do all I have asked , and even more .
57001022	Please get a room ready for me . I hope your prayers will be answered , and I can visit you .
57001023	Epaphras is also here in jail for being a follower of Christ Jesus . He sends his greetings ,
57001024	and so do Mark , Aristarchus , Demas , and Luke , who work together with me .
57001025	I pray that the Lord Jesus Christ will be kind to you !
58001001	Long ago in many ways and at many times God's prophets spoke his message to our ancestors .
58001002	But now at last , God sent his Son to bring his message to us . God created the universe by his Son , and everything will someday belong to the Son .
58001003	God's Son has all the brightness of God's own glory and is like him in every way . By his own mighty word , he holds the universe together . After the Son had washed away our sins , he sat down at the right side of the glorious God in heaven .
58001004	He had become much greater than the angels , and the name he was given is far greater than any of theirs .
58001005	God has never said to any of the angels , “ You are my Son , because today I have become your Father ! ” Neither has God said to any of them , “ I will be his Father , and he will be my Son ! ”
58001006	When God brings his first-born Son into the world , he commands all of his angels to worship him .
58001007	And when God speaks about the angels , he says , “ I change my angels into wind and my servants into flaming fire . ”
58001008	But God says about his Son , “ You are God , and you will rule as King forever ! Your royal power brings about justice .
58001009	You loved justice and hated evil , and so I , your God , have chosen you . I appointed you and made you happier than any of your friends . ”
58001010	The Scriptures also say , “ In the beginning , Lord , you were the one who laid the foundation of the earth and created the heavens .
58001011	They will all disappear and wear out like clothes , but you will last forever .
58001012	You will roll them up like a robe and change them like a garment . But you are always the same , and you will live forever . ”
58001013	God never said to any of the angels , “ Sit at my right side until I make your enemies into a footstool for you ! ”
58001014	Angels are merely spirits sent to serve people who are going to be saved .
58002001	We must give our full attention to what we were told , so we won't drift away .
58002002	The message spoken by angels proved to be true , and all who disobeyed or rejected it were punished as they deserved .
58002003	So if we refuse this great way of being saved , how can we hope to escape ? The Lord himself was the first to tell about it , and people who heard the message proved to us that it was true .
58002004	God himself showed that his message was true by working all kinds of powerful miracles and wonders . He also gave his Holy Spirit to anyone he chose to .
58002005	We know that God did not put the future world under the power of angels .
58002006	Somewhere in the Scriptures someone says to God , “ What makes you care about us humans ? Why are you concerned for weaklings such as we ?
58002007	You made us lower than the angels for a while . Yet you have crowned us with glory and honor .
58002008	And you have put everything under our power ! ” God has put everything under our power and has not left anything out of our power . But we still don't see it all under our control .
58002009	What we do see is Jesus , who for a little while was made lower than the angels . Because of God's gift of undeserved grace , Jesus died for everyone . And now that Jesus has suffered and died , he is crowned with glory and honor !
58002010	Everything belongs to God , and all things were created by his power . So God did the right thing when he made Jesus perfect by suffering , as Jesus led many of God's children to be saved and to share in his glory .
58002011	Jesus and the people he makes holy all belong to the same family . This is why he isn't ashamed to call them his brothers and sisters .
58002012	He even said to God , “ I will tell them your name and sing your praises when they come together to worship . ”
58002013	He also said , “ I will trust God . ” Then he said , “ Here I am with the children God has given me . ”
58002014	We are people of flesh and blood . This is why Jesus became one of us . He died to destroy the devil , who had power over death .
58002015	But he also died to rescue all of us who live each day in fear of dying .
58002016	Jesus clearly did not come to help angels , but he did come to help Abraham's descendants .
58002017	He had to be one of us , so he could serve God as our merciful and faithful high priest and sacrifice himself for the forgiveness of our sins .
58002018	And now that Jesus has suffered and was tempted , he can help anyone else who is tempted .
58003001	My friends , God has chosen you to be his holy people . So think about Jesus , the one we call our apostle and high priest !
58003002	Jesus was faithful to God , who appointed him , just as Moses was faithful in serving all God's people .
58003003	But Jesus deserves more honor than Moses , just as the builder of a house deserves more honor than the house .
58003004	Of course , every house is built by someone , and God is really the one who built everything .
58003005	Moses was a faithful servant and told God's people what would be said in the future .
58003006	But Christ is the Son in charge of God's people . And we are those people , if we keep on being brave and don't lose hope .
58003007	It is just as the Holy Spirit says , “ If you hear God's voice today ,
58003008	don't be stubborn ! Don't rebel like those people who were tested in the desert .
58003009	For forty years your ancestors tested God and saw the things he did .
58003010	“ Then God got tired of them and said , ‘ You people never show good sense , and you don't understand what I want you to do . ’
58003011	God became angry and told the people , ‘ You will never enter my place of rest ! ’ ”
58003012	My friends , watch out ! Don't let evil thoughts or doubts make any of you turn from the living God .
58003013	You must encourage one another each day . And you must keep on while there is still a time that can be called “ today . ” If you don't , then sin may fool some of you and make you stubborn .
58003014	We were sure about Christ when we first became his people . So let's hold tightly to our faith until the end .
58003015	The Scriptures say , “ If you hear his voice today , don't be stubborn like those who rebelled . ”
58003016	Who were those people that heard God's voice and rebelled ? Weren't they the same ones that came out of Egypt with Moses ?
58003017	Who were the people that made God angry for 40 years ? Weren't they the ones that sinned and died in the desert ?
58003018	And who did God say would never enter his place of rest ? Weren't they the ones that disobeyed him ?
58003019	We see that those people did not enter the place of rest because they did not have faith .
58004001	The promise to enter the place of rest is still good , and we must take care that none of you miss out .
58004002	We have heard the message , just as they did . But they failed to believe what they heard , and the message did not do them any good .
58004003	Only people who have faith will enter the place of rest . It is just as the Scriptures say , “ God became angry and told the people , ‘ You will never enter my place of rest ! ’ ” God said this , even though everything has been ready from the time of creation .
58004004	In fact , somewhere the Scriptures say that by the seventh day , God had finished his work , and so he rested .
58004005	We also read that he later said , “ You people will never enter my place of rest ! ”
58004006	This means that the promise to enter is still good , because those who first heard about it disobeyed and did not enter .
58004007	Much later God told David to make the promise again , just as I have already said , “ If you hear his voice today , don't be stubborn ! ”
58004008	If Joshua had really given the people rest , there would not be any need for God to talk about another day of rest .
58004009	But God has promised us a Sabbath when we will rest , even though it has not yet come .
58004010	On that day God's people will rest from their work , just as God rested from his work .
58004011	We should do our best to enter the place of rest , so none of us will disobey and miss going there , as they did .
58004012	God's word is alive and powerful ! It is sharper than any double-edged sword . His word can cut through our spirits and souls and through our joints and marrow , until it discovers the desires and thoughts of our hearts .
58004013	Nothing is hidden from God ! He sees through everything , and we will have to tell him the truth .
58004014	We have a great high priest , who has gone into heaven , and he is Jesus the Son of God . This is why we must hold on to what we have said about him .
58004015	Jesus understands every weakness of ours , because he was tempted in every way that we are . But he did not sin !
58004016	So whenever we are in need , we should come bravely before the throne of our merciful God . There we will be treated with undeserved grace , and we will find help .
58005001	Every high priest is appointed to help others by offering gifts and sacrifices to God because of their sins .
58005002	A high priest has weaknesses of his own , and he feels sorry for foolish and sinful people .
58005003	This is why he must offer sacrifices for his own sins and for the sins of others .
58005004	But no one can have the honor of being a high priest simply by wanting to be one . Only God can choose a priest , and God is the one who chose Aaron .
58005005	This is how it was with Christ . He became a high priest , but not just because he wanted the honor of being one . It was God who told him , “ You are my Son , because today I have become your Father ! ” “ You are a priest forever just like Melchizedek . ”
58005007	God had the power to save Jesus from death . And while Jesus was on earth , he begged God with loud crying and tears to save him . He truly worshiped God , and God listened to his prayers .
58005008	Jesus is God's own Son , but still he had to suffer before he could learn what it really means to obey God .
58005009	Suffering made Jesus perfect , and now he can save forever all who obey him .
58005010	This is because God chose him to be a high priest like Melchizedek .
58005011	Much more could be said about this subject . But it is hard to explain , and all of you are slow to understand .
58005012	By now you should have been teachers , but once again you need to be taught the simplest things about what God has said . You need milk instead of solid food .
58005013	People who live on milk are like babies who don't really know what is right .
58005014	Solid food is for mature people who have been trained to know right from wrong .
58006001	We must try to become mature and start thinking about more than just the basic things we were taught about Christ . We shouldn't need to keep talking about why we ought to turn from deeds that bring death and why we ought to have faith in God .
58006002	And we shouldn't need to keep teaching about baptisms or about the laying on of hands or about people being raised from death and the future judgment .
58006003	Let's grow up , if God is willing .
58006007	A field is useful to farmers , if there is enough rain to make good crops grow . In fact , God will bless such a field .
58006008	But land that produces only thornbushes is worthless . It is likely to fall under God's curse , and in the end it will be set on fire .
58006009	My friends , we are talking this way . But we are sure that you are doing those really good things people do when they are being saved .
58006010	God is always fair . He will remember how you helped his people in the past and how you are still helping them . You belong to God , and he won't forget the love you have shown his people .
58006011	We wish each of you would always be eager to show how strong and lasting your hope really is .
58006012	Then you would never be lazy . You would be following the example of those who had faith and were patient until God kept his promise to them .
58006013	No one is greater than God . So he made a promise in his own name when he said to Abraham ,
58006014	“ I , the Lord , will bless you with many descendants ! ”
58006015	Then after Abraham had been very patient , he was given what God had promised .
58006016	When anyone wants to settle an argument , they make a vow by using the name of someone or something greater than themselves .
58006017	So when God wanted to prove for certain his promise to his people could not be broken , he made a vow .
58006018	God cannot tell lies ! And so his promises and vows are two things that can never be changed . We have run to God for safety . Now his promises should greatly encourage us to take hold of the hope that is right in front of us .
58006019	This hope is like a firm and steady anchor for our souls . In fact , hope reaches behind the curtain and into the most holy place .
58006020	Jesus has gone there ahead of us , and he is our high priest forever , just like Melchizedek .
58007001	Melchizedek was both king of Salem and priest of God Most High . He was the one who went out and gave Abraham his blessing , when Abraham returned from killing the kings .
58007002	Then Abraham gave him a tenth of everything he had . The meaning of the name Melchizedek is “ King of Justice . ” But since Salem means “ peace , ” he is also “ King of Peace . ”
58007003	We are not told he had a father or mother or ancestors or beginning or end . He is like the Son of God and will be a priest forever .
58007004	Notice how great Melchizedek was ! Our famous ancestor Abraham gave him a tenth of what he had taken from his enemies .
58007005	The Law teaches that even Abraham's descendants must give a tenth of what they possess . And they are to give this to their own relatives , who are the descendants of Levi and are priests .
58007006	Although Melchizedek wasn't a descendant of Levi , Abraham gave him a tenth of what he had . Then Melchizedek blessed Abraham , who had been given God's promise .
58007007	Everyone agrees a person who gives a blessing is greater than the one who receives the blessing .
58007008	Priests are given a tenth of what people earn . But all priests die , except Melchizedek , and the Scriptures teach that he is alive .
58007009	Levi's descendants are now the ones who receive a tenth from people . We could even say that when Abraham gave Melchizedek a tenth , Levi also gave him a tenth .
58007010	This is because Levi was born later into the family of Abraham , who gave a tenth to Melchizedek .
58007011	Even though the Law of Moses says the priests must be descendants of Levi , those priests cannot make anyone perfect . So there needs to be a priest like Melchizedek , rather than one from the priestly family of Aaron .
58007012	And when the rules for selecting a priest are changed , the Law must also be changed .
58007013	The person we are talking about is our Lord , who came from a tribe that had never had anyone to serve as a priest at the altar .
58007014	Everyone knows he came from the tribe of Judah , and Moses never said priests would come from that tribe .
58007015	All of this becomes clearer , when someone who is like Melchizedek is appointed to be a priest .
58007016	That person wasn't appointed because of his ancestors , but because his life can never end .
58007017	The Scriptures say about him , “ You are a priest forever , just like Melchizedek . ”
58007022	This means that Jesus guarantees us a better agreement with God .
58007023	There have been a lot of other priests , and all of them have died .
58007024	But Jesus will never die , and so he will be a priest forever !
58007025	He is forever able to save the people he leads to God , because he always lives to speak to God for them .
58007026	Jesus is the high priest we need . He is holy and innocent and faultless , and not at all like us sinners . Jesus is honored above all beings in heaven ,
58007027	and he is better than any other high priest . Jesus doesn't need to offer sacrifices each day for his own sins and then for the sins of the people . He offered a sacrifice once for all , when he gave himself .
58007028	The Law appoints priests who have weaknesses . But God's promise , which came later than the Law , appoints his Son . And he is the perfect high priest forever .
58008001	What I mean is we have a high priest who sits at the right side of God's great throne in heaven .
58008002	He also serves as the priest in the most holy place inside the real tent there in heaven . This tent of worship was set up by the Lord , not by humans .
58008003	Since all priests must offer gifts and sacrifices , Christ also needed to have something to offer .
58008004	If he were here on earth , he would not be a priest at all , because here the Law appoints other priests to offer sacrifices .
58008005	But the tent where they serve is just a copy and a shadow of the real one in heaven . Before Moses made the tent , he was told , “ Be sure to make it exactly like the pattern you were shown on the mountain ! ”
58008006	Now Christ has been appointed to serve as a priest in a much better way , and he has given us much assurance of a better agreement .
58008007	If the first agreement with God had been all right , there would not have been any need for another one .
58008008	But the Lord found fault with it and said , “ I tell you the time will come , when I will make a new agreement with the people of Israel and the people of Judah .
58008009	It won't be like the agreement that I made with their ancestors , when I took them by the hand and led them out of Egypt . They broke their agreement with me , and I stopped caring about them !
58008010	“ But now I tell the people of Israel this is my new agreement : ‘ The time will come when I , the Lord , will write my laws on their minds and hearts . I will be their God , and they will be my people .
58008011	Not one of them will have to teach another to know me , their Lord . ’ “ All of them will know me , no matter who they are .
58008012	I will treat them with kindness , even though they are wicked . I will forget their sins . ”
58008013	When the Lord talks about a new agreement , he means that the first one is out of date . And anything that is old and useless will soon disappear .
58009001	The first promise included rules for worship and a tent for worship here on earth .
58009002	The first part of the tent was called the holy place , and a lampstand , a table , and the sacred loaves of bread were kept there .
58009003	Behind the curtain was the most holy place .
58009004	The gold altar for burning incense was in this holy place . The gold-covered sacred chest was also there , and inside it were three things . First , there was a gold jar filled with manna . Then there was Aaron's walking stick that sprouted . Finally , there were the flat stones with the Ten Commandments written on them .
58009005	On top of the chest were the glorious creatures with wings opened out above the place of mercy . Now isn't the time to go into detail about these things .
58009006	But this is how everything was when the priests went each day into the first part of the tent to do their duties .
58009007	However , only the high priest could go into the second part of the tent , and he went in only once a year . Each time he carried blood to offer for his sins and for any sins that the people had committed without meaning to .
58009008	All of this is the Holy Spirit's way of saying no one could enter the most holy place while the tent was still the place of worship .
58009009	This also has a meaning for today . It shows we cannot make our consciences clear by offering gifts and sacrifices .
58009010	These rules are merely about such things as eating and drinking and ceremonies for washing ourselves . And rules about physical things will last only until the time comes to change them for something better .
58009011	Christ came as the high priest of the good things that are now here . He also went into a much better tent that wasn't made by humans and that doesn't belong to this world .
58009012	Then Christ went once for all into the most holy place and freed us from sin forever . He did this by offering his own blood instead of the blood of goats and bulls .
58009013	According to the Law of Moses , those people who become unclean are not fit to worship God . Yet they will be considered clean , if they are sprinkled with the blood of goats and bulls and with the ashes of a sacrificed calf .
58009014	But Christ was sinless , and he offered himself as an eternal and spiritual sacrifice to God . This is why his blood is much more powerful and makes our consciences clear . Now we can serve the living God and no longer do things that lead to death .
58009015	Christ died to rescue those who had sinned and broken the old agreement . Now he brings his chosen ones a new agreement with its guarantee of God's eternal blessings !
58009016	In fact , making an agreement of this kind is like writing a will . This is because the one who makes the will must die before it is of any use .
58009017	In other words , a will doesn't go into effect as long as the one who made it is still alive .
58009018	Blood was also used to put the first agreement into effect .
58009019	Moses told the people all the Law said they must do . Then he used red wool and a hyssop plant to sprinkle the people and the book of the Law with the blood of bulls and goats and with water .
58009020	He told the people , “ With this blood God makes his agreement with you . ”
58009021	Moses also sprinkled blood on the tent and on everything else used in worship .
58009022	The Law says that almost everything must be sprinkled with blood , and no sins can be forgiven unless blood is offered .
58009023	These things are only copies of what is in heaven , and so they had to be made holy by these ceremonies . But the real things in heaven must be made holy by something better .
58009024	This is why Christ did not go into a tent made by humans and was only a copy of the real one . Instead , he went into heaven and is now there with God to help us .
58009025	Christ did not have to offer himself many times . He wasn't like a high priest who goes into the most holy place each year to offer the blood of an animal .
58009026	If he had offered himself every year , he would have suffered many times since the creation of the world . But instead , near the end of time he offered himself once and for all , so he could be a sacrifice that does away with sin .
58009027	We die only once , and then we are judged .
58009028	So Christ died only once to take away the sins of many people . But when he comes again , it will not be to take away sin . He will come to save everyone who is waiting for him .
58010001	The Law of Moses is like a shadow of the good things to come . This shadow isn't the good things themselves , because it cannot free people from sin by the sacrifices offered year after year .
58010002	If there were worshipers who already have their sins washed away and their consciences made clear , there would not be any need to go on offering sacrifices .
58010005	When Christ came into the world , he said to God , “ Sacrifices and offerings are not what you want , but you have given me my body .
58010006	No , you are not pleased with animal sacrifices and offerings for sin . ”
58010007	Then Christ said , “ And so , my God , I have come to do what you want , as the Scriptures say . ”
58010008	The Law teaches that offerings and sacrifices must be made because of sin . But why did Christ mention these things and say that God did not want them ?
58010009	Well , it was to do away with offerings and sacrifices and to replace them . This is what he meant by saying to God , “ I have come to do what you want . ”
58010010	So we are made holy because Christ obeyed God and offered himself once for all .
58010011	The priests do their work each day , and they keep on offering sacrifices that can never take away sins .
58010012	But Christ offered himself as a sacrifice that is good forever . Now he is sitting at God's right side ,
58010013	and he will stay there until his enemies are put under his power .
58010014	By his one sacrifice he has forever set free from sin the people he brings to God .
58010015	The Holy Spirit also speaks of this by telling us that the Lord said ,
58010016	“ When the time comes , I will make an agreement with them . I will write my laws on their minds and hearts .
58010017	Then I will forget about their sins and no longer remember their evil deeds . ”
58010018	When sins are forgiven , there is no more need to offer sacrifices .
58010019	My friends , the blood of Jesus gives us courage to enter the most holy place
58010020	by a new way that leads to life ! And this way takes us through the curtain that is Christ himself .
58010021	We have a great high priest who is in charge of God's house .
58010022	So let's come near God with pure hearts and a confidence that comes from having faith . Let's keep our hearts pure , our consciences free from evil , and our bodies washed with clean water .
58010023	We must hold tightly to the hope we say is ours . After all , we can trust the one who made the agreement with us .
58010024	We should keep on encouraging each other to be thoughtful and to do helpful things .
58010025	Some people have given up the habit of meeting for worship , but we must not do that . We should keep on encouraging each other , especially since you know that the day of the Lord's coming is getting closer .
58010026	No sacrifices can be made for people who decide to sin after they find out about the truth .
58010027	They are God's enemies , and all they can look forward to is a terrible judgment and a furious fire .
58010028	If two or more witnesses accused someone of breaking the Law of Moses , that person could be put to death .
58010029	But it is much worse to dishonor God's Son and to disgrace the blood of the promise that made us holy . And it is just as bad to insult the Holy Spirit , who shows us mercy .
58010030	We know that God has said he will punish and take revenge . We also know that the Scriptures say the Lord will judge his people .
58010031	It is a terrible thing to fall into the hands of the living God !
58010032	Don't forget all the hard times you went through when you first received the light .
58010033	Sometimes you were abused and mistreated in public , and at other times you shared in the sufferings of others .
58010034	You were kind to people in jail . And you gladly let your possessions be taken away , because you knew you had something better , something that would last forever .
58010035	Keep on being brave ! It will bring you great rewards .
58010036	Learn to be patient , so you will please God and be given what he has promised .
58010037	As the Scriptures say , “ God is coming soon ! It won't be very long .
58010038	The people God accepts will live because of their faith . But he isn't pleased with anyone who turns back . ”
58011001	Faith makes us sure of what we hope for and gives us proof of what we cannot see .
58011002	It was their faith that made our ancestors pleasing to God .
58011003	Because of our faith , we know that the world was made at God's command . We also know that what can be seen was made out of what cannot be seen .
58011004	Because Abel had faith , he offered God a better sacrifice than Cain did . God was pleased with him and his gift , and even though Abel is now dead , his faith still speaks for him .
58011005	Enoch had faith and did not die . He pleased God , and God took him up to heaven . This is why his body was never found .
58011006	But without faith no one can please God . We must believe that God is real and rewards everyone who searches for him .
58011007	Because Noah had faith , he was warned about something that had not yet happened . He obeyed and built a boat that saved him and his family . In this way the people of the world were judged , and Noah was given the blessings that come to everyone who pleases God .
58011008	Abraham had faith and obeyed God . He was told to go to the land that God had said would be his , and he left for a country he had never seen .
58011009	Because Abraham had faith , he lived as a stranger in the promised land . He lived there in a tent , and so did Isaac and Jacob , who were later given the same promise .
58011010	Abraham did this , because he was waiting for the eternal city God had planned and built .
58011011	Even when Sarah was too old to have children , she had faith that God would do what he had promised , and she had a son .
58011012	Her husband Abraham was almost dead , but he became the ancestor of many people . In fact , there are as many of them as there are stars in the sky or grains of sand along the seashore .
58011013	Every one of those people died . But they still had faith , even though they had not received what they had been promised . They were glad just to see these things from far away , and they agreed that they were only strangers and foreigners on this earth .
58011014	When people talk this way , it is clear they are looking for a place to call their own .
58011015	If they had been talking about the land where they had once lived , they could have gone back at any time .
58011016	But they were looking forward to a better home in heaven . This is why God wasn't ashamed for them to call him their God . He even built a city for them .
58011019	because he was sure that God could raise people to life . This was just like getting Isaac back from death .
58011020	Isaac had faith , and he promised blessings to Jacob and Esau .
58011021	Later , when Jacob was about to die , he leaned on his walking stick and worshiped . Then because of his faith he blessed each of Joseph's sons .
58011022	And right before Joseph died , he had faith that God would lead the people of Israel out of Egypt . So he told them to take his bones with them .
58011023	Because Moses' parents had faith , they kept him hidden until he was three months old . They saw that he was a beautiful child , and they were not afraid to disobey the king's orders .
58011024	Then after Moses grew up , his faith made him refuse to be called the king's grandson .
58011025	He chose to be mistreated with God's people instead of having the good time that sin could bring for a little while .
58011026	Moses knew that the treasures of Egypt were not as wonderful as what he would receive from suffering for the Messiah , and he looked forward to his reward .
58011027	Because of his faith , Moses left Egypt . Moses had seen the invisible God and wasn't afraid of the king's anger .
58011028	His faith also made him celebrate Passover . He sprinkled the blood of animals on the doorposts , so that the first-born sons of the people of Israel would not be killed by the destroying angel .
58011029	Because of their faith , the people walked through the Red Sea on dry land . But when the Egyptians tried to do it , they were drowned .
58011030	God's people had faith , and when they had walked around the city of Jericho for seven days , its walls fell down .
58011031	Rahab had been a prostitute , but she had faith and welcomed the spies . So she wasn't killed with the people who disobeyed .
58011032	What else can I say ? There isn't enough time to tell about Gideon , Barak , Samson , Jephthah , David , Samuel , and the prophets .
58011033	Their faith helped them conquer kingdoms , and because they did right , God made promises to them . They closed the jaws of lions
58011034	and put out raging fires and escaped from the swords of their enemies . Although they were weak , they were given the strength and power to chase foreign armies away .
58011035	Some women received their loved ones back from death . Many of these people were tortured , but they refused to be released . They were sure they would get a better reward when the dead are raised to life .
58011036	Others were made fun of and beaten with whips , and some were chained in jail .
58011037	Still others were stoned to death or sawed in two or killed with swords . Some had nothing but sheep skins or goat skins to wear . They were poor , mistreated , and tortured .
58011038	The world did not deserve these good people , who had to wander in deserts and on mountains and had to live in caves and holes in the ground .
58011039	All of them pleased God because of their faith ! But still they died without being given what had been promised .
58011040	This was because God had something better in store for us . And he did not want them to reach the goal of their faith without us .
58012001	Such a large crowd of witnesses is all around us ! So we must get rid of everything that slows us down , especially the sin that just won't let go . And we must be determined to run the race that is ahead of us .
58012002	We must keep our eyes on Jesus , who leads us and makes our faith complete . He endured the shame of being nailed to a cross , because he knew later on he would be glad he did . Now he is seated at the right side of God's throne !
58012003	So keep your mind on Jesus , who put up with many insults from sinners . Then you won't get discouraged and give up .
58012004	None of you have yet been hurt in your battle against sin .
58012005	But you have forgotten that the Scriptures say to God's children , “ When the Lord punishes you , don't make light of it , and when he corrects you , don't be discouraged .
58012006	The Lord corrects the people he loves and disciplines those he calls his own . ”
58012007	Be patient when you are being corrected ! This is how God treats his children . Don't all parents correct their children ?
58012008	God corrects all his children , and if he doesn't correct you , then you don't really belong to him .
58012009	Our earthly fathers correct us , and we still respect them . Isn't it even better to be given true life by letting our spiritual Father correct us ?
58012010	Our human fathers correct us for a short time , and they do it as they think best . But God corrects us for our own good , because he wants us to be holy , as he is .
58012011	It is never fun to be corrected . In fact , at the time it is always painful . But if we learn to obey by being corrected , we will do right and live at peace .
58012012	Now stand up straight ! Stop your knees from shaking
58012013	and walk a straight path . Then lame people will be healed , instead of getting worse .
58012014	Try to live at peace with everyone ! Live a clean life . If you don't , you will never see the Lord .
58012015	Make sure no one misses out on God's wonderful kindness . Don't let anyone become bitter and cause trouble for the rest of you .
58012016	Watch out for immoral and ungodly people like Esau , who sold his future blessing for only one meal .
58012017	You know how he later wanted it back . But there was nothing he could do to change things , even though he begged his father and cried .
58012018	You have not come to a place like Mount Sinai that can be seen and touched . There is no flaming fire or dark cloud or storm
58012019	or trumpet sound . The people of Israel heard a voice speak . But they begged it to stop ,
58012020	because they could not obey its commands . They were even told to kill any animal that touched the mountain .
58012021	The sight was so frightening that Moses said he shook with fear .
58012022	You have now come to Mount Zion and to the heavenly Jerusalem . This is the city of the living God , where thousands and thousands of angels have come to celebrate .
58012023	Here you will find all of God's dearest children , whose names are written in heaven . And you will find God himself , who judges everyone . Here also are the spirits of those good people who have been made perfect .
58012024	And Jesus is here ! He is the one who makes God's new agreement with us , and his sprinkled blood says much better things than the blood of Abel .
58012025	Make sure you obey the one who speaks to you . The people did not escape , when they refused to obey the one who spoke to them at Mount Sinai . Do you think you can possibly escape , if you refuse to obey the one who speaks to you from heaven ?
58012026	When God spoke the first time , his voice shook only the earth . This time he has promised to shake the earth once again , and heaven too .
58012027	The words “ once again ” mean that these created things will someday be shaken and removed . Then what cannot be shaken will last .
58012028	We should be grateful we were given a kingdom that cannot be shaken . And in this kingdom we please God by worshiping him and by showing him great honor and respect .
58012029	Our God is like a destructive fire !
58013001	Keep being concerned about each other as the Lord's followers should .
58013002	Be sure to welcome strangers into your home . By doing this , some people have welcomed angels as guests , without even knowing it .
58013003	Remember the Lord's people who are in jail and be concerned for them . Don't forget those who are suffering , but imagine you are there with them .
58013004	Have respect for marriage . Always be faithful to your partner , because God will punish anyone who is immoral or unfaithful in marriage .
58013005	Don't fall in love with money . Be satisfied with what you have . The Lord has promised that he will not leave us or desert us .
58013006	This should make you feel like saying , “ The Lord helps me ! Why should I be afraid of what people can do to me ? ”
58013007	Don't forget about your leaders who taught you God's message . Remember what kind of lives they lived and try to have faith like theirs .
58013008	Jesus Christ never changes ! He is the same yesterday , today , and forever .
58013009	Don't be fooled by any kind of strange teachings . It is better to receive strength from God's gift of undeserved grace than to depend on certain foods . After all , these foods don't really help the people who eat them .
58013010	But we have an altar where even the priests who serve in the place of worship have no right to eat .
58013011	After the high priest offers the blood of animals as a sin offering , the bodies of those animals are burned outside the camp .
58013012	Jesus himself suffered outside the city gate , so his blood would make people holy .
58013013	This is why we should go outside the camp to Jesus and share in his disgrace .
58013014	On this earth we don't have a city that lasts forever , but we are waiting for such a city .
58013015	Our sacrifice is to keep offering praise to God in the name of Jesus .
58013016	But don't forget to help others and to share your possessions with them . This too is like offering a sacrifice that pleases God .
58013017	Obey your leaders and do what they say . They are watching over you , and they must answer to God . So don't make them sad as they do their work . Make them happy . Otherwise , they won't be able to help you at all .
58013018	Pray for us . Our consciences are clear , and we always try to live right .
58013019	I especially want you to pray that I can visit you again soon .
58013020	God gives peace , and he raised our Lord Jesus Christ from death . Now Jesus is like a Great Shepherd whose blood was used to make God's eternal agreement with his flock .
58013021	I pray God will make you ready to obey him and that you will always be eager to do right . May Jesus help you do what pleases God . To Jesus Christ be glory forever and ever ! Amen .
58013022	My friends , I have written only a short letter to encourage you , and I beg you to pay close attention to what I have said .
58013023	By now you surely must know that our friend Timothy is out of jail . If he gets here in time , I will bring him with me when I come to visit you .
58013024	Please give my greetings to your leaders and to the rest of the Lord's people . His followers from Italy send you their greetings .
58013025	I pray that God will be kind to all of you !
59001001	From James , a servant of God and of our Lord Jesus Christ . Greetings to the twelve tribes scattered all over the world .
59001002	My friends , be glad , even if you have a lot of trouble .
59001003	You know you learn to endure by having your faith tested .
59001004	But you must learn to endure everything , so you will be completely mature and not lacking in anything .
59001005	If any of you need wisdom , you should ask God , and it will be given to you . God is generous and won't correct you for asking .
59001006	But when you ask for something , you must have faith and not doubt . Anyone who doubts is like an ocean wave tossed around in a storm .
59001009	Any of God's people who are poor should be glad he thinks so highly of them .
59001010	But any who are rich should be glad when God makes them humble . Rich people will disappear like wild flowers
59001011	scorched by the burning heat of the sun . The flowers lose their blossoms , and their beauty is destroyed . This is how the rich will disappear , as they go about their business .
59001012	God will bless you , if you don't give up when your faith is being tested . He will reward you with a glorious life , just as he rewards everyone who loves him .
59001013	Don't blame God when you are tempted ! God cannot be tempted by evil , and he doesn't use evil to tempt others .
59001014	We are tempted by our own desires that drag us off and trap us .
59001015	Our desires make us sin , and when sin is finished with us , it leaves us dead .
59001016	Don't be fooled , my dear friends .
59001017	Every good and perfect gift comes down from the Father who created all the lights in the heavens . He is always the same and never makes dark shadows by changing .
59001018	He wanted us to be his own special people , and so he sent the true message to give us new birth .
59001019	My dear friends , you should be quick to listen and slow to speak or to get angry .
59001020	If you are angry , you cannot do any of the good things God wants done .
59001021	You must stop doing anything immoral or evil . Instead be humble and accept the message planted in you to save you .
59001022	Obey God's message ! Don't fool yourselves by just listening to it .
59001023	If you hear the message and don't obey it , you are like people who stare at themselves in a mirror
59001024	and forget what they look like as soon as they leave .
59001025	But you must never stop looking at the perfect law that sets you free . God will bless you in everything you do , if you listen and obey , and don't just hear and forget .
59001026	If you think you are being religious , but can't control your tongue , you are fooling yourself , and your religion is useless .
59001027	Religion that pleases God the Father must be pure and spotless . You must help needy orphans and widows and not let this world make you evil .
