59002001	My friends , if you have faith in our glorious Lord Jesus Christ , you won't treat some people better than others .
59002002	Suppose a rich person wearing fancy clothes and a gold ring comes to one of your meetings . And suppose a poor person dressed in worn-out clothes also comes .
59002003	You must not give the best seat to the one in fancy clothes and tell the one who is poor to stand at the side or sit on the floor .
59002004	This is the same as saying that some people are better than others , and you would be acting like a crooked judge .
59002005	My dear friends , pay attention . God has given a lot of faith to the poor people in this world . God has also promised them a share in his kingdom that he will give to everyone who loves him .
59002006	You mistreat the poor . But isn't it the rich who boss you around and drag you off to court ?
59002007	Aren't they the ones who make fun of your Lord ?
59002008	You will do all right , if you obey the most important law in the Scriptures . It is the law that commands us to love others as much as we love ourselves .
59002009	But if you treat some people better than others , you have done wrong , and the Scriptures teach that you have sinned .
59002010	If you obey every law except one , you are still guilty of breaking them all .
59002011	The same God who told us to be faithful in marriage also told us not to murder . So even if you are faithful in marriage , but murder someone , you still have broken God's Law .
59002012	Speak and act like people who will be judged by the law that sets us free .
59002013	Do this , because on the day of judgment there will be no pity for those who have not had pity on others . But even in judgment , God is merciful !
59002014	My friends , what good is it to say you have faith , when you don't do anything to show you really do have faith ? Can this kind of faith save you ?
59002015	If you know someone who doesn't have any clothes or food ,
59002016	you shouldn't just say , “ I hope all goes well for you . I hope you will be warm and have plenty to eat . ” What good is it to say this , unless you do something to help ?
59002017	Faith that doesn't lead us to do good deeds is all alone and dead !
59002018	Suppose someone disagrees and says , “ It is possible to have faith without doing kind deeds . ” I would answer , “ Prove that you have faith without doing kind deeds , and I will prove that I have faith by doing them . ”
59002019	You surely believe there is only one God . That's fine . Even demons believe this , and it makes them shake with fear .
59002020	Does some stupid person want proof that faith without deeds is useless ?
59002021	Well , our ancestor Abraham pleased God by putting his son Isaac on the altar to sacrifice him .
59002022	Now you see how Abraham's faith and deeds worked together . He proved his faith was real by what he did .
59002023	This is what the Scriptures mean by saying , “ Abraham had faith in God , and God accepted him . ” That's how Abraham became God's friend .
59002024	You can now see that we please God by what we do and not only by what we believe .
59002025	For example , Rahab had been a prostitute . But she pleased God when she welcomed the spies and sent them home by another way .
59002026	Anyone who doesn't breathe is dead , and faith that doesn't do anything is just as dead !
59003001	My friends , we should not all try to become teachers . In fact , teachers will be judged more strictly than others .
59003002	All of us do many wrong things . But if you can control your tongue , you are mature and able to control your whole body .
59003003	By putting a bit into the mouth of a horse , we can turn the horse in different directions .
59003004	It takes strong winds to move a large sailing ship , but the captain uses only a small rudder to make it go in any direction .
59003005	Our tongues are small too , and yet they brag about big things . It takes only a spark to start a forest fire !
59003006	The tongue is like a spark . It is an evil power that dirties the rest of the body and sets a person's entire life on fire with flames that come from hell itself .
59003007	All kinds of animals , birds , reptiles , and sea creatures can be tamed and have been tamed .
59003008	But our tongues get out of control . They are restless and evil , and always spreading deadly poison .
59003011	Can clean water and dirty water both flow from the same spring ?
59003012	Can a fig tree produce olives or a grapevine produce figs ? Does fresh water come from a well full of salt water ?
59003013	Are any of you wise or sensible ? Then show it by living right and by being humble and wise in everything you do .
59003014	But if your heart is full of bitter jealousy and selfishness , don't brag or lie to cover up the truth .
59003015	This kind of wisdom doesn't come from above . It is earthly and selfish and comes from the devil himself .
59003016	Whenever people are jealous or selfish , they cause trouble and do all sorts of cruel things .
59003017	But the wisdom that comes from above leads us to be pure , friendly , gentle , sensible , kind , helpful , genuine , and sincere .
59003018	When peacemakers plant seeds of peace , they will harvest justice .
59004001	Why do you fight and argue with each other ? Isn't it because you are full of selfish desires that fight to control your body ?
59004002	You want something you don't have , and you will do anything to get it . You will even kill ! But you still cannot get what you want , and you won't get it by fighting and arguing . You should pray for it .
59004003	Yet even when you do pray , your prayers are not answered , because you pray just for selfish reasons .
59004004	You people aren't faithful to God ! Don't you know if you love the world , you are God's enemies ? And if you decide to be a friend of the world , you make yourself an enemy of God .
59004005	Do you doubt the Scriptures that say , “ God truly cares about the Spirit he has put in us ” ?
59004006	In fact , God treats us with even greater kindness , just as the Scriptures say , “ God opposes everyone who is proud , but he blesses all who are humble with undeserved grace . ”
59004007	Surrender to God ! Resist the devil , and he will run from you .
59004008	Come near to God , and he will come near to you . Clean up your lives , you sinners . Purify your hearts , you people who can't make up your mind .
59004009	Be sad and sorry and weep . Stop laughing and start crying . Be gloomy instead of glad .
59004010	Be humble in the Lord's presence , and he will honor you .
59004011	My friends , don't say cruel things about others ! If you do , or if you condemn others , you are condemning God's Law . And if you condemn the Law , you put yourself above the Law and refuse to obey either it
59004012	or God who gave it . God is our judge , and he can save or destroy us . What right do you have to condemn anyone ?
59004013	You should know better than to say , “ Today or tomorrow we will go to the city . We will do business there for a year and make a lot of money ! ”
59004014	What do you know about tomorrow ? How can you be so sure about your life ? It is nothing more than mist that appears for only a little while before it disappears .
59004015	You should say , “ If the Lord lets us live , we will do these things . ”
59004016	Yet you are stupid enough to brag , and it is wrong to be so proud .
59004017	If you don't do what you know is right , you have sinned .
59005001	You rich people should cry and weep ! Terrible things are going to happen to you .
59005002	Your treasures have already rotted , and moths have eaten your clothes .
59005003	Your money has rusted , and the rust will be evidence against you , as it burns your body like fire . Yet you keep on storing up wealth in these last days .
59005004	You refused to pay the people who worked in your fields , and now their unpaid wages are shouting out against you . The Lord All-Powerful has surely heard the cries of the workers who harvested your crops .
59005005	While here on earth , you have thought only of filling your own stomachs and having a good time . But now you are like fat cattle on their way to be butchered .
59005006	You have condemned and murdered innocent people , who couldn't even fight back .
59005007	My friends , be patient until the Lord returns . Think of farmers who wait patiently for the autumn and spring rains to make their valuable crops grow .
59005008	Be patient like those farmers and don't give up . The Lord will soon be here !
59005009	Don't grumble about each other or you will be judged , and the judge is right outside the door .
59005010	My friends , follow the example of the prophets who spoke for the Lord . They were patient , even when they had to suffer .
59005011	In fact , we praise the ones who endured the most . You remember how patient Job was and how the Lord finally helped him . The Lord did this because he is so merciful and kind .
59005012	My friends , above all else , don't take an oath . You must not swear by heaven or by earth or by anything else . “ Yes ” or “ No ” is all you need to say . If you say anything more , you will be condemned .
59005013	If you are having trouble , you should pray . And if you are feeling good , you should sing praises .
59005014	If you are sick , ask the church leaders to come and pray for you . Ask them to put olive oil on you in the name of the Lord .
59005015	If you have faith when you pray for sick people , they will get well . The Lord will heal them , and if they have sinned , he will forgive them .
59005016	If you have sinned , you should tell each other what you have done . Then you can pray for one another and be healed . The prayer of an innocent person is powerful , and it can help a lot .
59005017	Elijah was just as human as we are , and for three and a half years his prayers kept the rain from falling .
59005018	But when he did pray for rain , it fell from the skies and made the crops grow .
59005019	My friends , if any followers have wandered away from the truth , you should try to lead them back .
59005020	If you turn sinners from the wrong way , you will save them from death , and many of their sins will be forgiven .
60001001	From Peter , an apostle of Jesus Christ . To God's people who are scattered like foreigners in Pontus , Galatia , Cappadocia , Asia , and Bithynia .
60001002	God the Father decided to choose you as his people , and his Spirit has made you holy . You have obeyed Jesus Christ and are sprinkled with his blood . I pray that God will be kind to you and will keep on giving you peace !
60001003	Praise God , the Father of our Lord Jesus Christ . God is so good , and by raising Jesus from death , he has given us new life and a hope that lives on .
60001004	God has something stored up for you in heaven , where it will never decay or be ruined or disappear .
60001005	You have faith in God , whose power will protect you until the last day . Then he will save you , just as he has always planned to do .

60001009	you are to be saved . This is why you have faith .

60001016	That's why the Scriptures say , “ I am the holy God , and you must be holy too . ”
60001017	You say that God is your Father , but God doesn't have favorites ! He judges all people by what they do . So you must honor God while you live as strangers here on earth .
60001018	You were rescued from the useless way of life you learned from your ancestors . But you know you were not rescued by such things as silver or gold that don't last forever .
60001019	You were rescued by the precious blood of Christ , that spotless and innocent lamb .
60001020	Christ was chosen even before the world was created , but because of you , he did not come until these last days .
60001021	And when he did come , it was to lead you to have faith in God , who raised him from death and honored him in a glorious way . This is why you have put your faith and hope in God .
60001022	You obeyed the truth , and your souls were made pure . Now you sincerely love each other . But you must keep on loving with all your heart .
60001023	Do this because God has given you new birth by his message that lives on forever .
60001024	The Scriptures say , “ Humans wither like grass , and their glory fades like wild flowers . Grass dries up , and flowers fall to the ground .
60001025	But what the Lord has said will stand forever . ” Our good news to you is what the Lord has said .

60002006	It is just as God says in the Scriptures , “ Look ! I am placing in Zion a choice and precious cornerstone . No one who has faith in this one will be disappointed . ”

60002008	They disobeyed the message and stumbled and fell over this stone , because they were doomed .
60002009	But you are God's chosen and special people . You are a group of royal priests and a holy nation . God has brought you out of darkness into his marvelous light . Now you must tell all the wonderful things he has done . The Scriptures say ,
60002010	“ Once you were nobody . Now you are God's people . At one time no one had mercy on you . Now God has treated you with kindness . ”
60002011	Dear friends , you are foreigners and strangers on this earth . So I beg you not to surrender to those desires that fight against you .
60002012	Always let others see you behaving properly , even though they may still accuse you of doing wrong . Then on the day of judgment , they will honor God by telling the good things they saw you do .

60002020	You don't gain anything by being punished for some wrong you have done . But God will bless you , if you have to suffer for doing something good .

60002022	Christ did not sin or ever tell a lie .

60002024	Christ carried the burden of our sins . He was nailed to the cross , so we would stop sinning and start living right . By his cuts and bruises you are healed .
60002025	You had wandered away like sheep . Now you have returned to the one who is your shepherd and protector .

60004001	Christ suffered here on earth . Now you must be ready to suffer as he did , because suffering shows that you have stopped sinning .

61002021	They would have been better off if they had never known about the right way . Even after they knew what was right , they turned their backs on the holy commandments they were given .
61002022	What happened to them is just like the true saying , “ A dog will come back to lick up its own vomit . A pig that has been washed will roll in the mud . ”

61003002	what God's prophets said would happen . You must never forget what the holy prophets taught in the past . And you must remember what the apostles told you our Lord and Savior has commanded us to do .

61003004	and say , “ Didn't your Lord promise to come back ? Yet the first leaders have already died , and the world hasn't changed a bit . ”

62001009	But if we confess our sins to God , he can always be trusted to forgive us and take our sins away .

66008001	When the Lamb opened the seventh seal , there was silence in heaven for about half an hour .
66008002	I noticed that the seven angels who stood before God were each given a trumpet .
66008003	Another angel , who had a gold container for incense , came and stood at the altar . This one was given a lot of incense to offer with the prayers of God's people on the gold altar in front of the throne .
66008004	Then the smoke of the incense , together with the prayers of God's people , went up to God from the hand of the angel .
66008005	After this , the angel filled the incense container with fire from the altar and threw it on the earth . Thunder roared , lightning flashed , and the earth shook .
66008006	The seven angels now got ready to blow their trumpets .
66008007	When the first angel blew his trumpet , hail and fire mixed with blood were thrown down on the earth . A third of the earth , a third of the trees , and a third of all green plants were burned .
66008008	When the second angel blew his trumpet , something like a great fiery mountain was thrown into the sea . A third of the sea turned to blood ,
66008009	a third of the living creatures in the sea died , and a third of the ships were destroyed .
66008010	When the third angel blew his trumpet , a great star fell from heaven . It was burning like a torch , and it fell on a third of the rivers and on a third of the springs of water .
66008011	The name of the star was Bitter , and a third of the water turned bitter . Many people died because the water was so bitter .
66008012	When the fourth angel blew his trumpet , a third of the sun , a third of the moon , and a third of the stars were struck . They each lost a third of their light . So during a third of the day there was no light , and a third of the night was also without light .
66008013	Then I looked and saw a lone eagle flying across the sky . It was shouting , “ Trouble , trouble , trouble to everyone who lives on earth ! The other three angels are now going to blow their trumpets . ”
66009001	When the fifth angel blew his trumpet , I saw a star fall from the sky to earth . It was given the key to the tunnel that leads down to the deep pit .
66009002	As it opened the tunnel , smoke poured out like the smoke of a great furnace . The sun and the air turned dark because of the smoke .
66009003	Locusts came out of the smoke and covered the earth . They were given the same power that scorpions have .
66009004	The locusts were told not to harm the grass on the earth or any plant or any tree . They were to punish only those people who did not have God's mark on their foreheads .
66009005	The locusts were allowed to make them suffer for five months , but not to kill them . The suffering they caused was like the sting of a scorpion .
66009006	In those days people will want to die , but they will not be able to . They will hope for death , but it will escape from them .
66009007	These locusts looked like horses ready for battle . On their heads they wore something like gold crowns , and they had human faces .
66009008	Their hair was like a woman's long hair , and their teeth were like those of a lion .
66009009	On their chests they wore armor made of iron . Their wings roared like an army of horse-drawn chariots rushing into battle .
66009010	Their tails were like a scorpion's tail with a stinger that had the power to hurt someone for five months .
66009011	Their king was the angel in charge of the deep pit . In Hebrew his name was Abaddon , and in Greek it was Apollyon .
66009012	The first horrible thing has now happened ! But wait . Two more horrible things will happen soon .
66009013	Then the sixth angel blew his trumpet . I heard a voice speak from the four corners of the gold altar that stands in the presence of God .
66009014	The voice spoke to this angel and said , “ Release the four angels who are tied up beside the great Euphrates River . ”
66009015	The four angels had been prepared for this very hour and day and month and year . Now they were set free to kill a third of all people .
66009016	By listening , I could tell there were more than 200,000,000 war horses .
66009017	In my vision their riders wore fiery-red , dark-blue , and yellow armor on their chests . The heads of the horses looked like lions , with fire and smoke and sulfur coming out of their mouths .
66009018	One third of all people were killed by the three terrible troubles caused by the fire , the smoke , and the sulfur .
66009019	The horses had powerful mouths , and their tails were like poisonous snakes that bite and hurt .
66009020	The people who lived through these terrible troubles did not turn away from the idols they had made , and they did not stop worshiping demons . They kept on worshiping idols that were made of gold , silver , bronze , stone , and wood . Not one of these idols could see , hear , or walk .
66009021	No one stopped murdering or practicing witchcraft or being immoral or stealing .

66010002	and with his hand he held a little scroll that had been unrolled . He stood there with his right foot on the sea and his left foot on the land .
66010003	Then he shouted with a voice that sounded like a growling lion . Thunder roared seven times .

66021001	I saw a new heaven and a new earth . The first heaven and the first earth had disappeared , and so had the sea .
66021002	Then I saw New Jerusalem , the holy city , coming down from God in heaven . It was like a bride dressed in her wedding gown and ready to meet her husband .
66021003	I heard a loud voice shout from the throne :
66021005	Then the one sitting on the throne said :
66021009	I saw one of the seven angels who had the bowls filled with the seven last terrible troubles . The angel came to me and said , “ Come on ! I will show you the one who will be the bride and wife of the Lamb . ”
66021010	Then with the help of the Spirit , he took me to the top of a very high mountain . There he showed me the holy city of Jerusalem coming down from God in heaven .
66021011	The glory of God made the city bright . It was dazzling and crystal clear like a precious jasper stone .
66021012	The city had a high and thick wall with twelve gates , and each one of them was guarded by an angel . On each of the gates was written the name of one of the twelve tribes of Israel .
66021013	Three of these gates were on the east , three were on the north , three more were on the south , and the other three were on the west .
66021014	The city was built on twelve foundation stones . On each of the stones was written the name of one of the Lamb's twelve apostles .
66021015	The angel who spoke to me had a gold measuring stick to measure the city and its gates and its walls .
66021016	The city was shaped like a cube , because it was just as high as it was wide . When the angel measured the city , it was about 2,400 kilometers high and 2,400 kilometers wide .
66021017	Then the angel measured the wall , and by our measurements it was about 60 meters high .
66021018	The wall was built of jasper , and the city was made of pure gold , clear as crystal .
66021019	Each of the twelve foundations was a precious stone . The first was jasper , the second was sapphire , the third was agate , the fourth was emerald ,
66021020	the fifth was onyx , the sixth was carnelian , the seventh was chrysolite , the eighth was beryl , the ninth was topaz , the tenth was chrysoprase , the eleventh was jacinth , and the twelfth was amethyst .
66021021	Each of the twelve gates was a solid pearl . The streets of the city were made of pure gold , clear as crystal .
66021022	I did not see a temple there . The Lord God All-Powerful and the Lamb were its temple .
66021023	And the city did not need the sun or the moon . The glory of God was shining on it , and the Lamb was its light .
66021024	Nations will walk by the light of that city , and kings will bring their riches there .
66021025	Its gates are always open during the day , and night never comes .
66021026	The glorious treasures of nations will be brought into the city .
66021027	But nothing unworthy will be allowed to enter . No one who is dirty-minded or who tells lies will be there . Only those whose names are written in the Lamb's book of life will be in the city .
66022001	The angel showed me a river that was crystal clear , and its waters gave life . The river came from the throne where God and the Lamb were seated .
66022002	Then it flowed down the middle of the city's main street . On each side of the river are trees that grow a different kind of fruit each month of the year . The fruit gives life , and the leaves are used as medicine to heal the nations .
66022003	God's curse will no longer be on the people of that city . He and the Lamb will be seated there on their thrones , and its people will worship God
66022004	and will see him face to face . God's name will be written on the foreheads of the people .
66022005	Never again will night appear , and no one who lives there will ever need a lamp or the sun . The Lord God will be their light , and they will rule forever .
66022006	Then I was told :
66022008	My name is John , and I am the one who heard and saw these things . Then after I had heard and seen all this , I knelt down and began to worship at the feet of the angel who had shown it to me .
66022009	But the angel said ,
66022012	Then I was told :
66022017	The Spirit and the bride say , “ Come ! ” Everyone who hears this should say , “ Come ! ” If you are thirsty , come ! If you want life-giving water , come and take it . It's free !
66022018	Here is my warning for everyone who hears the prophecies in this book :
66022020	The one who has spoken these things says , “ I am coming soon ! ” So , Lord Jesus , please come soon !
66022021	I pray that the Lord Jesus will be kind to all of you .
